# 3.18 SRS Framework

## 3.18.0-4 SRS Framework Modification of SRS configuration and activation (ID: 11153999)

**3.18.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `12493288`)

SRS Framework
The modification of the SRS configuration is triggered by the C-Plane. The new configuration is activated only after the indication that the UE is expected to use this new setting. Before this indication the current configuration is applied.

The U-Plane uses the new configuration to manage the DCI Format 0\_1 size, not after one of the following condition is met:

 If C-Plane requested U-Plane to apply a specifc procedure (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26859\_replaced([11153624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksnXLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the RRC message processing in the UE is completed from the gNB point of view, at most after the RRC processing delay following the RRC message delivery by the MAC layer to the UE (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17940\_replaced([11153286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kslh8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 The C-Plane provides the RRC Reconfiguration Complete Indication to the U-Plane, if the MAC layer was able to receive the UL-SCH transmission(s), handling the RRC Confirmation message..

When NRBTS/actEnhRrcReconfUlPrbRandom is set to disable, between the modification of the configuration and its activation, the gNB-DU, if needed, shall use the DCI Format 0\_0.

**[CB014465-A] If NRCELL.actMulSrsInSplSlot is true and the available SRS symbol positions for the cell are changed due to online modification of NRCELL.mulSrsPositions, gNB-DU shall stop decoding SRS resources on the symbol that is not available after the parameter modification. Rationale: L1 can not support decoding 3 SRS symbols at the same time when both new and old SRS symbols has SRS resources under usage.**[End CB014465-A]\*\*\*\*

---

## 3.18.0-5 SRS Framework Interworking with FR1 Carrier Aggregation (ID: 11154017)

**3.18.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `12647021`)

SRS Framework
If:

 UE is already configured with DL+UL SCell, and

 step-wise SCell Addition procedure for another SCell is ongoing [CB010741-C]

OR

 UE is already configured with DL-only SCell, and

 SCell Upgrade procedure of existing SCell to DL&UL SCell is ongoing [End CB010741-C]

then:

a) for UE configured with FDD PCell and TDD DL+UL SCell:

if:

 the periodic-SRS (p-SRS) resources in the TDD DL+UL SCell were configured before step-wise SCell Addition and they are being released

OR

 there was no p-SRS resource in TDD DL+UL SCell before step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C] and the p-SRS are being configured

OR

 slots (i.e. slots number) used for p-SRS in TDD DL+UL SCell are being changed

then:

Case 1: If p-SRS reconfiguration is **NOT accompanied by reconfiguration of UL Tx switching:**

 gNB-DU shall not update the dedicated PUSCH TDRA List for FDD PCell ([11115802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpyFlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 when FDD PCell PUSCH slots overlap with TDD DL+UL SCell periodic SRS (p-SRS) slots, the gNB-DU shall schedule the UE using shortened symbols in the FDD PCell ([11144548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_236NffvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

Case 2: If p-SRS reconfiguration is **accompanied by reconfiguration of** UL Tx switching:\*\*\*\*

 gNB-DU may update the dedicated PUSCH TDRA List for FDD PCell; the need for the re-calculation of the list is described in ([11115928](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpzTt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 UL branch of FDD PCell 5G-L2-PS shall enter the transient state ([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), in addition UE shall not be scheduled in FDD PCell PUSCH slots which overlap with TDD DL+UL SCell p-SRS slots ([11195069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv5UqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

b) for UE configured with TDD PCell and FDD DL+UL SCell:

if:

 the p-SRS resources in the TDD PCell were configured before step-wise SCell Addition and they are being released

OR

 there was no p-SRS resource in TDD PCell before step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C] and the p-SRS are being configured

then:

Case 1: If p-SRS reconfiguration is **NOT accompanied by reconfiguration of UL Tx switching nor critical band reconfiguration**

 gNB-DU shall not update the dedicated PUSCH TDRA List ([11115802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpyFlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) nor dedicated PDSCH TDRA List for FDD DL+UL SCell

Case 2: If p-SRS reconfiguration is **accompanied by reconfiguration of** UL Tx switching:\*\*\*\*

 gNB-DU may update the dedicated PUSCH TDRA List for FDD DL+UL SCell; the need for the re-calculation of the list is described in ([11115928](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpzTt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Case 3: If p-SRS reconfiguration is **accompanied by entering or leaving the** critical band combination:\*\*\*\*

if:

- UE Capability ‘txSwitchWithAnotherBand’ for the new band combination is changed, which causes to enter the critical band combinations

then:

- gNB-DU may update the dedicated PUSCH TDRA List for FDD DL+UL SCell; the need for the re-calculation of the list is described in ([11115928](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpzTt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

if:

- UE Capability ‘txSwitchWithAnotherBand’ for the new band combination is changed, which causes to leave the critical band combinations

then:

- gNB-DU shall not update the dedicated PUSCH TDRA List for FDD DL+UL SCell;

if:

- UE Capability ‘txSwitchImpactToRx’ for the new band combination is changed, which causes to enter the critical band combinations

then:

- gNB-DU may update the dedicated PDSCH TDRA List for FDD DL+UL SCell according to ([11115315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kptNFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11115584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpvpWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

if:

- UE Capability ‘txSwitchImpactToRx’ for the new band combination is changed, which causes to leave the critical band combinations

then:

- gNB-DU shall not update the dedicated PDSCH TDRA List for FDD DL+UL SCell according to ([11115315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kptNFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11115584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpvpWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

For more details and examples refer to EFS CP3 requirement ([11144548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_236NffvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

## 3.18.1 Periodic codebook SRS for UL BM

### 3.18.1.1 State Machine for Ul BM

#### 3.18.1.1.0-1 State Machine for Ul BM Overview of state machine for Ul BM (ID: 11154039)

**3.18.1.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13378089`)

State Machine for Ul BM
13378089:
State Machine for Ul BM
Two state machines are introduced for periodic SRS resource set with usage codebook: one is the state machine for SU-MIMO (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3236\_replaced([11155554](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksv6C_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), another is the state machine for UL BM. This requirement defines the state machine for UL BM.
 
The overall state machine for UL BM is defined in the below diagram.
 
For users which are configured with codebook usage periodic SRS resource set:
The UL BM state machine shall be maintained; If DL also needs beams from this SRS resource set, additional validity of best/second best beams for DL shall be determined as defined in 
[CB015122-A]
if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1,
the beam selection algorithm is moved to L1-DU, see [13328734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-30ziNTeEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
else
[End CB015122-A]
5G\_UP\_ALG\_2181\_replaced([11154797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kstdx_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) .
[CB015122-A]
end
[End CB015122-A]
Note that DL always needs 2nd best beam even when it is not 4Rx when UL does not need 2nd best beam.
 
For CA UE with UL configured according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) over SCell, the UL BM state machine shall be maintained.
 
- The **rrmCoMaAgedTimer is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2144\_replaced([11154145](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**
- State of **SRS\_UL\_BM\_AGED is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2138\_replaced([11154054](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqadvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));**
- State of **SRS\_UL\_BM\_VALID is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2140\_replaced([11154089](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqafPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));**
**- State of** SRS\_UL\_BM\_CHGED is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2142\_replaced([11154118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));***\*

#### 3.18.1.1.0-2 State Machine for Ul BM State of SRS_UL_BM_AGED (ID: 11154054)

**3.18.1.1.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `13364374`)

State Machine for Ul BM
It's the initial state of the state machine. For CA UE with UL configured according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) over SCell, it's the initial state of the state machine.

When state is entered:

 Stop the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer.**

[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

 Stop the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer ([13378910](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_KtvcY_3CEfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).**

else

[End CB015122-A]

 Stop the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2173\_replaced([11154691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

 Clear the **rrmAvgCoMa (set to 0) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2166\_replaced([11154579](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

[CB015122-A]

end

[End CB015122-A]

 If **rrmExtendOdftTimer (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2147\_replaced([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not running or expired:**

- If the number of spatial streams for a given subcell is 4 or 2 (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the UL beam(s) shall be selected based on beam reports from UE (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1987\_replaced([11112050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpSWY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2017\_replaced([11112151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- If the number of spatial streams for a given subcell is 8  or larger than 8 **(5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and CoMa is aged, L2PS shall use UE-reported best SSB beams in UE context and extend one or two beams to four beams according to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_10722\_replaced([11296872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqFevPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

**- If DL also needs beams from UL state machine (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2181\_replaced([11154797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kstdx_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), beams for DL algorithm shall be as** SRS\_DL\_BM\_AGED defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6965\_replaced([11155684](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxII_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*

**- If NRBTS.NRCELL.actProbingUlSrsBeams = 'Beams3rd4th' and beam probing is going on due to previously selected oDFT beams, the beam probing shall be abandoned. The next beam probing (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32455\_replaced([11155432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be started from the beginning after a valid beam selection instance.**

· else oDFT beam is still seen as valid until **rrmExtendOdftTimer is expired.**

Under this state:

[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

 After receiving notification from L1-DU, see [13336532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_smL_F9mHEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), that instantaneous CoMa over 2 polarities and total ports in same period are valid, 5G-L2-PS shall switch to SRS\_UL\_BM\_VALID state.

else

[End CB015122-A]

 When receiving a valid CoMa (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2164\_replaced([11154500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), update **rrmAvgCoMa.**

* After continuous reception of **rrmNumOfCoMa (default value is 3) valid CoMa reports from L1, switch to** SRS\_UL\_BM\_VALID.\*\*\*\*

[CB015122-A]

end

[End CB015122-A]

#### 3.18.1.1.0-3 State Machine for Ul BM State of SRS_UL_BM_VALID (ID: 11154089)

**3.18.1.1.0-3.0-7**  (ID: `13364919`)

State Machine for Ul BM
When state is entered:

[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

 UL beams selection algorithm is performed by L1-DU, see [13328734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-30ziNTeEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-30ziNTeEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9"), upon notification of 5G-L2-PS. 5G-L2-PS receives valid beams from L1-DU through the interface between both components. If the best UL beam or second-best UL beam is changed, the state shall be changed to SRS\_UL\_BM\_CHGED.

 Start the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer as defined in [13378910](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_KtvcY_3CEfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).**

else

[End CB015122-A]

 Execute **the UL beam selection algorithms defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2168\_replaced([11154601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

If the best UL beam or second-best UL beam is changed, the state shall be changed to **SRS\_UL\_BM\_CHGED.**

 Start the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer, see 13378910.**

end[CB015122-A]

endend

[End CB015122-A]

 Start the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer.**

 Stop **rrmExtendOdftTimer (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2147\_replaced([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if it is running.**

Under this state:

[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

 When the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer expires:**

1) UL beams selection algorithm is performed by L1-DU, see [13328734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-30ziNTeEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). When 5G-L2-PS receives valid UL beams from L1-DU, see 13328734, then if at least one beam among (NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming / 2) UL best beams is changed, the state shall be changed to **SRS\_UL\_BM\_CHGED.**

2) Restart the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer.**

 When the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer expires, indicate to L1-DU expiry, see event (4) in [13413759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_p8GZghKBEfG3gf_qmG8Vww?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_p8gzghkbefg3gf_qmg8vww?oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9"), and switch to** SRS\_UL\_BM\_AGED state.\*\*\*\*

 When received a valid instantaneous CoMa in L1-DU is indicated in [13331610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3PiwQdWeEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), restart the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer.**

 For CA UE with UL configured according to [11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) over SCell, switch to **SRS\_UL\_BM\_AGED state after SCell is deactivated successfully. pSRS is configured on the UL Carrier of the SCell and is used for UL beam management of this carrier independently of the PCell configuration.**

 When receive oDFT beam set online changed, execute the beam selection algorithm defined in [13328734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-30ziNTeEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), restart **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer,** switch to **SRS\_UL\_BM\_CHGED.**\*\*\*\*

Note: Whether considering the beam selection is to be performed for all UEs with DFT beam, it is left to CP3 to define how to distribute these UEs over multiple slots. A general requirement is, L2-PS shall trigger L1-DU beam selection to get the latest beams for each UE as soon as possible.

else

[End CB015122-A]

 When the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer expires or gNB-DU skips evaluation SRS occurrence for avoid purposes (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29538\_replaced([11158109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_xqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

1) if long-term CoMa updated condition (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29616\_replaced([11154157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBiPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is met, execute the UL beam selection algorithms defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2168\_replaced([11154601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20242\_replaced([11154912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).  If at least one best beam among (NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming / 2) UL best beams ischanged, the state shall be changed to **SRS\_UL\_BM\_CHGED.**

2) Restart the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer.**

 When the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer expires, switch to** SRS\_UL\_BM\_AGED state.\*\*\*\*

 After reception of a valid instantaneous CoMa (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2164\_replaced([11154500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), update **rrmAvgCoMa and restart the** rrmCoMaAgedTimer.\*\*\*\*

 For CA UE with UL configured according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) over SCell, switch to **SRS\_UL\_BM\_AGED state after SCell is deactivated successfully. pSRS is configured on the UL Carrier of the SCell and is used for UL beam management of this carrier independently of the PCell configuration.**

 When receive oDFT beam set online changed, execute the beam selection algorithm defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2168\_replaced([11154601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), restart **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer,** switch to **SRS\_UL\_BM\_CHGED. Note: Whether considering the beam selection is to be performed for all UEs with DFT beam, it is left to CP3 to define how to distribute these UEs over multiple slots. A general requirement is, L2-PS shall perform the beam selection to get the latest beams for each UE as soon as possible.**\*\*\*\*

[CB015122-A]

end

[End CB015122-A]

---

#### 3.18.1.1.0-4 State Machine for Ul BM State of SRS_UL_BM_CHGED (ID: 11154118)

**3.18.1.1.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `13366104`)

State Machine for Ul BM
Under this state:

[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

 When the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer expires:**

1) 5G-L2-PS shall notify L1-DU for UL beam selection, as in [13372362](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_V9lzgfqiEfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and restart **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer**as defined in [13378910](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_KtvcY_3CEfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).\*\*\*\*

 When the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer expires, indicate to L1-DU expiry, see event (4) in [13413759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_p8GZghKBEfG3gf_qmG8Vww?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_p8gzghkbefg3gf_qmg8vww?oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9"), and switch to** SRS\_UL\_BM\_AGED state.\*\*\*\*

 When received a valid instantaneous CoMa in L1-DU is indicated in [13331610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3PiwQdWeEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), restart **the** **rrmCoMaAgedTimer.**

 After reception of a valid SU-MIMO report from PUSCH or SRS from L1-DU, switch to **SRS\_UL\_BM\_VALID state.**

 For CA UE with UL configured according to [11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) over SCell, switch to **SRS\_UL\_BM\_AGED state after SCell is deactivated successfully. pSRS is configured on the UL Carrier of the SCell and is used for UL beam management of this carrier independently of the PCell configuration.**

 When receive oDFT beam set online changed, the rrmUlBeamSelectTimer shall be restarted and the beam selection algorithm defined in [13372362](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_V9lzgfqiEfCPDo8cGBoqIw "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showArtifactPage&artifactURI=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fresources%2FMD_taUaAPvFEe-AqvopbP1qhQ&oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9&artifactInModule=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fresources%2FBI_V9lzgfqiEfCPDo8cGBoqIw&componentURI=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Frm-projects%2F_T-lVkJ5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA%2Fcomponents%2F_UBjxEJ5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA") should be executed by L1-DU.

Note: Whether considering the beam selection is to be performed for all UEs with DFT beam, it is left to CP3 to define how to distribute these UEs over multiple slots. A general requirement is, L2-PS shall trigger L1-DU beam selection to get the latest beams for each UE as soon as possible.

else

[End CB015122-A]

 When the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer expires or gNB-DU skips evaluation SRS occurrence for avoid purposes (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29538\_replaced([11158109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_xqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

1) if averaged CoMa updated condition (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29616\_replaced([11154157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBiPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is met, execute **the UL beam selection algorithms defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2168\_replaced([11154601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.\*\*\*\*

2) Restart the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer.**

 When the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer expires, switch to** SRS\_UL\_BM\_AGED state.\*\*\*\*

 When receive valid CoMa (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2164\_replaced([11154500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), update **rrmAvgCoMa and restart** the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer.**\*\*\*\*

 After reception of a valid SU-MIMO report from PUSCH or SRS, switch to **SRS\_UL\_BM\_VALID state.**

 For CA UE with UL configured according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) over SCell, switch to **SRS\_UL\_BM\_AGED state after SCell is deactivated successfully. pSRS is configured on the UL Carrier of the SCell and is used for UL beam management of this carrier independently of the PCell configuration.**

 When receive oDFT beam set online changed, execute the beam selection algorithm defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2168\_replaced([11154601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), restart **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer. Note: Whether considering the beam selection is to be performed for all UEs with DFT beam, it is left to CP3 to define how to distribute these UEs over multiple slots. A general requirement is, L2-PS shall trigger L1-DU beam selection to get the latest beams for each UE as soon as possible..**

[CB015122-A]

end

[End CB015122-A]

---

#### 3.18.1.1.0-5 State Machine for Ul BM Age of covariance matrix (CoMa) (ID: 11154145)

**3.18.1.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11154151`)

State Machine for Ul BM
5G-L2-PS shall maintain independent timer of rrmCoMaAgedTimer for Ul BM or Dl BM state machine of one UE. The duration of rrmCoMaAgedTimer shall be calculated as the number of slots in value of (rrmCoMaAgedCycle \* SRS periodicity). The SRS periodicity is from the periodicityAndOffset in SRS configuration (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2147\_replaced([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The rrmCoMaAgedCycle shall be implemented as a R&D parameter (default value is 10, reuse rdDlCoMaAgedCycle, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11386\_replaced([11114017](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpgYzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 3.18.1.1.0-6 State Machine for Ul BM Averaged CoMa updated condition (ID: 11154157)

**3.18.1.1.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11154164`)

State Machine for Ul BM
The condition has initial value as true.

If reduced periodic SRS processing functionality is not triggered (5G\_UP\_543\_replaced([11351277](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubsma_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

The condition is always true.

Else:

The condition is true if averaged CoMa has been updated since last beam determination. Otherwise, it is false.

---

### 3.18.1.2 SRS Reception

#### 3.18.1.2.0-1 SRS Reception Periodic SRS configuration (ID: 11154174)

**3.18.1.2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11154194`)

SRS Reception
**[CB009527-A]**

**NOTE: to make requirement to be more generic, this requirement is revised by replacing names of WB SRS and SB SRS to SB BF and WB BF. PLEASE remove this NOTE when a new version is created.**

**[End CB009527-A]**

If the NIDD actUlSrsBm is true, 5G-L2-PS may receive periodic SRS resource configuration of a user from L3 during the user setup or user modification procedures. The following parameters shall be stored in user context.

Please note: it's possible that some users are configured with aperiodic SRS and others are configured with periodic SRS by L3. The SRS allocation algorithm is specified by L3.

· nrofSRS-Ports

· transmissionComb

o n2

§ combOffset-n2

§ cyclicShift-n2

o Or n4

§ combOffset-n4

§ cyclicShift-n4

· resourceMapping

o startPosition

o nrofSymbols

o repetitionFactor

· freqDomainPosition, corresponds to n-RRC

· freqDomainShift, corresponds to n-shift

· freqHopping

o c-SRS

o b-SRS

o b-hop

· groupOrSequenceHopping

· resourceType

o periodic

§ periodicityAndOffset

· sequenceId

* When periodic SRS resource for SB BF is shared between DL and UL BM as defined by 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_11074\_replaced([11305745](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqzQZvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS shall request only a part of this SRS for CoMa to L1 as defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20838\_replaced([11156649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2nsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* When periodic codebook SRS resource configuration is changed, 5G-L2-PS shall delete all previous SRS resource related handling in UL BM defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2135\_replaced([11154028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqacvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), except oDFT beam will be invalid according to its own **rrmExtendOdftBeamTimer which has the same length as remaining** rrmCoMaAgedTimer for UL in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2144\_replaced([11154145](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*
* When periodic codebook SRS resource is released, 5G-L2-PS shall delete all this SRS resource related handling in UL BM defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2135\_replaced([11154028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqacvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) including oDFT beams.

---

#### 3.18.1.2.0-2 SRS Reception Cyclic shift of SRS ports (ID: 11154208)

**3.18.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11154214`)

SRS Reception
The cyclic shift values of each SRS port shall be calculated according to equations defined in 3GPP 38.211 6.4.1.4.2. Below table is an example about how to calculate cyclic shift value of SRS port from the values of nrofSRS-Ports, transmissionComb and cyclicShift in UE’s context (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2147\_replaced([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| nrofSRS-Ports | SRS port | Cyclic shift(s) (transmissionComb = n2) | Cyclic shift(s) (transmissionComb = n4) |
| Port1 | 1000 | cyclicShift | cyclicShift |
| Ports2 | 1000 | cyclicShift | cyclicShift |
| 1001 | (cyclicShift + 4) mod 8 | (cyclicShift + 6) mod 12 |  |

---

#### 3.18.1.2.0-3 SRS Reception SRS measurement cycle (periodic SRS) (ID: 11154219)

**3.18.1.2.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11154384`)

SRS Reception
11154384:
SRS Reception
5G-L2-PS shall trigger SRS reception for UEs, which are configured with periodic SRS in active BWP and for which the UE dedicated configuration is activated (5G\_UP\_ALG\_18227\_replaced([11153313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kslh9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in slots satisfying the below condition:

$(N\_{slot}^{frame,u} n\_f + n\_{s,f}^u - T\_{of f set}) \mod T\_{ars} = 0$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10184.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where:

 [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N frame,u slot". The text is in a mathematical notation, with "frame,u" as a superscript to "N" and "slot" as a subscript. The text is blurry and difficult to read clearly.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10184.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] is the number of slots per frame.

 [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a close-up of a white surface with a blurred, colorful gradient on the left side. The gradient appears to be composed of shades of yellow, orange, purple, and blue, forming abstract shapes. The right side of the image is entirely black. 5G-L2-PS shall NOT trigger SRS reception for UEs which are NOT in duration of DRX active status even above slot condition for periodic SRS is satisfied. Note SW designed some simplified solution, detail refers to CP3.

5G-L2-PS shall NOT trigger SRS reception for UEs which are in measurement GAP period even above slot condition for periodic SRS is satisfied.

5G-L2-PS shall NOT trigger SRS based BM reception for UEs due to remote interference mitigation scheme (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9172\_replaced([11163373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

5G-L2-PS shall NOT trigger **periodic SRS reception for UEs due to additional UL mitigation for RIM RS detection (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13520\_replaced([11162042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-APvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

5G-L2-PS shall skip some periodic SRS processing for the purpose of reducing SRS load as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29538\_replaced([11158109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_xqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[CB014465-A] 5G-L2-PS shall NOT trigger** periodic SRS reception if the SRS resources are not available due to online modification of SRS symbol positions of the cell as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26832\_replaced([11153999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**[End CB014465-A]**\*\*\*\*

For each UE for which SRS reception needs to be triggered, 5G-L2-PS shall provide below SRS related information to L1-UL according to SRS configuration stored in UE’s context (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2147\_replaced([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

 Time domain position: startPosition and nrofSymbols (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2147\_replaced([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Frequency domain position: starting PRB and number of PRBs (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2153\_replaced([11154391](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksromvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Transmission comb: combOffset and cyclicShift (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2149\_replaced([11154208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrokvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Sequence ID.

 For the case that UL SU-MIMO needs to be measured over SRS, additional SU-MIMO related information shall be provided to L1. See the details in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3246\_replaced([11155645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhHPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

SRS Reception

#### 3.18.1.2.0-5 SRS Reception SRS Reception Over SCell for UL Carrier Aggregation (ID: 11154419)

**3.18.1.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11154424`)

SRS Reception
If the NIDD actUlSrsBm of SCell with UL configured according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is true for FR1 UL CA UE, 5G-L2-PS may receive periodic SRS resource configuration according to 5G\_UL\_ALG\_2147.

Per TS38.321, UE will transmit SRS over SCell according to timing defined in TS38.213 after SCell activation/Deactivation MAC-CE received.

 After SCell activation status is active according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2804\_replaced([11121880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS will start the reception of SRS according to periodic SRS configuration;

 After SCell deactivation(SCell deactivation MAC-CE is ACKed), 5G-L2-PS will stop the reception of SRS;

### 3.18.1.3 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)

#### 3.18.1.3.0-1 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Process covariance matrices (ID: 11154436)

**3.18.1.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13370905`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

This requirement has been moved to L1-DU, see [11107143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koco1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

else

[End CB015122-A]

After 5G-L2-PS receives covariance matrices from L1, it shall process matrices according to below steps. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2136\_replaced([11154035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqac_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) about the state machine for BM.

Note: the calculation and maintenance of the covariance matrices shall be implemented in a separate thread or process to decouple it from the normal scheduler process

1. Read covariance matrices per subband and find context of related UE(s) according to subband information.

a.  The number of covariance matrices per UE is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2160\_replaced([11154462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

b.  The size of covariance matrix is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2158\_replaced([11154448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2. Calculate Cov(H) and Cov(V) per UE (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2162\_replaced([11154482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

3. Validate Cov(H) and Cov(V) per UE (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2164\_replaced([11154500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2165\_replaced([11154516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

4. If Cov(H) and Cov(V) are valid:

a.  Average them via the IIR filter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2166\_replaced([11154579](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

b.  Store averaged Cov(H) and Cov(V) in UE’s context.

5. If Cov(H) or Cov(V) is invalid:

a.  Discard Cov(H) and Cov(V) of UE which are reported by L1.

[CB015122-A]

end

[End CB015122-A]

---

#### 3.18.1.3.0-2 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Size of covariance matrix (ID: 11154448)

**3.18.1.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13370921`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

This requirement has been moved to L1-DU, see [13331607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_UX1xktWeEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-A]

The size of horizontal and vertical covariance matrix is decided according to layout of radio unit according to the below layout table:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Number of TRXs | Number of columns (**rrmTrxColumn)** | Number of rows (**rrmTrxRow)** | First Feature |
| 16 | 4 | 2 | 5GC001086-C |
| 16 | 8 | 1 | 5GC001086-C |
| 32 | 8 | 2 | 5GC001086-C |
| 32 | 4 | 4 | 5GC001086-C |
| 64 | 8 | 4 | 5GC001086-A |

The horizontal covariance matrix is a square matrix of size **rrmTrxColumn.**

The vertical covariance matrix is a square matrix of size **rrmTrxRow.**

Note: Only the lower triangle of the covariance matrix is filled by L1. L2 shall restore values of full covariance matrix according to the rule of Cov(i, j) = conjugate(Cov(j, i)) for any j > i.

Note: The number of TRXs may be smaller than the total number of the tx array, due to split panel configuration used.

[CB015122-A]

end

[End CB015122-A]

---

#### 3.18.1.3.0-3 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Covariance matrix per UE (ID: 11154462)

**3.18.1.3.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13370953`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

This requirement has been moved to L1-DU, see [13331607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_UX1xktWeEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-A]

If periodic sub-band SRS for multiple UEs are scheduled in SRS slot, if NRBTS.actEcpri72e is set to ‘disabled’, 5G-L1-UL will report one covariance matrix per set of parameters {comb offset, cyclic shift, polarization, direction} to 5G-L2-PS. For a given UE sounding on 2 SRS ports, the parameter comb offset is the same on both ports.

if NRBTS.actEcpri72e is set to other value than ‘disabled’, 5G-L1-UL will report one covariance matrix per set of parameters {comb offset, cyclic shift, direction} to 5G-L2-PS. For a given UE sounding on 2 SRS ports, the parameter comb offset is the same on both ports.

The size of horizontal and vertical instantaneous covariance matrices is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2158\_replaced([11154448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Based on UE’s capability, if UE is configured with single port SRS, if NRBTS.actEcpri72e is set to ‘disabled’, 5G-L1-UL will report 4 instantaneous covariance matrices to upper layer; NRBTS.actEcpri72e is set to other value than ‘disabled’, 5G-L1-radio will report 2 instantaneous covariance matrices to upper layer. If UE is configured with two-port SRS, if NRBTS.actEcpri72e is set to ‘disabled’, 5G-L1-UL will report 8 instantaneous covariance matrices. Reported covariance matrices per UE are listed in the below table. NRBTS.actEcpri72e is set to other value than ‘disabled’, 5G-L1-radio will report 4 covariance matrices to upper layer. The table assumes transmissionComb = n2 and cyclicShift-n2 = 0 on SRS.

if NRBTS.actEcpri72e is set to ‘disabled’:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **SRS configuration** | **SRS port** | **Cyclic shifts** | **Directions** | **Polarizations** | **Covariance matrix** |
| Single port | 1000 (p0) | CS0 | H | +45 | Cov(H, p0, +45) |
| CS0 | H | -45 | Cov(H, p0, -45) |  |  |
| CS0 | V | +45 | Cov(V, p0, +45) |  |  |
| CS0 | V | -45 | Cov(V, p0, -45) |  |  |
| Two ports | 1000 (p0) | CS0 | H | +45 | Cov(H, p0, +45) |
| CS0 | H | -45 | Cov(H, p0, -45) |  |  |
| CS0 | V | +45 | Cov(V, p0, +45) |  |  |
| CS0 | V | -45 | Cov(V, p0, -45) |  |  |
| 1001 (p1) | CS4 | H | +45 | Cov(H, p1, +45) |  |
| CS4 | H | -45 | Cov(H, p1, -45) |  |  |
| CS4 | V | +45 | Cov(V, p1, +45) |  |  |
| CS4 | V | -45 | Cov(V, p1, -45) |  |  |

if NRBTS.actEcpri72e is set to other value than ‘disabled’:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **SRS configuration** | **SRS port** | **Cyclic shifts** | **Directions** | **Covariance matrix** |
| Single port | 1000 (p0) | CS0 | H | Cov(H, p0) |
| CS0 | V | Cov(V, p0) |  |  |
| Two ports | 1000 (p0) | CS0 | H | Cov(H, p0) |
| CS0 | V | Cov(V, p0) |  |  |
| 1001 (p1) | CS4 | H | Cov(H, p1) |  |
| CS4 | V | Cov(V, p1) |  |  |

[CB015122-A]

end

[End CB015122-A]

#### 3.18.1.3.0-4 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Combine covariance matrices per UE (ID: 11154482)

**3.18.1.3.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `13370986`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

This requirement has been moved to L1-DU, [13332437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_DVMIENXOEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-A]

For each direction (H and V), instantaneous covariance matrices from different polarities (only for eCPRI 7-2a)**and ports shall be combined into one instantaneous covariance matrix by averaging over all instantaneous covariance matrices obtained for the same UE at the same time. For eCPRI 7-2e, before calculating average values, the covariance matrices shall be validated according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2165\_replaced([11154516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Only if the covariance matrix is valid, then perform the averaging.**

For eCPRI 7-2a (NRBTS.actEcpri72e is set to ‘disabled’):

If the number of SRS ports is one:

Cov(H) = (Cov(H, p0, +45) + Cov(H, p0, -45)) / 2

Cov(V) = (Cov(V, p0, +45) + Cov(V, p0, -45)) / 2

If the number of SRS ports is two:

Cov(H) = (Cov(H, p0, +45) + Cov(H, p0, -45) + Cov(H, p1, +45) + Cov(H, p1, -45)) / 4

Cov(V) = (Cov(V, p0, +45) + Cov(V, p0, -45) + Cov(V, p1, +45) + Cov(V, p1, -45)) / 4

For eCPRI 7-2e (NRBTS.actEcpri72e is set to other value than ‘disabled’):

If the number of SRS ports is one:

The received covariance matrix is already averaged over RU polarities in L1-radio, so no average in L2.

If the number of SRS ports is two:

Cov(H) = (Cov(H, p0) + Cov(H, p1)) / 2

Cov(V) = (Cov(V, p0) + Cov(V, p1)) / 2

[CB015122-A]

end

[End CB015122-A]

---

#### 3.18.1.3.0-5 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Instantaneous Covariance matrix validation (ID: 11154500)

**3.18.1.3.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13378822`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

This requirement has been moved to L1-DU, details for instantaneous CoMa validation are described in L1-DU, [13367270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Lj97U_bTEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-A]

5G-L2-PS shall validate the instantaneous covariance matrix Cov(H) and Cov(V), according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2165\_replaced([11154516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (see [11154516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

Note: No instantaneous covariance matrix validation needed anymore.

[CB015122-A]

#### 3.18.1.3.0-6 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Covariance matrix validation (ID: 11154516)

**3.18.1.3.0-6.0-6**  (ID: `13371028`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
13371028:
SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-A]
if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1
The requirement has been moved to L1-DU, [13367270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Lj97U_bTEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
else
[End CB015122-A]
**For the case of eCPRI 7-2e:**
The covariance matrix shall be validated in L1 Radio (supported by CB010887). 5G-L2-PS shall maintain averaged SRS power according to algorithm defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27600\_replaced([11154591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
**For the case of eCPRI 7-2a:**
5G-L2-PS shall validate covariance matrix Cov(H) and Cov(V) before filtering them over time via an IIR filte . It includes below steps:
 
1. Calculate SRS power per virtual antenna according to below equations:
 
      [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$rrmSrsPower\_{relative} = 10 \times \log\_{10}\left(\frac{Tr(R\_h) + Tr(R\_v)}{N\_h + N\_v}\right)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10207.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
    Convert rrmSrsPowerrelative to dBm unit as rrmSrsPowerdBm, the details are defined is EFS.
 
where
- Tr(R) returns sum of diagonal elements in matrix R;
- Rh is the covariance matrix Cov(H), see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2162\_replaced([11154482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
- Rv is the covariance matrix Cov(V), see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2162\_replaced([11154482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
    For covariance matrix validation for SB CoMa correlation metric (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22742\_replaced([11157172](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks6SFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall validate the instantaneous covariance matrix per port (Cov\_pi(H) and Cov\_pi(V) in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6991\_replaced([11155895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), not per SRS resource as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2162\_replaced([11154482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
- Rh is the covariance matrix Cov\_pi(H)
- Rv is the covariance matrix Cov\_pi(V) 
- Nh is the number of columns in the matrix Rh. If Nh = 1, values of Tr(Rh) and Nh shall not be considered in above equation.
- Nv is the number of columns in the matrix Rv. If Nv = 1, valuess of Tr(Rv) and Nv shall not be considered in above equation.
     
2. If the value of rrmSrsPowerdBm is higher than **rrmSrsPowerThreshold for UL/**srsPowerThresholdForDlBm for DL, the covariance matrix is valid, otherwise it is not valid.\*\*\*\*
      The rrmSrsPowerThreshold is NRCELL/srsForBeamMgmt/srsPowerThresholdForUlBm.
      The srsPowerThresholdForDlBm is NRCELL/srsForBeamMgmt/srsPowerThresholdForDlBm.
 
For more information, please refer to the document at the below link:
[CB015122-A]
end
[End CB015122-A]

#### 3.18.1.3.0-7 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Filter CoMa per UE in time domain (ID: 11154579)

**3.18.1.3.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `13371061`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The requirement has been moved to L1-DU, [13331611.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-DV_UdWeEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

else

[End CB015122-A]

The instantaneous covariance matrics Cov(H) and Cov(V) shall be used to update the respective long-term covariance matrices via an IIR filter which is defined as below (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2164\_replaced([11154500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

**rrmAvgCov = (1 - rrmUlCoMaFilterCoefficient) \* rrmAvgCov + rrmUlCoMaFilterCoefficient \* rrmInstCov**

where

* rrmInstCov is the average over all isntantaneous covariance matrices (Cov(H) and Cov(V)) received for a given UE at the same time 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2162\_replaced([11154482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
* rrmCoMaFilterCoefficient is the filter coefficient. It shall be calculated as the value of **(SRS periodicity/rrmUlBeamSelectTimer). The** rrmUlBeamSelectTimer is the timer duration (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2173\_replaced([11154691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), for UL beam selection. The SRS periodicity is from the periodicityAndOffset in SRS configuration (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2147\_replaced([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*\*\*

- Note: When rrmCoMaFilterCoefficient is less than 1.0, if the number of to-be-averaged CoMa is less than or equal to **rrmNumOfCoMa (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2138\_replaced([11154054](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqadvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the rrmAvgCov shall be calculated as arithmetic average, if the number of to-be-averaged CoMa is higher than** rrmNumOfCoMa, the rrmAvgCov shall be calculated according to above IIR filter equation.AvgCov is the averaged covariance matrix with IIR filter;\*\*\*\*

[CB015122-A]

end

[End CB015122-A]

#### 3.18.1.3.0-8 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) SRS power averaging from CoMa report (ID: 11154591)

**3.18.1.3.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11154597`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
This requirement only applies to eCPRI 7-2e.

If NIDD:actDlSrsSubbandBm is TRUE, 5G-L2-PS shall average SRS power when it receives non-DTX CoMa report from L1 Radio using the IIR filter defined as below. Only the CoMa that are used for DL BM shall be considered. The averaged SRS power in unit of dBm, rrmAvgSrsPower\_dbm, shall be calculated from rrmAvgSrsPower\_linear.

rrmAvgSrsPower\_linear = (1 - rrmUlCoMaFilterCoefficient) \* rrmAvgSrsPower\_linear + rrmUlCoMaFilterCoefficient \* rrmInstSrsPower\_linear

where

* rrmAvgSrsPower\_linear is the averaged linear SRS power;
* rrmInstSrsPower\_linear is the instantaneous linear SRS power reported by L1 Radio in CoMa report. For example, UE is 2T4R, L1 Radio shall report 4 SRS power values in unit of dBm in CoMa report: p0 (45), p0 (-45), p1 (45), p1 (-45), 5G-L2-PS shall covert these power values to linear values and calculate linear arithmetic average value among these power values. The linear arithmetic average value is rrmInstSrsPower\_linear;
* rrmCoMaFilterCoefficient is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2166\_replaced([11154579](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

NOTE: When rrmCoMaFilterCoefficient is less than 1.0, if the number of CoMa report received from L1 Radio is less than or equal to rrmNumOfCoMa (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2138\_replaced([11154054](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqadvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the rrmAvgSrsPower\_linear shall be calculated as arithmetic average, otherwise it shall be calculated according to above IIR filter equation.

---

### 3.18.1.4 Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver

#### 3.18.1.4.0-1 Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver Simplified approach with 2D-DFT beams (informative) (ID: 11154608)

**3.18.1.4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13371110`)

Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver
13371110:
Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver
[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

else

[End CB015122-A]

This is an informative requirement to explain how to simplify the calculation of [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written as $w\_k^H \cdot R\_{SRS} \cdot w\_k$. The characters are in a dark color against a light background. The expression appears to be slightly blurred.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] if beams are 2D-DFT beams.

For each 2D-DFT beam, its beam weights are the Kronecker product of DFT beams in vertical and horizontal directions. The 2D-DFT beam weight [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w k" in a stylized font. The letters are blurred and have a gradient effect, with colors ranging from orange and yellow to blue and purple. The background is white, and the text is framed by a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] can be represented as [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression written in a blurry, light-colored font against a white background. The expression appears to be "w\_{v,i} ⊗ w\_{h,j}". The symbol "⊗" is a circled cross, commonly used to denote the Kronecker product.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] where [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w v,i" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient of blue, yellow, and orange, and have a slight glow effect. The text is positioned in the lower left corner of a black background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] **is DFT beam in vertical direction, [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w h j" in a blurry, stylized font with a gradient effect. The letters are colored in shades of orange, yellow, and blue.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] is DFT beam in horizontal direction. In below equation, [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w k" in a stylized font. The letters are blurred and have a gradient effect, with colors ranging from orange and yellow to blue and purple. The background is white, and the text is framed by a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.002.png[/image\_path][/image-5] / [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w v,i" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient of blue, orange, and yellow, and have a slight glow effect. The text is positioned in the lower left quadrant of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.006.png[/image\_path][/image-6] / [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w h j" in a blurry, stylized font with a gradient effect. The letters are colored in shades of orange, yellow, and blue.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.005.png[/image\_path][/image-7] are vertical vectors which include weights of beams.**

[image-8][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written as $w\_k^H \cdot R\_{SRS} \cdot w\_k$. The characters are in a dark color against a light background. The expression appears to be slightly blurred.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.001.png[/image\_path][/image-8]

[image-9][image\_desc]= (w\_{v,i} \otimes w\_{h,j})^H \cdot (R\_{SRS,v} \otimes R\_{SRS,h}) \cdot (w\_{v,i} \otimes w\_{h,j})[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.007.png[/image\_path][/image-9]

[image-10][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$$ = (w\_{v,i}^H \otimes w\_{h,j}^H)(R\_{SRS,v} \cdot W\_{v,i}) \otimes (R\_{SRS,h} \cdot W\_{h,j}) $$
The equation involves several mathematical symbols and variables, including:
- An equals sign (=)
- Parentheses ()
- Subscripts (v,i), (h,j), (SRS,v), (SRS,h)
- Superscript H (Hermitian transpose)
- The tensor product symbol ($\otimes$)
- A multiplication dot ($\cdot$)
- Variables w, R, and W.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.008.png[/image\_path][/image-10]

[image-11][image\_desc]= (w\_{v,i}^H \cdot R\_{SRS,v} \cdot w\_{v,i}) \otimes (w\_{h,j}^H \cdot R\_{SRS,h} \cdot w\_{h,j})[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.009.png[/image\_path][/image-11]

[image-12][image\_desc]= (W\_{v,i}^H \cdot R\_{SRS,v} \cdot W\_{v,i}) \cdot (W\_{h,j}^H \cdot R\_{SRS,h} \cdot W\_{h,j})[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10214.010.png[/image\_path][/image-12]

#### 3.18.1.4.0-2 Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver Beamforming weights of UL beams (ID: 11154681)

**3.18.1.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13371113`)

Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver
[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The requirement has been moved to L1-DU, [13337075](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZK_mUdm2EfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

For configured UL beamset, then L2-PS shall inform lower layer (L1-DU) about number of best beams which is 2 for

NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is equal to 4.

else

[End CB015122-A]

The L3 shall send sets of horizontal and vertical DFT beams to 5G-L2-PS during the cell setup procedure. The 2D-DFT beams are Kronecker products of horizontal and vertical DFT beams . Note: some horizontal and vertical DFT beams may be excluded by L3 for performance reason.

NOTE: If NIDD:actUlMuMimo is enabled, the L3 shall always shall send tapered and non-tapered sets of horizontal and vertical DFT beams with to 5G-L2-PS during the cell setup procedure.

If the configured UL beamset is NOT 2D-DFT beams, the L3 shall send the mapping table between 2D-DFT beams and beams in beamset to 5G-L2-PS during the cell setup procedure.

[CB015122-A]

end

#### 3.18.1.4.0-3 Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver Calculate the best UL beam (ID: 11154691)

**3.18.1.4.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13371137`)

Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver
[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

When the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer of a UE is expired, the below step shall be executed:**

1. Restart the timer of **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer with parameter value delivered from gNB-CU-CP, see [13378910](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_KtvcY_3CEfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).**

Other steps have been moved to L1-DU, [13337075](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZK_mUdm2EfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-A]

This requirement defines the algorithm for finding the best UL beam from covariance matrices which are averaged via the IIR filter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2166\_replaced([11154579](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The algorithm shall be triggered when the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer of UE is expired. The** rrmUlBeamSelectTimer shall be maintained per UE based.\*\*\*\*

Its slot duration shall be defined as R&D parameter (default value is 200 slot, reuse **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11383\_replaced([11113992](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpgYxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It shall not be be smaller than SRS periodicity in slot so** rrmUlCoMaFilterCoefficient in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2166\_replaced([11154579](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) will not be larger than 1). gNB-DU shall double **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer for the UEs described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29538\_replaced([11158109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_xqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**\*\*\*\*

When the **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer of a UE is expired, the below steps shall be executed:**

1. Restart the timer of **rrmUlBeamSelectTime.**

2. Find the best horizontal and vertical DFT beams (**hBest and** vBest) according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2176\_replaced([11154707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kstdwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*

3. If the configured UL beamset is 2D-DFT beams, the best UL beam is the Kronecker product of DFT beams **vBest and** hBest.\*\*\*\*

5. If the configured UL beamset is NOT 2D-DFT beams, 5G-L2-PS shall map the selected 2D-DFT beam to a UL beam according to the mapping table defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2171\_replaced([11154681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2vfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: the calculation of best UL beams shall be implemented in a parallel thread or process such as to decouple it form the normal scheduler process.

[CB015122-A]

end

[End CB015122-A]

---

#### 3.18.1.4.0-4 Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver Calculate the best 2D-DFT UL beam (ID: 11154707)

**3.18.1.4.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13371147`)

Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver
13371147:
Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver
[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The requirement has been moved to L1-DU, [13337124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wfJIodm-EfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-A]

This requirement defines the algorithm for finding **the best 2D-DFT UL beam. For further information, please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2169\_replaced([11154608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2u_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

1. Go through all horizontal DFT beams and find one oversampled DFT beam, **hBest, which maximizes the following term:**

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is: $W\_{h,j}^H \cdot R\_{SRS,h} \cdot W\_{h,j}$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10221.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where

- [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w h j" in a blurry, stylized font with a gradient effect. The letters are colored in shades of orange, yellow, and blue.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10221.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] **is a column vector which is compiled by weights of one horizontal oversampled DFT beam. 5G-L2-PS shall receive the set of horizontal oversampled DFT beams from CP-RT during cell setup procedure (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2171\_replaced([11154681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2vfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

- [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "RSRS,h" in a stylized font. The text is in a dark color with a slight gradient, and it is set against a white background. The letters are slightly blurred, giving them a soft appearance. The "R" is larger than the other letters and is positioned to the left of "SRS,h". The "SRS,h" is written in a smaller font and is positioned to the right of the "R". The comma and the "h" are slightly smaller than the "SRS" and are positioned below the baseline of the "SRS".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10221.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] **is the long-term covariance matrix in horizontal direction. see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2166\_replaced([11154579](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

2. Go through all vertical DFT beams and find one oversampled DFT beam, **vBest, which maximizes the following term:**

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is: $W\_{v,i}^H \cdot R\_{SRS,v} \cdot W\_{v,i}$. The expression consists of three terms multiplied together. The first term is $W\_{v,i}^H$, which represents the conjugate transpose of $W\_{v,i}$. The second term is $R\_{SRS,v}$, which is likely a matrix or a tensor. The third term is $W\_{v,i}$, which is the same as the first term's base. The dots between the terms indicate multiplication.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10221.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

where

- [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w v,i" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient of blue, yellow, and orange, and have a slight glow effect. The text is positioned in the lower left corner of a black background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10221.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] **is a column vector which is compiled by weights of a vertical oversampled DFT beam. 5G-L2-PS shall receive the set of vertical oversampled DFT beams from CP-RT during cell setup procedure (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2171\_replaced([11154681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2vfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

- [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "RSRS,v" in a stylized font. The text is black and appears to be slightly blurred. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10221.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5] **is the is compiled by, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2166\_replaced([11154579](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

3. The best 2D-DFT UL beam is the Kronecker product of oversampled DFT beams **vBest and** hBest.\*\*\*\*

In the procedure to go through all horizontal DFT beams and all vertcial DFT beams, L2RT shall store all the Kronecker product results of [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is: $W\_{h,j}^H R\_{SRS,h} W\_{h,j}$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10221.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6] and [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. L2RT shall store all the Kronecker product results of [image-10][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written as: $\hat{W}*{h,j}^H R*{SRS,h} \hat{W}*{h,j}$.
The expression consists of the following components:
- $\hat{W}*{h,j}^H$: This represents the conjugate transpose (Hermitian transpose) of a matrix denoted by $\hat{W}*{h,j}$. The hat symbol ($\hat{}$) often indicates an estimated quantity. The subscripts 'h' and 'j' likely represent indices or parameters.
- $R*{SRS,h}$: This represents a matrix denoted by $R\_{SRS,h}$. The subscript 'SRS' might stand for a specific type of matrix or operation, and 'h' again likely indicates an index or parameter.
- $\hat{W}*{h,j}$: This is the same matrix as mentioned earlier, $\hat{W}*{h,j}$.
The expression shows the product of these three components. The dots between the components indicate matrix multiplication.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10221.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10] and [image-11][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. It is represented as $\hat{w}\_{n,i}$, where $\hat{w}$ is a variable with a hat symbol above it, and $n$ and $i$ are subscripts. The hat symbol typically denotes an estimated or predicted value. The colors in the image are a mix of blue, orange, and yellow, suggesting a gradient or a stylized rendering of the mathematical notation.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10221.013.png[/image\_path][/image-12] is a column vector which comprises tapered weights of one horizontal oversampled DFT beam;

The expression appears to be "$\hat{W}\_{v,i}$".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10221.014.png[/image\_path][/image-13] is a column vector which comprises tapered weights of a vertical oversampled DFT beam**.**

NOTE: The tapered beam and non-tapered beam shall be one-to-one mapping.

#### 3.18.1.4.0-5 Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver Calculate the second-best UL beam (ID: 11154774)

This algorithm defines how to find the second-best UL beam. This algorithm shall be executed if the receiver type is 4RX (the UL subcell type is C4) or if Dl also needs beams from this SRS resource set as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2181 or if the UL subcell is configured with 8 or 16 **spatial streams for a given subcell(5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

1. Find the second-best horizontal and vertical DFT beams (**hSecondBest and** vSecondBest)  according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2181\_replaced([11154797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kstdx_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*

2. If the configured UL beamset is 2D-DFT beams, the second-best UL beam is the Kronecker product of **vSecondBest and** hSecondBest.\*\*\*\*

3. If the configured UL beamset is NOT 2D-DFT beams, 5G-L2-PS shall map the selected 2D-DFT beam to a UL beam according to the mapping table defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2171\_replaced([11154681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2vfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: the calculation of second best UL beams shall be implemented in a parallel thread or process such as to decouple it form the normal scheduler process.
