#### 3.18.1.4.0-6 Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver Calculate the second-best 2D-DFT UL beam (ID: 11154797)

**3.18.1.4.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13372532`)

Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver
13372532:
Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver
[CB015122-A]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The requirement has been moved to L1-DU, [13337175](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ogBjttnDEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-A]

This requirement defines the algorithm for finding **the second-best 2D-DFT UL beam.**

After the best 2D-DFT beam is selected (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2176\_replaced([11154707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kstdwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the second-best 2D-DFT UL beam is the one which meets below equation:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is:
$$ \underset{w\_k}{\arg \max} (w\_k^H \cdot R'\_{SRS} \cdot w\_k) $$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

The [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written in a blurry, white font against a white background. The expression reads: $W\_k^H \cdot R'\_{SRS} \cdot W\_k$. The characters are: 'W', a subscript 'k', a superscript 'H', a dot, 'R', a prime symbol, a subscript 'SRS', a dot, and 'W' with a subscript 'k'.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] **can be derived by the below equation if beams are 2D-DFT beams:**

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a white background. The equation is presented in two lines.
The first line is:
$w\_k^H R'*{SRS} w\_k = w\_k^H R*{SRS} w\_k - \lambda\_{Best} \* w\_k^H \frac{w\_{best}}{||w\_{best}||} \* \frac{w\_{best}^H}{||w\_{best}||}$
The second line is:
$= (w\_{k,v}^H R\_{SRS,v} w\_{k,v}) \* (w\_{k,h}^H R\_{SRS,h} w\_{k,h}) - \lambda\_{Best} \* \frac{1}{N} \* |w\_{k,v}^H w\_{best,v}|^2 \* |w\_{k,h}^H w\_{best,h}|^2$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

where:

- [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Wk,v". The text is in a stylized font with a gradient of colors, appearing to be a mix of blue, orange, and yellow. The letters are slightly blurred, and the background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] and [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression written in a stylized font. The expression appears to be "Wk,h". The letters and subscripts are rendered with a gradient effect, giving them a colorful and somewhat translucent appearance. The background is white, and the expression is positioned in the lower-left quadrant of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]  are vertical and horizontal DFT beams of 2D-DFT beam [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains blurry, colorful text that is difficult to read. The text appears to be "wyk".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5];

- [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w best,v" in a stylized font. The text is blurry and appears to be in a dark color against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6] and [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains the text "W best,h". The text is in a dark color and appears to be slightly blurry.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7]  are vertical and horizontal DFT beams of the best 2D-DFT beam [image-8][image\_desc]The image contains the text "W best" in a stylized font with a rainbow gradient effect. The text is blurry and has a slight glow. The background is white, and the text is framed by a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8] (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2176\_replaced([11154707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kstdwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

- lamdaBest **equals to** [image-9][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$$ \frac{1}{N} \* (W\_{beat,v}^H \* R\_{SRS,v} \* W\_{beat,v}) \* (W\_{beat,h}^H \* R\_{SRS,h} \* W\_{beat,h}) $$
The formula involves the following variables:
- N: A scalar value, likely representing a count or dimension.
- $W\_{beat,v}$: A matrix or vector, possibly representing beamforming weights for the vertical direction. The superscript 'H' indicates the conjugate transpose.
- $R\_{SRS,v}$: A matrix, likely representing a covariance matrix for the SRS (Sounding Reference Signal) in the vertical direction.
- $W\_{beat,h}$: A matrix or vector, possibly representing beamforming weights for the horizontal direction.
- $R\_{SRS,h}$: A matrix, likely representing a covariance matrix for the SRS in the horizontal direction.
The formula calculates a product of two terms, each of which is a product of a conjugate transpose of beamforming weights, a covariance matrix, and the beamforming weights themselves. This type of expression is common in signal processing, particularly in areas like array processing, beamforming, and channel estimation, where it might represent a performance metric or a calculation related to signal power or gain.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9];\*\*\*\*

- N equals to rrmTrxColumn\*rrmTrxRow.

Notes: the performance can be optimized for calculating below values:

- To speed up calculation of [image-10][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is enclosed in absolute value bars and raised to the power of 2. Inside the absolute value bars, there is a product of two terms. The first term is $w\_{v,i}^H$, where $w$ is a variable, $v$ is a subscript, $i$ is a subscript, and $H$ is a superscript. The second term is $w\_{v,vBest}$, where $w$ is a variable, $v$ is a subscript, and $vBest$ is a subscript. There is a dot between the two terms, indicating multiplication.
The expression is: $|w\_{v,i}^H \cdot w\_{v,vBest}|^2$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10], a lookup table can be calculated during the cell setup which includes correlations between all vertical DFT beams.

- To speed up calculation of [image-11][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is enclosed in absolute value bars and raised to the power of 2. Inside the absolute value bars, there is a product of two terms. The first term is $W\_{h,j}^H$, and the second term is $W\_{h,hBest}$. The dot between the two terms indicates multiplication.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.012.png[/image\_path][/image-11], a lookup table can be calculated during the cell setup which includes correlations between all horizontal DFT beams.

- Values of [image-12][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is: $W\_{v,i}^H \cdot R\_{SRS,v} \cdot W\_{v,i}$. The expression consists of three terms multiplied together, separated by dots representing multiplication. The first term is $W\_{v,i}^H$, where $W$ is a variable, $v$ and $i$ are subscripts, and $H$ is a superscript. The second term is $R\_{SRS,v}$, where $R$ is a variable, $SRS$ is a subscript, and $v$ is a subscript. The third term is $W\_{v,i}$, which is identical to the first term without the superscript $H$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.013.png[/image\_path][/image-12] **,** [image-13][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is: $W\_{h\_j}^H \cdot R\_{SRS,h} \cdot W\_{h\_j}$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.014.png[/image\_path][/image-13] **and [image-14][image\_desc]The image contains the text "lambdaBest" in a blurry, sans-serif font. The text is horizontally aligned and appears to be in a dark color with a slight gradient or halo effect. The background is a light, off-white color.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.015.png[/image\_path][/image-14]** are already calculated at the stage of finding the best 2D-DFT beam in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2176\_replaced([11154707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kstdwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). No need to calculate them again in this algorithm.***\****\*

To find the second-best UL 2D-DFT beam, the value of [image-15][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is: $W\_k^H \cdot R'\_{SRS} \cdot W\_k$. The characters are in a sans-serif font and are slightly blurred. The expression appears to be a scalar value, likely representing a quadratic form.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.016.png[/image\_path][/image-15] shall be maximized according to below steps:

1. Go through available combinations of horizontal and vertical DFT beams and find the vertical DFT beam (**vSecondBest) and the horizontal DFT beam (**hSecondBest) that can maximize the value of [image-16][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is: $W\_k^H \cdot R'\_{SRS} \cdot W\_k$. The characters are in a sans-serif font and are slightly blurred. The expression appears to be a scalar value, likely representing a quadratic form.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.016.png[/image\_path][/image-16].\*\*\*\*

2. The 2D-DFT beam (Kronecker product of **vSecondBest and** hSecondBest) is a candidate of the second-best 2D-DFT beam.\*\*\*\*

3. If the configured UL beamset is NOT 2D-DFT beams, find UL beam from the candidate according to the mapping table defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2171\_replaced([11154681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2vfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If the UL beam is same as the best UL beam, go to step 1 to find a new candidate.

4. Calculate correlation between candidate and the best 2D-DFT beam. If  [image-17][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical inequality. The inequality is:
$|w\_{v,i}^H \cdot w\_{v,vBest}| / ||w\_{v,vBest}|| \cdot |w\_{h,i}^H \cdot w\_{h,Best}| \geq (rmTrxColumn + rmTrxRow) \cdot rm2ndBeamCorrThreshold$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10227.017.png[/image\_path][/image-17], save this candidate as **nonOptimalCandidate and go to step 1 to find a new candidate. Value of rrmTrxColumn and rrmTrxRow are defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2158\_replaced([11154448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The** rrm2ndBeamCorrThreshold shall be implemented as RD parameter. Its default value is **0.5.**\*\*\*\*

5. If the candidate meets above conditions, it is the second-best 2D-DFT beam.

6. If no candidate can be found, use **nonOptimalCandidate as the second-best 2D-DFT beam.**

If (actDlSrsBm is true) and (*srsTypeAllocForDlBm is not 'antena switching') and (the UE only has codebook SRS resource set configured while antenna switching SRS resource set is not): best/2nd best beams shall be checked whether they are valid for Dl usage as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7008\_replaced([11156149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The validity of beams for Dl shall not impact the beam usage for Ul.*

Notes: Optimization of searching vSecondBest and hSecondBest is left to CP3.

[CB015122-A]

end

[End CB015122-A]

---

#### 3.18.1.4.0-7 Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver Workaround solution for the pronto 03016370 high rBLER issue in TMO (ID: 11154881)

**3.18.1.4.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `11154895`)

Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver
Due to the pronto 03016370, there is higher residual HARQ BLER issue in TMO field. It's similar as the PR 02688605 for DL. Before the problem is solved between RU and L1, a workaround solution is requested in L2-PS: if the current PUSCH transmission is HARQ retransmission with the number of retransmission >= a given threshold, then use the legacy beams (SSB/Refined beams) instead of SRS beams for the current PUSCH transmission.

If actUlSrsBm = true **AND NRCELL.actSrsUlBeamFallbackByRetrx = true** AND the current number of HARQ retransmission >= rdSrsBeamFallbackByReTrxThrd [PR852940] AND the current beam for PUSCH is DFT beam AND the used beam for previous PUSCH (re)transmission on the current HARQ process is DFT beam [End PR852940] (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17126\_replaced([11114114](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kphm6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then\*\*\*\*

 The beam(s) of PUSCH for following HARQ retransmission shall be SSB/Refined beams defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20070\_replaced([11112279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUyk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The beam change does not affect on the SRS state defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2136\_replaced([11154035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqac_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **[Before CNI-133534-B] It is only the beam replacement for PUSCH transmission in the scheduling occasion.** [CNI-133534-B] The time duration of using legacy beams for PUSCH is dependent on the value of NIDD parameter srsUlBeamFallbackOption:\*\*\*\*

 If srsUlBeamFallbackOption = "fallback once", then legacy beam is only used for the following HARQ retransmission of this TB. For the next TB transmission, SRS beam is used if it is valid.

 If srsUlBeamFallbackOption = "fallback until next beam calculation", then legacy beam is used until the next beam selection time (rrmUlBeamSelectTimer expired). When rrmUlBeamSelectTimer expired, SRS beam is used according to beam selection method (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2173\_replaced([11154691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 If srsUlBeamFallbackOption = "fallback until different beam available", then until the next beam selection time (rrmUlBeamSelectTimer expired) legacy beam is used. When rrmUlBeamSelectTimer expired,  if averaged CoMa updated condition (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29619\_replaced([11155739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvMPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is met, gNB-DU executes the beams selection algorithms defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2173\_replaced([11154691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

o If the new best SRS beam is different with the last best SRS beam, then stop fallback and use SRS beam;

o otherwise use the legacy beam until the next beam selection time.

**[End CNI-133534-B]**

Note: This workaround solution is only enabled before the SRS lost issue is solved. When the SRS lost issue is solved, this workaround solution shall be disabled or removed.

---

#### 3.18.1.4.0-8 Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver Supporting of srsUlBeamFallbackOption online modification (ID: 11154901)

**3.18.1.4.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11154906`)

Beam Selection for UL 4RX receiver
The parameter srsUlBeamFallbackOption can be online modified. When the value of srsUlBeamFallbackOption is online modified:

 For UEs who are not triggered to fallback, the new value shall take effect immediately. From the current slot, L2-PS shall use the new value to determine the fallback option.

 For UEs who are already triggered to fallback, the new value shall take effect as below:

o If the old value is “fallback once”, then for UEs who are using legacy beam(SSB beam) as fallback, L2-PS shall continue to use legacy beam for the current TB. From next TB transmission, L2-PS shall stop fallback and determine if UEs shall be fallback to legacy beams according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22392\_replaced([11154881](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kstdyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the new value of srsUlBeamFallbackOption.

o If the old value is "fallback until next beam calculation", then for UEs who are using legacy beam(SSB beam) as fallback, L2-PS shall continue to use legacy beam until next beam selection time (rrmUlBeamSelectTimer expired). From next beam selection time, L2-PS shall stop fallback and determine if UEs shall be fallback to legacy beams according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22392\_replaced([11154881](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kstdyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the new value of srsUlBeamFallbackOption.

o If the old value is "fallback until different beam available",  then for UEs who are using legacy beam(SSB beam) as fallback, L2-PS shall continue to use legacy beam until next beam selection time (rrmUlBeamSelectTimer expired). From next beam selection time, no matter if the new selected best SRS beam is same as the old best SRS beam or not, L2-PS shall stop fallback. And from next beam selection time, L2-PS shall determine if UEs shall be fallback to legacy beams according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22392\_replaced([11154881](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kstdyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the new value of srsUlBeamFallbackOption.

---

**3.18.1.5.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13372822`)

osDFT Beam Selection for UL 8RX/16RX receiver
Beam type in beam selection

**3.18.1.5.0-1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13372877`)

osDFT Beam Selection for UL 8RX/16RX receiver
When the configured UL beamset is 2D-DFT beams and the parameter `NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming` is equal to 16, the gNB-DU shall set the `rrmUlSplitPanelModeFor16Rx` parameter based on the value of rrmPanelSplitMode , see [13372822](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_iAbQQ_rDEfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), as follows:

* If rrmPanelSplitMode is 'FULL\_PANEL', the gNB-DU shall set `rrmUlSplitPanelModeFor16Rx` to 'none'.
* If rrmPanelSplitMode is 'UD\_MODE', the gNB-DU shall set `rrmUlSplitPanelModeFor16Rx` to 'UD split mode'.
* For all other values of rrmPanelSplitMode, the gNB-DU shall set `rrmUlSplitPanelModeFor16Rx` to 'hybrid split mode'.

Note:

The parameter rrmPanelSplitMode is received from L1-DU via parameter panelMode, detailed in requirement [13338298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NKTPBdqPEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and [13338301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_iF44INqPEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

The parameter `rrmUlSplitPanelModeFor16Rx` is used in requirement [11151025](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksW4cvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

This algorithm defines how to find the 3rd, 4th.. Nth best UL beam, where N refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27644\_replaced([11154947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE2PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

3.  If the configured UL beamset is NOT 2D-DFT beams, 5G-L2-PS shall map the selected 2D-DFT beam to a UL beam according to the mapping table defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2171\_replaced([11154681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2vfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

To find the m-th (m >2) UL 2D-DFT beam, the value of [image-10][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written in a blurry, white font against a white background. The expression reads: $W\_k^H \cdot R'*{SRS} \cdot W\_k$. The characters are: 'W', a subscript 'k', a superscript 'H', a dot, 'R', a prime symbol, a subscript 'SRS', a dot, and 'W' with a subscript 'k'.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10251.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10] shall be maximized according to below steps:
1. Go through available combinations of horizontal and vertical DFT beams and find [image-11][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10251.012.png[/image\_path][/image-11] DFT beam and  [image-12][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10251.013.png[/image\_path][/image-12] DFT beam that can maximize the value of [image-13][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written in a blurry, white font against a white background. The expression reads: $W\_k^H \cdot R'*{SRS} \cdot W\_k$. The characters are: 'W', a subscript 'k', a superscript 'H', a dot, 'R', a prime symbol, a subscript 'SRS', a dot, and 'W' with a subscript 'k'.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10251.011.png[/image\_path][/image-13].
2. The 2D-DFT beam (Kronecker product of vertical DFT beam and horizontal DFT beam) is a candidate of the m-th (m >2) 2D-DFT beam.
 
3. If the configured UL beamset is NOT 2D-DFT beams, find UL beam from the candidate according to the mapping table defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2171\_replaced([11154681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2vfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If the UL beam is same as one of the first m-1 best beams, go to step 1 to find a new candidate.
 
4. Calculate correlation between candidate and the first m-1 best 2D-DFT beam. If 
[image-14][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10251.014.png[/image\_path][/image-14]
, save this candidate as* *nonOptimalCandidate and go to step 1 to find a new candidate, where, the value of* rrmTrxColumn and *rrmTrxRow are defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2158\_replaced([11154448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),* correlation is defined as rd3rdBeamCorrThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_30861\_replaced([11158895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktF4QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rd4thBeamCorrThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_30865\_replaced([11158904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktF4RPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the 3rd and 4th best beam correlation check and defined as rdBeamCorrThd for the 5th best beam ~ Nth best beam correlation check.***\**
 
5. If the candidate meets above conditions, it is the m-th best 2D-DFT beam.
 
6. If no candidate can be found, use** nonOptimalCandidate as the m-th best 2D-DFT beam.\*\*
[CB015122-C]
end
[End CB015122-C]

**3.18.1.5.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11155149`)

osDFT Beam Selection for UL 8RX/16RX receiver

**3.18.1.5.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13378031`)

osDFT Beam Selection for UL 8RX/16RX receiver
13378031:
osDFT Beam Selection for UL 8RX/16RX receiver
[CB015122-C]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The requirement has been moved to L1-DU, see [13338460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_RhXuYdq6EfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-C]

This requirement defines the algorithm for finding **the first-best 2D-DFT UL horizontal beam and the first-best 2D-DFT UL vertical beam.**

1. Go through all horizontal DFT beams and find one DFT beam, **hBest, which maximizes the following equation:**

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is: $W\_{h,j}^H \cdot R\_{SRS,h} \cdot W\_{h,j}$. The expression consists of three terms multiplied together. The first term is $W\_{h,j}^H$, which represents the conjugate transpose of $W\_{h,j}$. The second term is $R\_{SRS,h}$, and the third term is $W\_{h,j}$. The dots between the terms indicate multiplication.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10257.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where

- [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w h j" in a blurry, stylized font with a gradient effect. The letters are colored in shades of orange, yellow, and blue.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10257.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] **is a vertical vector which includes weights of one horizontal DFT beam. 5G-L2-PS shall receive the set of horizontal DFT beams from CP-RT during cell setup procedure (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2171\_replaced([11154681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2vfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

- [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "RSRS,h" in a stylized font. The text is black with a slight gradient effect, appearing to be on a white background. The letters are slightly blurred, and the overall image quality is not very high.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10257.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] **is covariance matrix Cov(H). See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2166\_replaced([11154579](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

2. Go through all vertical DFT beams and find one DFT beam, **vBest, which maximized the following equation:**

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is: $W\_{v,i}^H \cdot R\_{SRS,v} \cdot W\_{v,i}$. The expression consists of three terms multiplied together. The first term is $W\_{v,i}^H$, which represents the conjugate transpose of $W\_{v,i}$. The second term is $R\_{SRS,v}$, which is likely a matrix or a tensor. The third term is $W\_{v,i}$, which is the same as the first term's base. The dots between the terms indicate multiplication.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10257.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

where

- [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w v,i" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient of blue, yellow, and orange, and have a slight glow effect. The text is positioned in the lower left corner of a black background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10257.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] **is a vertical vector which includes weights of a vertical DFT beam. 5G-L2-PS shall receive the set of vertical DFT beams from CP-RT during cell setup procedure (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2171\_replaced([11154681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2vfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

- [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "RSRS,v" in a stylized font. The text is dark and appears to be slightly blurred. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10257.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5] **is the covariance matrix Cov(V). See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2166\_replaced([11154579](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

[CB015122-C]

end

[End CB015122-C]

If the configured UL beamset is 2D-DFT beams, L2PS shall select N best beams, where N refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27644\_replaced([11154947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE2PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Step 1: For the number of best horizontal beams (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20263\_replaced([1155132](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksur5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fmd_tauaapvfee-aqvopbp1qhq&artifactinmodule=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_ksur5fvsee-aqvopbp1qhq&oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9&componenturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2frm-projects%2f_t-lvkj5eee2a-5u7tzedra%2fcomponents%2f_ubjxej5eee2a-5u7tzedra"))) and number of vertical DFT beams (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20266\_replaced([1155132](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksur5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fmd_tauaapvfee-aqvopbp1qhq&artifactinmodule=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_ksur5fvsee-aqvopbp1qhq&oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9&componenturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2frm-projects%2f_t-lvkj5eee2a-5u7tzedra%2fcomponents%2f_ubjxej5eee2a-5u7tzedra"))), the beam power are calculated as:**

For horizontal beam i, [image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10264.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] ,  where, i = 1, 2, .. number of horizontal beams (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27647\_replaced([11155132](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksur5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For vertical beam j, [image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10264.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1], where [image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10264.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] and [image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10264.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20263\_replaced([11155183](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksur7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20266\_replaced([11155237](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksur7vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where, j = 1, 2, .. number of vertical beams (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27647\_replaced([11155132](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksur5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .

**Step 2: For each 2D-DFT beam k , the beam power is the product of horizontal beam power and vertical beam power:**

[image-4][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image, a corrupted file, or a deliberately black image with no discernible content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10264.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]

**Step3: Sort beam power [image-5][image\_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10264.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]of four 2D-DFT beams in Step2 from the higest to the lowest. When L2PS select the mth best beam, it shall be the Kronecker product of the vertical beam j and horizontal beam i which is corresponding to the mth highest power in Step2.**

**Note: If the configured UL beamset is NOT 2D-DFT beams, 5G-L2-PS shall map the selected 2D-DFT beam to a UL beam according to the mapping table defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2171\_replaced([11154681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2vfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

[CB015122-C]

end

[End CB015122-C]

##### 3.18.1.5.0-4 osDFT Beam Selection for UL 8RX/16RX receiver Find best beams with hybrid split panel beams (ID: 11155345)

**3.18.1.5.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13378048`)

osDFT Beam Selection for UL 8RX/16RX receiver
13378048:
osDFT Beam Selection for UL 8RX/16RX receiver
[CB015122-E]
if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1
The requirement has been moved to L1-DU, [13338298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NKTPBdqPEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
else
[End CB015122-E]
This requirement is only applied when the following conditions are satisfied.
- NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming = 16RX AND rdSuUeReceiverSize (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27595\_replaced([11114156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = 16 AND rdUlSplitPanelModeFor16RX (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29390\_replaced([11114144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = "hybrid split mode".
- SU-MIMO UEs.
**Note, for MU-MIMO UEs, always full panel beams after re-ordering in** Step1 shall be used.***\**\*Step1:After all** five beams are found in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20247\_replaced([11154965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20257\_replaced([11155127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksur5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) which is decided by rdosDFTBeamSelectionFor16RX (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27370\_replaced([11114136](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2RT shall re-order beams [CB015122-E] indices [End CB015122-E] according to the each beam's power from highest to lowest, where the power of  ith best beam  [image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10266.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] is equal to 10*log10([image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10266.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] ), the unit is dB. Note,  [image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10266.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is calculated when L2RT select the ith best beams in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20247\_replaced([11154965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20257\_replaced([11155127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksur5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) which is decided by rdosDFTBeamSelectionFor16RX (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27370\_replaced([11114136](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).***\*Step2:**
**If abs([image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10266.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]) < rdUlBeamsSigPowerDiff (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29491\_replaced([11158885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktF4QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),**
 - L2RT shall select the 1st best, 2nd best, 3rd best and 4th best beams after re-ordering in **Step1 as the first** four best beams.***\*
 - The 5th, 6th, 7th and 8th best beam shall be got by splitting the 5th best beam in* \*Step1 with 2x2 split mode (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29283\_replaced([11155383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**
 
**Else if abs([image-4][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10266.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]) < rdUlBeamsSigPowerDiff  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29491\_replaced([11158885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktF4QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),**
 - L2RT select the 1st, 2nd and 3rd best beams after re-ordering in **Step1 as the first three best beams.**
 - The 4th, 5th and 6th best beam shall be got by spliting the 4th best beam in **Step1 with hybrid split mode (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29283\_replaced([11155383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**
 - The 7th and 8th best beam shall be got by spliting the 5th best beam in Step1 with LR split mode (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29283\_replaced([11155383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
 
**Else**
 - L2RT select the 1st and 2nd best beams aftr re-ordering in **Step1 as the first two best beams.**
 - The 3rd, 4th, 5th and 6th best beam shall be got by spliting the 3rd best beam in **Step1 with 2x2 split mode (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29283\_replaced([11155383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**
 - The 7th and 8th best beam shall be got by spliting the 4th best beam in Step1 with LR split mode (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29283\_replaced([11155383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
**End**
 
**Note: Because of the limitation of maximum number of beams in L1-RRU, L2RT shall indicate L1-RRU the split mode and corresponding patternID of full panel beam if split beams are needed.**
[CB015122-E]
end
[End CB015122-E]

##### 3.18.1.5.0-5 osDFT Beam Selection for UL 8RX/16RX receiver Find best beams with UD split panel beams (ID: 11155374)

osDFT Beam Selection for UL 8RX/16RX receiver

The requirement has been moved to L1-DU, [13327328](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_84nh0NRPEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

else

This requirement is only applied when the following conditions are satisfied.

* NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming = 16RX AND rdSuUeReceiverSize (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27595\_replaced([11114156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = 16 AND rdUlSplitPanelModeFor16RX (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29390\_replaced([11114144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = "UD split mode".
* SU-MIMO UEs.

**Note, for MU-MIMO UEs, always full panel beams used in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20247\_replaced([11154965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20257\_replaced([11155127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksur5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) which is controlled by rdosDFTBeamSelectionFor16RX (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27370\_replaced([11114136](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

After all of **four beams are found in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20247\_replaced([11154965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20257\_replaced([11155127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksur5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) which is controlled by rdosDFTBeamSelectionFor16RX (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27370\_replaced([11114136](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),**

- The 1st and 2nd best beam which are used in L1-RRU to receive PUSCH data shall be got by spliting the 1st best beam in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20247\_replaced([11154965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with **UD split mode (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29283\_replaced([11155383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

- The 3rd and 4th best beam which are used in L1-RRU to receive PUSCH data shall be got by spliting the 2nd best beam in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20247\_replaced([11154965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with **UD split mode(5G\_UP\_ALG\_29283\_replaced([11155383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

- The 5th and 6th best beam which are used in L1-RRU to receive PUSCH data shall be got by spliting the 3rd best beam in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20247\_replaced([11154965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with **UD split mode(5G\_UP\_ALG\_29283\_replaced([11155383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

- The 7th and 8th best beam which are used in L1-RRU to receive PUSCH data shall be got by spliting the 4th best beam in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20247\_replaced([11154965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with **UD split mode(5G\_UP\_ALG\_29283\_replaced([11155383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

**Note: Because of the limitation of maximum number of beams in L1-RRU, L2RT shall indicate L1-RRU the split mode and corresponding patternID of full panel beam if split beams are needed.**

##### 3.18.1.5.0-6 osDFT Beam Selection for UL 8RX/16RX receiver Split panel mode (ID: 11155383)

**3.18.1.5.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13378054`)

osDFT Beam Selection for UL 8RX/16RX receiver
[CB015122-E]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The requirement has been moved to 5G System level spcification, [11354596](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucJSWfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

else

[End CB015122-E]

The beaming vector shall be constructed  according to the **Logic View of antenna and full panel beam.**

**Logic View : One vector for one polarization, each vector consists Ntrx/2 complex values, [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Ners" in a blurry, colorful font.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10270.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] is RU’s TRX number for the current cell with both polarizations counted. Observing the antenna array from the front (from UE), the complex values in the vector are mapped to RU’s TRX from bottom to top, left to right.**

Notice: Split panel beam weight vector shall be got according to different antenna geometry.

Split panel mode for 64TRX RU with 4 columns, 8 rows, 2 polarizations is as following. 32TRX with 2 columns, 8 rows, 2 polarizations has similar behavior.

[image-1][image\_desc]The image displays four figures, each illustrating a different "split mode" with a grid of red and blue "X" symbols. The figures are labeled from left to right as "Figure 1: 2x2 split mode", "Figure 2: hybrid split mode", "Figure 3: LR split mode", and "Figure 4: UD split mode".
Figure 1 shows a 4x4 grid of "X" symbols, divided into four 2x2 subgrids by dashed blue lines. The "X" symbols alternate in color (red and blue) and orientation (/) within each row and column.
Figure 2 presents a 4x4 grid of "X" symbols, also divided by dashed blue lines. However, the division is different from Figure 1. The top half of the grid is divided into two 2x2 subgrids, and the bottom half is also divided into two 2x2 subgrids. The "X" symbols follow a similar alternating color and orientation pattern.
Figure 3 displays a larger grid of "X" symbols, appearing to be 4x8. This grid is divided by dashed blue lines into three sections: a 4x4 section on the left, and two 4x2 sections on the right. The "X" symbols maintain the alternating color and orientation pattern.
Figure 4 shows a 4x4 grid of "X" symbols, divided by dashed blue lines into two horizontal sections. The top section is a 2x4 grid, and the bottom section is also a 2x4 grid. The "X" symbols continue the alternating color and orientation pattern.
The text below each figure describes the respective split mode.

[image-6][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a sans-serif font. The equation is:
$W\_2 = [O\_{1 \times 4}, W\_4, W\_5, W\_6, W\_7, O\_{1 \times 4}, W\_{12}, W\_{13}, W\_{14}, W\_{15}, O\_{1 \times 16}]^T$;
Here's a breakdown of the components:
- $W\_2$: This is the variable being defined.
- $=$: The equals sign.
- $[ ... ]^T$: This denotes a column vector, where the elements inside the brackets are arranged vertically.
- $O\_{1 \times 4}$: This represents a row vector of zeros with dimensions 1x4.
- $W\_4, W\_5, W\_6, W\_7, W\_{12}, W\_{13}, W\_{14}, W\_{15}$: These are likely other variables or matrices.
- $O\_{1 \times 16}$: This represents a row vector of zeros with dimensions 1x16.
- The commas separate the elements within the vector.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04141119.png[/image\_path][/image-6]

### 3.18.1.6 Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements

#### 3.18.1.6.0-1 Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements Overview: Third and Fourth Beam probing of 8RX IRC receiver (ID: 11155438)

**3.18.1.6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11155443`)

Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements
gNB shall do Third and Fourth beam probing of 8RC IRC receiver only when all the following conditions are met.

1. 8RX IRC receiver (NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming = 8)
2. when the beam probing functionality is activated using NRBTS.NRCELL.actProbingUlSrsBeams = 'Beams3rd4th'
3. *rrmUlBeamSelectTimer is atleast 20 slots to allow sufficient slots for beam probing. (cf. slides <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:p:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CNI/CNI-128587%203rd%20and%204th%20beam%20probing%20using%20L1%20measurements/CP2/CNI-128587%20rrmUlBeamSelectTime%20vs%20Probing%20decision.pptx?d=w261b03c3b0f140e99538dba1aa17cf08&csf=1&web=1&e=A9EqGq).>  The* rrmUlBeamSelectTimer is the timer duration (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2173\_replaced([11154691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in unit of slot, for UL beam selection.\*\*

IRC gains are dependent on beam selection for 8RX receiver. gNB-DU selects the beams for 8 RX receiver as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27573\_replaced([11154921](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Third and fourth x-pol beams may toggle frequently and weaker beams can be observed. On top of the beam selection (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27573\_replaced([11154921](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), probing of the candidate beams for third and fourth best beams with an additional measurement check based on L1 PUSCH measurements prevents the beam toggling and brings additional gain through better signal quality.

After gNB-DU receives the covariance matrices (CoMa) from L1, CoMa is processed as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2156\_replaced([11154436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to get long-term Cov(H) and Cov(V). Using the long-term CoMa, 4 best beams are selected and applied for the next RX processing. L2-PS shall store the indices of the third and fourth beam. With probing, when new SRS covariance matrices are received from L1, apart from selecting the 4 best beams for RX processing, L2-PS shall additionally compare the signal measurements of stored ‘old’ beams with the ‘new’ beams by the probing mechanism as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32462\_replaced([11155488](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksv6AfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32510\_replaced([11155507](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksv6A_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If degradation is expected after probing measurements, then old beams shall be kept otherwise new beams shall be used.

For the first UL oDFT beam selection after beam weights for oDFT beams are online changed, the beam probing defined in [11155432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) shall not be conducted.

If real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric value is greater than or equal to the value set for activation threshold of rd8RxSrsUlBmBeamProbingDeactOlcUlPerCent ([12627247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_WPCX4TrLEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), then gNB-DU shall pause the beam probing due to activation of the load control.

If probing procedure is interrupted due to any reason, the following cases apply.

 Case 1: Probing is finished but new beams are not applied (UE not scheduled until next SRS CoMa). Next probing shall be started with same behavior as if the UE had been scheduled, meaning old beams shall be the one decided from the previous probing.

 Case2: Probing is not finished, and decision is not made. Then Next probing shall be started using *OldBeamsX = NewBeamsX from previous CoMa.*

---

#### 3.18.1.6.0-2 Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements Preconditions of Probing (ID: 11155448)

**3.18.1.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11155457`)

Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements
11155457:
Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements
The indices of third and fourth best beams stored in L2-PS are referred to as *OldBeam3 and* OldBeam4 respectively*. The indices of third and fourth best beams computed from the latest SRS covariance matrix are referred to as* NewBeam3 and *NewBeam4.* *All the following pre-conditions shall be satisfied to initiate probing mechanism.***\***\*

1. The beam indices are not same, that is, *NewBeam3  is not equal to*OldBeam3 OR *NewBeam4 is not equal to*OldBeam4 and the beam indices are not simply swapped. A simple swap is defined as *NewBeam3 =* OldBeam4 AND *NewBeam4 =* OldBeam3.***\****\*

2. *NewBeam1 or*NewBeam2 do not collide with *OldBeam3 or*OldBeam4. i.e, Products [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression written in a serif font. The expression is:
((NewBeam1 - OldBeam3) x (NewBeam2 - OldBeam3)) OR ((NewBeam2 - OldBeam4) x (NewBeam1 - OldBeam4))[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10279.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] is not 0, where *NewBeam1 and* NewBeam2 are the first and second best beam computed from the latest SRS covariance matrix.**\***\*

3.  Combinations of the conditions 1 & 2 where collision in combination with the simple swap leads to no new beams for probing has not occurred. If both *OldBeam3 and* OldBeam4 are repeated in the set of new beams {*NewBeam1, NewBeam2, NewBeam3, NewBeam4}, probing shall not be started.*\*\*

1. If *rdAngularSeparationProbing3and4 (defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32444\_replaced([11158936](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktF4SvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is true, Horizontal DoA difference between* OldBeamX and *NewBeamX (X={3,4})* shall be checked. If the difference is less than *rdAngularSeparationThreshold (defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32453\_replaced([11158947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktF4TPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), probing shall be skipped for the* BeamX and L2-PS continues to schedule PUSCH using {*NewBeam1, NewBeam2, OldBeam3, OldBeam4}. If one of the* OldBeam3 or *OldBeam4 collides with* NewBeam1 or *NewBeam2, L2-PS shall continue to schedule PUSCH using {*NewBeam1, NewBeam2, OldBeamX, OldBeamY} where  *OldBeamX and* OldBeamY are selected from the set {*OldBeam1,* OldBeam2, *OldBeam3,* OldBeam4} which are not *NewBeam1 or*NewBeam2.***\*******\******\***\*

Note: Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32465\_replaced([11155522](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksv6BfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for flowchart of preconditions of probing.

---

#### 3.18.1.6.0-3 Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements Harmonic mean of the L1 measurements (ID: 11155465)

**3.18.1.6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11155479`)

Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements
11155479:
Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements
At the end of each probing slot, harmonic mean of the L1 reported pre-equalized SINR or RSSI (see Note 2) per polarization of each probed beam is calculated.

Note 1: Harmonic mean is computed only if the L1 measurements are valid (not -255) or no DTX.

Note 2: Selection of measurement quantity (Pre-equalized SINR or RSSI) from L1 for probing is based on R&D parameter: *rdSourceProbingBeam3and4 defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32442\_replaced([11158926](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktF4SPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If* rdSourceProbingBeam3and4 is 0, pre-equalized SINR shall be used. If *rdSourceProbingBeam3and4 is 1, RSSI shall be used. The term 'Pre-equalized SINR' is used as L1 measurement quantity for specification purpose of the beam probing functionality. Pre-equalized SINR shall be replaced by RSSI when* rdSourceProbingBeam3and4 is 1.\*\*\*\*

The equation to calculate the harmonic mean is same as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3084\_replaced([11131461](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The harmonic mean is calculated in linear domain and then converted to dB.

[image-0][image\_desc]averageSINRdB = 10log₁₀(2 / (1/SINR0 + 1/SINR1))[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10277.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Where [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "SINRO" in a stylized font. The letters are a dark color with a gradient of orange and blue hues, giving them a metallic or iridescent appearance. The background is a bright white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10277.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] and [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "SINR1" in a blurry, pixelated font. The letters are a dark color with a slight gradient, appearing to be a dark blue or black with hints of brown and yellow. The background is a bright white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10277.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] are pre-equalized SINRs (r*dSourceProbingBeam3and4 is 0) of x-pol beam reported in* PuschReceiveResponsePs message. Mapping of index of SINR in *PuschReceiveResponsePs to the beam index is shown in the table below.*\*\*

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **“Antenna”****index in PuschReceiveResp**\*\*\*\* |  | **Beam** |  | ***\*Polarities***\* |  |  |
| **0,1** |  | Best beam |  | +45,-45 |  |  |
|  | **2,3** |  | 2nd Best beam |  | +45,-45 |  |
|  | **4,5** |  | 3rd beam |  | +45,-45 |  |
|  | **6,7** |  | 4th beam |  | +45,-45 |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

#### 3.18.1.6.0-4 Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements Probing Procedure Step 1: Measurement of the changed 3rd and/or 4th UL beams (ID: 11155488)

**3.18.1.6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11155503`)

Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements
11155503:
Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements
When the preconditions of probing (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32458\_replaced([11155448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are satisfied, gNB-DU shall initiate probing. Two cases are possible.

**Case 1: One slot probing**

When only one beam index **among third or fourth beam is changed due to the latest SRS measurements, one uplink slot is used for probing using the set of beams {*NewBeam1, NewBeam2, *OldBeam3, NewBeam3} or {*NewBeam1, NewBeam2, \*OldBeam4, NewBeam4}***\*\*\*

Note :  If among *NewBeam 3,4 there is only one* OldBeam as below:\*\*

 *NewBeam3 ==* OldBeam4 then probe beam4 only. One slot probing shall be done using the set of beams {*NewBeam1, NewBeam2, OldBeam3, NewBeam4}*\*\*

 *NewBeam4 ==* OldBeam3 then probe beam3 only. One slot probing shall be done using the set of beams {*NewBeam1, NewBeam2, OldBeam4, NewBeam3}*\*\*

When two beams are changed (*NewBeam3, NewBeam4) and either* NewBeam1 or NewBeam2 collide with *OldBeam3 or OldBeam4, i.e., one of the products*\*\*

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression written in a serif font. The expression is:
((NewBeam1 - OldBeam3) x (NewBeam2 - OldBeam3)) OR ((NewBeam2 - OldBeam4) x (NewBeam1 - OldBeam4))[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10279.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

is 0, one slot probing shall be used for probing.

 If [image-1][image\_desc]((NewBeam1 - OldBeam3) x (NewBeam2 - OldBeam3))[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10279.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]is 0 then Probe *Beam4*

 If [image-2][image\_desc]((NewBeam2 - OldBeam4) x (NewBeam1 - OldBeam4))[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10279.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is 0 then Probe *Beam3*

**Case 2: Two slots probing**

When both beam indices, i.e, third and fourth beams are changed due to latest SRS measurements, two consecutive uplink slots are used for probing.

 In the first UL slot, the set of beams {*NewBeam1, NewBeam2, OldBeam3, NewBeam3} is used.*

 In the second UL slot, the set of beams {*NewBeam1, NewBeam2, OldBeam4, NewBeam4} is used.*

After end of each probing slot, using the reported measurements (pre-equalized SINR measurement per RX antenna stream (see [12687121](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_RsXQcFUCEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) in L1 EFS)), L2-PS shall compute according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32460\_replaced ([11155465](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and store the harmonic mean of pre-equalized SINR of each beam.

Note: Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32465\_replaced([11155522](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksv6BfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for flowchart for the Decision of number of slots for Probing (NumberSlotsProbingDecision).

---

#### 3.18.1.6.0-5 Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements Probing Procedure Step 2: Probing decision (ID: 11155507)

**3.18.1.6.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11155517`)

Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements
11155517:
Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements
Until the probing decision is completed, L2-PS continues to schedule PUSCH using {*NewBeam1, NewBeam2, OldBeam3, OldBeam4}. If one of the* OldBeam3 or *OldBeam4 collides with* NewBeam1 or *NewBeam2, L2-PS shall continue to schedule PUSCH using {*NewBeam1, NewBeam2, OldBeamX, OldBeamY} where  *OldBeamX and* OldBeamY are selected from the set {*OldBeam1,* OldBeam2, *OldBeam3,* OldBeam4} which are not *NewBeam1 or*NewBeam2.***\*******\****

The harmonic mean comparison function is represented as

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a serif font. The formula is:
`comp(X) = (HarmonicMean(NewBeamX) > (HarmonicMean(OldBeamX) + rdSinrDiff NewBeam3And4))`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10281.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where

- *HarmonicMean(BeamX) is the Harmonic mean computation function defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32460\_replaced([11155465](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*

- *rdSinrDiffNewBeam3And4 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32437\_replaced([11158915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktF4RvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*

If probing is done in **only one slot, probing decision and final beam selection shall be done as below.**

If (*comp(X)==true)*

then

selectedBeamX = *NewBeamX*

else

selectedBeamX = *OldBeamX*

where X = 3 or 4.

Note: Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32725\_replaced([11155531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksv6B_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for flowchart of one slot probing.

If probing is done in **two slots, beam selection is done by the following logic at the end of the second slot.  NewBeamX and OldBeamX are compared and the result of the comparison determines the selection of beams.**

If ( *comp(3)==true and* comp(4)==true )  OR (*OldBeam3 measures Invalid and* OldBeam4 measures Invalid)\*\*\*\*

Beam3= *NewBeam3 and Beam4=*NewBeam4\*\*

Else if ( *comp(3)==true AND {*comp(4)==false OR (*NewBeam4 measures Invalid) OR DTX(2ndULslotProbing)} AND (*NewBeam3 - *OldBeam4) is not zero*\*\*\*\*

Beam3=*NewBeam3 and Beam4=*OldBeam4\*\*

Else if ( *comp(4)==true AND (*comp(3)==false OR (*NewBeam3 measures Invalid) OR DTX(1stULslotProbing))  AND (*NewBeam4 - *OldBeam3) is not zero*\*\*\*\*

Beam3=*OldBeam3 and Beam4=*NewBeam4\*\*

Else

Beam3=*OldBeam3 and Beam4=*OldBeam4\*\*

Note: Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32727\_replaced([11155543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksv6CfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for flowchart of two slots probing.

#### 3.18.1.6.0-8 Beam probing for 8 RX IRC using L1 measurements Flowchart: Two Slots Probing (ID: 11155543)

## 3.18.2 Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO

### 3.18.2.0-1 Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO Periodic SRS for UL SU-MIMO (ID: 11155560)

**3.18.2.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12877316`)

Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO
**[CB009527-A]**

**NOTE: to make requirement to be more generic, this requirement is revised by replacing names of WB SRS and SB SRS to SB BF and WB BF. PLEASE remove this NOTE when a new version is created.**

**[End CB009527-A]**

For TDD frame structure and some RRC connected users, 5G-L2-PS may receive from 5G-CP their periodic SRS resource configuration during the user setup or user modification procedures.

The 5G-L2-PS shall use codebook usage periodic SRS to estimate UL beams (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2135\_replaced([11154028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqacvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in beamforming cell**and measure PMI/RI/SINR for SU-MIMO (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3236\_replaced([11155554](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksv6C_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for these users which are configured with codebook usage periodic SRS in active BWP.**

If NIDD:actUlSrsBm is true and NIDD:actDlSrsBm is true:

{

* When periodic SRS resource is shared between DL and UL BM as defined by 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_11074\_replaced([11305745](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqzQZvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

The 5G-L2-PS shall use the shared periodic SRS to for UL beams, UL SU-MIMO and DL beams (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6962\_replaced([11155660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in active BWP.

~~- If NIDD:actDlSrsSubbandBm is true:~~

* When periodic SRS resource for SB BF is shared between DL and UL BM as defined by 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_11074\_replaced([11305745](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqzQZvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS shall request only a part of this SRS for UL SU-MIMO to L1 and this part shall have the same size as the subband for CoMa defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20838\_replaced([11156649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2nsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* When periodic codebook SRS resource is released, 5G-L2-PS shall delete all this SRS resource related handling in UL SU-MIMO defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3236\_replaced([11155554](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksv6C_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

}

Please note: it's possible that some users are configured with aperiodic SRS and others are configured with periodic SRS by L3. The SRS allocation algorithm is specified by L3.

---

### 3.18.2.0-2 Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO Overall state machine (ID: 11155590)

**3.18.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11155599`)

Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO
11155599:
Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO
Two state machines are introduced for codebook usage periodic SRS: one is the state machine for SU-MIMO, another is the state machine for BM ( (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2137\_replaced([11154039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqadPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This requirement defines the state machine for SU-MIMO.
 
The overall state machine for SU-MIMO is defined in the below diagram. The state machine shall be maintained for users which are configured with periodic 2 ports SRS.
 
When the SRS port number is changed from 2 to 1, the state machine for SU-MIMO will not be used anymore for the UE. when the SRS port number is changed from 1 to 2, the state machine shall be created for the UE.
 
- The rrmSuMimoAgedTimer is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3244\_replaced([11155635](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
- State of SU\_MIMO\_AGED is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3238\_replaced([11155604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
- State of SU\_MIMO\_VALID is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3240\_replaced([11155613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
 
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a state diagram illustrating the states and transitions related to SU MIMO (Single User Multiple-Input Multiple-Output) reporting.
There are two states depicted:
1. **SU\_MIMO\_AGED**: This state is represented by a double circle, indicating it is a terminal or final state.
2. **SU\_MIMO\_VALID**: This state is represented by a single circle.
There are two transitions shown:
\* **Transition 1**: From SU\_MIMO\_AGED to SU\_MIMO\_VALID. The label for this transition is "SU MIMO report from SRS 2 port, UL SINR for PUSCH rank1 or singleTx".
\* **Transition 2**: From SU\_MIMO\_VALID back to SU\_MIMO\_VALID. This is a self-loop transition. The label for this transition is "SU MIMO report from PUSCH rank2 or SRS 2 port, UL SINR for PUSCH single Tx (SRS 1 port)".
\* **Transition 3**: From SU\_MIMO\_VALID to SU\_MIMO\_AGED. The label for this transition is "rrmSuMimoAgedTimer expires".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10295.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
File: SRS\_states.vsd
Folder:

---

### 3.18.2.0-3 Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO State of SU_MIMO_AGED (ID: 11155604)

**3.18.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11155608`)

Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO
It’s the initial state of the state machine.

When enters this state:

 reset memory of N (=rdNumSrsFreqHops, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9938\_replaced([11141147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) last measurements ST rank from periodic SRS

 The rrmUlRiLongTerm shall be set to 1.

 The default PMI precoder of rank 1 shall be used for PUSCH. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3231\_replaced([11139991](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq7_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 Stop the rrmSuMimoAgedTimer.

Under this state:

 When receive any new measurement as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3242\_replaced([11155624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and switch to the SU\_MIMO\_VALID state.

---

### 3.18.2.0-4 Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO State of SU_MIMO_VALID (ID: 11155613)

**3.18.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12638015`)

Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO
When enters this state:

 Start the **rrmSuMimoAgedTimer.**

Rank selection (based on long term average and comparison to thresholds) is handled according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3226\_replaced([11139957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq79_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*.*

When scheduled PUSCH is with rank 2:

When receive a valid SU-MIMO report from **PUSCH (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3081\_replaced([11131259](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCCw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

a. [Before PR841823]

**[Before PR830194] restart the** rrmSuMimoAgedTimer [PR830194] stop the **rrmSuMimoAgedTimer if started**[End PR830194].***\****\*

[PR841823]

Stop the **rrmSuMimoAgedTimer when NIDD:actCoverageNonCoherentUE = True and UlFullPowerTransmissionR16 (in puschConfig) is ‘notConfigured', otherwise restart the** rrmSuMimoAgedTimer**.**\*\*\*\*

[End PR841823]

b. reset **memory of N (=rdNumSrsFreqHops, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9938\_replaced([11141147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) last measurements ST rank from subband SRS.**

c. To update long-term rank according to algorithm defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19663\_replaced([11139919](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krq78PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Each short term rank from PUSCH is used as one rrmUlRiShortTerm (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3223\_replaced([11139902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

d. To update averaged SINR according to algorithm defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3081\_replaced([11131259](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCCw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

e.  To update PMIs according to PUSCH report.

When scheduled PUSCH is with rank 1 (i.e. 2SRS ports):

When receive a valid SU-MIMO report from **SRS (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3081\_replaced([11131259](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCCw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), restart the** rrmSuMimoAgedTimer and:\*\*\*\*

a. To update long-term rank according to below:

 at L2 Memory of N (=rdNumSrsFreqHops, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9938\_replaced([11141147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) last measurements ST rank from subband SRS

rrmUlRiShortTerm =Min over N(=rdNumSrsFreqHops) last measurements as input to rrmUlRiLongTerm computation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3223\_replaced([11139902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Until the number of measurements N is reached, minimum value is not computed and rrmUlRiShortTerm=1.

b. To update averaged SINR according to algorithm defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3081\_replaced([11131259](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCCw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

c.  To update PMIs according to SRS report.

When scheduled PUSCH is with single Tx (i.e. 1 SRS port):

When receive a valid UL SINR measurement from PUSCH (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3081\_replaced([11131259](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCCw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), restart the **rrmSuMimoAgedTimer and:**

a. To update long-term rank according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3232\_replaced([11140029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krrjAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 If **rrmSuMimoAgedTimer expires, switch to the** SU\_MIMO\_AGED state.\*\*\*\*

---

### 3.18.2.0-5 Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO Set averaged Rank/SINR for PUSCH (ID: 11155624)

**3.18.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11155630`)

Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO
When the SU-MIMO state machine is under SU\_MIMO\_AGED, once receive any valid SU-MIMO report from SRS or valid UL SINR from PUSCH rank1 or single Tx (1SRS port) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3081\_replaced([11131259](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCCw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the averaged rank/SINR for PUSCH shall be updated according to algorithm defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3232\_replaced([11140029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krrjAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for aperiodic SRS.

If SRS is received with valid report, rank is used as first measurement to restart memory of N (=rdNumSrsFreqHops, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9938\_replaced([11141147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) last ST rank measurements  from periodic SRS

---

### 3.18.2.0-6 Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO Age of SU-MIMO measurement (via PUSCH and SRS) (ID: 11155635)

**3.18.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11155639`)

Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO
5G-L2-PS shall maintain the timer of rrmSuMimoAgedTimer for each user that is configured with periodic SRS. The duration of rrmSuMimoAgedTimer shall be implemented as a R&D parameter (rdSuMimoAgedTimer: default value is 1500 ms ; 5G\_L2\_1443\_replaced([11186437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_275VnvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

### 3.18.2.0-7 Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO Select candidates to measure SU-MIMO based on periodic SRS (ID: 11155645)

**3.18.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11155655`)

Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO
11155655:
Periodic codebook SRS for UL SU-MIMO
In each SRS measurement cycle, 5G-L2-PS shall trigger SRS reception for UEs which meet conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2151\_replaced([11154219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrolPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall select UE candidates for measuring SU-MIMO, from the set of UEs which have SRS reception in the current SRS measurement cycle, according to the algorithm defined in this requirement. UEs which only support 1-port SRS shall not be selected as candidate for SU-MIMO measurement.

1. For each UE in current SRS measurement cycle, 5G-L2-PS shall calculate weight of them according to the below equation:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in black text on a white background. The equation is:
`weight = lastReport * Π factor(i)`
The product symbol (Π) has `max_index` above it and `i=0` below it.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10305.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

- lastReport: current time minus the received time of last SU-MIMO report in unit of slot. If no SU-MIMO is reported before, the slot number of received time of last SU-MIMO report is the slot that UE enters network.

- max\_index: the maximum index number listed in the below table.

- factor(i): factor value listed in the below table for each index. NOTE: these factors shall be implmented as R&D parameter to ensure tuning in field.

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Index |  |  | Factor(i) | Notes |
| 0 | Under SRS\_BM\_CHGED state | Yes | 2 | UE with changed UL beam has higher priority |
| No | 1 |  |  |  |
| 1 | Under SU\_MIMO\_AGED state | Yes | 1 | UE with aged SU-MIMO measurement has lower priority because UE has no data and can exit the state on PUSCH reception (valid UL SINR). |
| No | 2 | UE in active state with rank1 (2SRS ports) has higher priority because UE has data and needs N SRS SU MIMO reports to update the rank. |  |  |
| 2 | In active state, UE is rank1 with 2 SRS port : Has the UE received N SU MIMO report ? | Yes | 1 | In active state UE with rank1 and without N SRS SU MIMO reports has higher priority |
| No | 2 |  |  |  |

Note: Two ports w/ rank 2 shall not be scheduled with periodic SRS for SU MIMO. One SRS port UE shall not be scheduled with periodic SRS for SU MIMO.

2. Select UEs as candidates which have higher weight values from the set. The maximum number of candidates can be selected per TTI depends L1 capacity and frame structure. The detailed algorithm shall be specified in CP3 .

4. Send SU-MIMO related information L1-UL for each candidate by providing below information:

a. RNTI

b. SRS sub-band information

c. Pattern IDs of PUSCH beams

d. UE’s coherent capacity

---

## 3.18.3 Periodic TAS SRS for DL WB BF

### 3.18.3.1 State Machine for Dl BM

#### 3.18.3.1.0-1 State Machine for Dl BM Overview of state machine for Dl BM (ID: 11155671)

**3.18.3.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11155678`)

State Machine for Dl BM
11155678:
State Machine for Dl BM
The Dl BM state machine is similar to Ul BM state machine in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2137\_replaced([11154039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqadPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
A UE may have two state machines based on periodic SRS resource set with codebook usage: one is the state machine for SU-MIMO (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3236\_replaced([11155554](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksv6C_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), another is the state machine for Ul BM(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2137\_replaced([11154039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqadPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
Additionally, state machine for Dl BM based on periodic SRS resource set with antenna switching usage shall be maintained. This requirement defines the state machine for Dl BM.
If the UE has periodic SRS antenna switching usage resource set configured, then Dl BM state machine shall be maintained.
 
[CB006137-BB] For CA UE with UL configured according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) over SCell and the UE has periodic SRS antenna switching usage resource set configured over SCell, The Dl BM state machine shall be maintained. [End CB006137-BB]
 
The overall state machine for Dl BM is defined in the below diagram.
- The rrmCoMaAgedTimer is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6971\_replaced([11155728](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxIK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
- State of SRS\_DL\_BM\_AGED is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6965\_replaced([11155684](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxII_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
- State of SRS\_DL\_BM\_VALID is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6967\_replaced([11155701](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxIJvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
 
 
[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a state machine diagram with two states: "SRS\_BM\_AGED" and "SRS\_BM\_VALID". The "SRS\_BM\_AGED" state is represented by a double circle, indicating it is the initial state. An arrow originates from "SRS\_BM\_AGED" and points to "SRS\_BM\_VALID", labeled with "SRS\_BM\_VALID\_TRANSITION". The "SRS\_BM\_VALID" state is represented by a single circle.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10309.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
