#### 3.18.3.1.0-2 State Machine for Dl BM State of SRS_DL_BM_AGED (ID: 11155684)

**3.18.3.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13373823`)

State Machine for Dl BM
It's the initial state of the state machine. For CA UE with UL configured according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) over SCell, It's the initial state of the state machine.

When enters this state:

· Stop the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer.**

[CB015122-B]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

· Stop the **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer ([13378891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0hm4w_2-EfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).**

else

[End CB015122-B]

· Stop the **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7000\_replaced([11156122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

· Clear the **rrmDlAvgCoMa (set to 0) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6993\_replaced([11156001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9UfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

· If **rrmExtendOdftTimer (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6974\_replaced([11155756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvM_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not running or expired**

· If NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode is "CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" or "OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" (values 1,3), the beam(s) for PDCCH/PDSCH/UE specific CSI-RS for channel acquisition shall be SSB/Refined beams defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2025\_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

· If dlMimoMode is "CL 8x4": for UEs under 4 ports mode, the beam(s) for PDCCH/PDSCH/UE specific CSI-RS shall be SSB/Refined beams defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2025\_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); for UEs under 8 ports mode, the beam(s) for PDCCH/PDSCH shall be PMI /SSB/Refined beams defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2028\_replaced([11112211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

· else oDFT beam is still seen as valid until **rrmExtendOdftTimer expired**

[CB015122-B]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

Under this state:

· When receiving valid CoMa indication from L1-DU, see [13332435](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9S7quNXNEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), switch to **SRS\_DL\_BM\_VALID.**

else

[End CB015122-B]

Under this state:

· When receive a valid CoMa (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6991\_replaced([11155895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2164\_replaced([11154500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), update **rrmDlAvgCoMa.**

· After receiving notification from L1-DU, see [13336532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_smL_F9mHEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), that instantaneous coma over 2 polarities and total ports in same period are valid, 5G-L2-PS shall switch to SRS\_DL\_BM\_VALID state. High important note: one CoMa here refers to combined covariance matrix (Cov(H) and Cov(V)) which are combined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6989\_replaced([11155973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

#### 3.18.3.1.0-3 State Machine for Dl BM State of SRS_DL_BM_VALID (ID: 11155701)

**3.18.3.1.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `13374055`)

State Machine for Dl BM
When state is entered:

· Execute **the beams selection algorithms defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2168\_replaced([11154601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

[CB015122-B]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

· Start the **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer as defined in [13378891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0hm4w_2-EfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).**

else

[End CB015122-B]

· Start the **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer.**

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

· Start the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer.**

· Stop **rrmExtendOdftTimer (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6974\_replaced([11155756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvM_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if it is running.**

[CB015122-B]

Under this state:

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

· When the **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer expires or gNB-DU skips evaluation of SRS occurrence for load purposes (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29538\_replaced([11158109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_xqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

1) if averaged CoMa updated condition (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29619\_replaced([11155739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvMPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is met**, L1-DU executes beam selection algorithm as in [13327330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_LzBroNRQEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and sends beam related information to L2-PS.**

2) Restart the **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer as defined in [13378891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0hm4w_2-EfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).**

· When the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer expires, indicate to L1-DU expiry, see event (4) in [13415096](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Mu6pYBNMEfG3gf_qmG8Vww?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_mu6pybnmefg3gf_qmg8vww?oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9"), switch to** SRS\_DL\_BM\_AGED state and trigger WB SRS to be released if it is evaluated as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21380\_replaced([11157558](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8HSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*

· At the reception of a valid CoMa indication by L1-DU, in [13331610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3PiwQdWeEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), restart the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer and execute the beam selection algorithm defined in [13327330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_LzBroNRQEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).**

· For CA UE with UL configured according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) over SCell, switch to **SRS\_DL\_BM\_AGED state after SCell is deactivated successfully. pSRS is configured on the UL Carrier of the SCell and is used for DL beam management of this carrier independently of the PCell configuration. Note: when subband BF is supported for SCell later, the release of WB SRS should be considered.**

· On reception of oDFT beam set due to online change, execute the beam selection algorithm defined in [13327330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_LzBroNRQEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), and restart **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer.** Note: considering the beam selection is to be performed for all UEs with DFT beam support, it is left to CP3 to define **how to distribute the best beam determination for these UEs over multiple slots.**

else

[End CB015122-B]

· When the **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer expires or gNB-DU skips evaluation  SRS occurrence for load purposes (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29538\_replaced([11158109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_xqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

1) if averaged CoMa updated condition (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29619\_replaced([11155739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvMPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is met**, execute the beams selection algorithms defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6995\_replaced([11156011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9U_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

2) Restart the **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer.**

· When the **rrmCoMaAgedTimer expires, switch to** SRS\_DL\_BM\_AGED state and trigger WB SRS to be released if it is configured as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21380\_replaced([11157558](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8HSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*

· On reception of a valid instantaneous CoMa (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6991\_replaced([11155895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2164\_replaced([11154500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), update **rrmDlAvgCoMa and restart the** rrmCoMaAgedTimer.\*\*\*\*

· For CA UE with UL configured according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) over SCell, switch to **SRS\_DL\_BM\_AGED state after SCell is deactivated successfully. pSRS is configured on the UL Carrier of the SCell and is used for DL beam management of this carrier independently of the PCell configuration. Note: when subband BF is supported for SCell later, the release of WB SRS should be considered.**

· On reception of oDFT beam set due to online change, execute the beam selection algorithm defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6995\_replaced([11156011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9U_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and restart **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer.** Note: considering the beam selection is to be performed for all UEs with DFT beam support, it is left to CP3 to define **how to distribute the best beam determination for these UEs over multiple slots. A general requirement is, L2-PS should perform the beam selection to get the update for the beams for each UE as soon as possible.**

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

---

#### 3.18.3.1.0-4 State Machine for Dl BM Age of covariance matrix (ID: 11155728)

**3.18.3.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11155735`)

State Machine for Dl BM
5G-L2-PS shall maintain a timer of rrmCoMaAgedTimer for each UE which has DL BM state machine maintained. The length of the timer is defined in the same way as that of codebook usage periodic SRS in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2144\_replaced([11154145](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) except independent rdDlCoMaAgedCycle (5G\_UP\_ALG\_11386\_replaced([11114017](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpgYzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is used for Dl.

---

#### 3.18.3.1.0-5 State Machine for Dl BM Averaged CoMa updated condition (ID: 11155739)

**3.18.3.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11155745`)

State Machine for Dl BM
The condition is defined the same way as UL in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29616\_replaced([11154157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBiPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) but the value is independent for DL.

### 3.18.3.2 SRS Reception

#### 3.18.3.2.0-1 SRS Reception Periodic SRS configuration (ID: 11155756)

**3.18.3.2.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11155781`)

SRS Reception
**[CB009527-A]**

**NOTE: to make requirement to be more generic, this requirement is revised by replacing names of WB SRS and SB SRS to SB BF and WB BF. PLEASE remove this NOTE when a new version is created.**

**[End CB009527-A]**

If the NIDD:actDlSrsBm is true

* 5G-L2-PS may receive antenna switching usage periodic SRS (TAS SRS) resource set configuration for a user from L3 during the user setup or user modification procedures. The related parameters are the same with codebook usage periodic SRS(5G\_UP\_ALG\_2147\_replaced([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and shall be stored in user context. Additionally, usage shall be saved.
* 5G-L2-PS shall distinguish the SRS resource that is shared between TAS SRS resource set and codebook SRS resource set. Whether the shared resource is used or not in Dl BM refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6989\_replaced([11155973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If NIDD actUlSrsBm is true,

* *If* srsTypeAllocForDlBm is 'codebook', 5G-L2-PS shall only use codebook SRS resource set in DL BM. If codebook SRS resource set is not available, then 5G-L2-PS shall handle as SRS is not available for UE.\*\*
* If *srsTypeAllocForDlBm is 'antenna switching', 5G-L2-PS shall only use antenna switching SRS resource set in DL BM. If antenna switching SRS resource set is not available, then 5G-L2-PS shall handle as SRS is not available for UE. In addition for UL CA UE(refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with FR1 TDD as SCell, 5G-L2-PS shall use codebook SRS resource set in DL BM if codebook SRS resource set is available for critical band combination(refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9795\_replaced([11307653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tq-PjfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), otherwise 5G-L2-PS shall handle as SRS is not available for UE.*
* If *srsTypeAllocForDlBm is 'antenna switching or codebook', 5G-L2-PS shall firstly check if antenna switching SRS resource set is available or not. If antenna switching SRS resource set is available, then 5G-L2-PS shall use antenna switching SRS resource set in DL BM. Otherwise 5G-L2-PS shall check if codebook SRS resource set is available or not. If codebook SRS resource set is available, then 5G-L2-PS shall use codebook SRS resource set in DL BM. Otherwise 5G-L2-PS shall handle as SRS is not available for UE.*

Else

5G-L2-PS shall only use antenna switching SRS resource set in DL BM. If antenna switching SRS resource set is not available, then 5G-L2-PS shall handle as SRS is not available for UE. In addition for UL CA UE(refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with FR1 TDD as SCell, 5G-L2-PS shall use codebook SRS resource set in DL BM if codebook SRS resource set is available for critical band combination(refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9795\_replaced([11307653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tq-PjfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), otherwise 5G-L2-PS shall handle as SRS is not available for UE.

~~If NIDD:actDlSrsSubbandBm is true:~~

* When periodic TAS SRS resource that is used for subband BF is received, 5G-L2-PS shall request only a part of this SRS for CoMa to L1 as defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20838\_replaced([11156649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2nsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* When periodic TAS or codebook SRS resource configuration is changed, 5G-L2-PS shall delete all previous SRS resource related handling in DL BM defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6962\_replaced([11155660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), except oDFT beam will be invalid according to its own **rrmExtendOdftBeamTimer which has the same length as remaining** rrmCoMaAgedTimer for DL 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6971\_replaced([11155728](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxIK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*
* When periodic TAS or codebook SRS resource is released, 5G-L2-PS shall delete all this SRS resource related handling in DL BM defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6962\_replaced([11155660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) including oDFT beams.

Note1: From NIDD parameter relations, NRCELL/actDlSrsSubbandBm depends on NRCELL/actDlSrsBm, but not NRCELL/actUlSrsBm.

Note2: When NRCELL/actDlSrsSubbandBm is true, *srsTypeAllocForDlBm is not used when L3 configurates TAS SRS for subband BF.*

---

#### 3.18.3.2.0-2 SRS Reception Cyclic shift of SRS ports (ID: 11155794)

**3.18.3.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11155797`)

SRS Reception
The cyclic shift values of each SRS port shall be calculated according to equations defined in 3GPP 38.211 6.4.1.4.2.

Maximum 4 ports shall be supported.

---

#### 3.18.3.2.0-3 SRS Reception SRS measurement cycle (periodic SRS) (ID: 11155803)

**3.18.3.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11155813`)

SRS Reception
5G-L2-PS shall trigger antenna switching SRS reception for UEs the same as 5G\_ALG\_2151, except that no UL SU-MIMO related measurement is needed for antenna switching SRS or due to remote interference mitigation scheme (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9172\_replaced([11163373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB006991-C] or due to RIM RS detection  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13520\_replaced([11162042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-APvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [end CB006991-C] .

Additionally, if the UE has SRS resource shared between resource sets with antenna switching and codebook usage, the shared SRS resource reception only need to be triggered one time.

SRS Reception
11155836:
SRS Reception
The starting PRB of SRS shall be calculated according to equations defined in the chapter of 6.4.1.4.3 in 3GPP TS 38.211.

#### 3.18.3.2.0-5 SRS Reception SRS Reception Over SCell for UL Carrier Aggregation or SRS carrier switching (ID: 11155841)

**3.18.3.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11155846`)

SRS Reception
If the NIDD actDlSrsBm of SCell with UL configured according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is true for FR1 UL CA UE, 5G-L2-PS may receive periodic SRS resource configuration according to 5G\_UL\_ALG\_6974.

Per TS38.321, UE will transmit SRS over SCell according to timing defined in TS38.213 after SCell activation/Deactivation MAC-CE received.

 After guard period of SCell activation according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2792\_replaced([11121815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS will start the reception of SRS according to periodic SRS configuration;

 After SCell deactivation(SCell deactivation MAC-CE is ACKed), 5G-L2-PS will stop the reception of SRS;

### 3.18.3.3 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)

#### 3.18.3.3.0-1 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Process covariance matrices (ID: 11155856)

**3.18.3.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13377783`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-B]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The requirement has been moved to L1-DU,  L2-PS does not receive CoMa as input for beam selection.

else

[End CB015122-B]

After 5G-L2-PS has received instantaneous CoMas from L1, it shall process them according to below steps. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6963\_replaced([11155665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxIIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) about the state machine for DL BM.

Note: the calculation and maintenance of the LT covariance matrices shall be implemented in a separate thread or process to decouple it from the normal scheduler process

1. Find instantaneous CoMas of related UE(s) from L1.

a.  The number of instantaneous CoMas per UE is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6987\_replaced([11155881](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

b.  The size of instantaneous and LT CoMas is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6985\_replaced([11155868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2. Calculate Cov(H) and Cov(V) per UE (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6989\_replaced([11155973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

3. Validate instantaneous CoMas Cov(H) and Cov(V) per UE (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6991\_replaced([11155895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2164\_replaced([11154500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2165\_replaced([11154516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

4. If instantaneous CoMas Cov(H) and Cov(V) are valid:

a.  Apply the IIR filter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6993\_replaced([11156001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9UfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

b.  Store updated LT CoMas, Cov(H) and Cov(V), in UE’s context.

5. If at least one of the instantaneous CoMas Cov(H) or Cov(V) is invalid:

a.  Discard Cov(H) and Cov(V) of UE which are reported by L1.

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

---

#### 3.18.3.3.0-2 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Size of covariance matrix (ID: 11155868)

**3.18.3.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13377896`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-B]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The requirement has been moved to L1-DU,  [13332433](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_z34FhNXNEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

else

[End CB015122-B]

The size of horizontal and vertical covariance matrix based on SRS usage antenna switching is decided in the same way as covariance matrix from codebook SRS, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2158\_replaced([11154448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

---

#### 3.18.3.3.0-3 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Covariance matrix per UE (ID: 11155881)

**3.18.3.3.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13377898`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-B]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The requirement has been moved to L1-DU, see [13332434](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_4zK60NXNEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-B]

If periodic sub-band SRS for multiple UEs are scheduled in SRS slot, for eCPRI 7-2a, 5G-L1-UL will report multiple instantaneous CoMas per sub-band per comb per cyclic shift per polarization per projection to H and V to 5G-L2-PS;  for eCPRI 7-2e, 5G-L1-radio will report multiple covariance matrices per sub-band per comb offset per cyclic shift per direction to 5G-L2-PS. The size of horizontal and vertical covariance matrices is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6985\_replaced([11155868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Based on UE’s capability, if UE is configured with overall P ports' SRS, for eCPRI 7-2a, 5G-L1-UL will report 4*P covariance matrices to upper layer. With 2 directions horizontal and vertical, 2 polarizations per port. For eCPRI 7-2e, 5G-L1-UL will report 2*P covariance matrices to upper layer. With 2 directions horizontal and vertical per port.

Note that these P ports may be configured to different resources and different resources may be located at different slots.

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

---

#### 3.18.3.3.0-4 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Covariance matrix DTX detection (ID: 11155895)

**3.18.3.3.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `13377903`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
13377903:
SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-B]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The requirement has been moved to L1-DU, see [13332435](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9S7quNXNEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-B]

For each direction (H and V), 5G-L2-PS shall validate covariance matrix from L1 per port: Cov\_pi(H) and Cov\_pi(V) before averaging and average them per UE.

For eCPRI 7-2a:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
Cov\_pi(H) = Σ [Cov(H, polar\_x) / NumPolar]
where the summation is over polar\_x.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10349.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
Cov\_pi(V) = Σ\_{polar\_x} (Cov(V, polar\_x) / NumPolar)
The equation defines Cov\_pi(V) as the sum over polar\_x of the covariance between V and polar\_x, divided by NumPolar.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10349.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Where [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "Cov(H, polarx)". The text is in a light color against a slightly darker, blurred background. The expression is written in italics.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10349.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is the received covariance matrixes for the SRS resource set, with [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the word "polar" with a subscript "x". The text is blurry and appears to be in a light color against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10349.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] indicates polarization x.

[image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "NumPolar" in a stylized font. The letters are black with a slight chromatic aberration, giving them a subtle rainbow effect around the edges. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10349.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] is the number of polarities of received covariance matrixes.

For eCPRI 7-2e, L2-PS does not perform the average over polarization since it is already done in L1-radio.

The validation method is the same as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2165\_replaced([11154516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note: per port average or all port average may not change the DTX threshold.

If **all the ports of the SRS resource set are DTX, then consider covariance matrices for this UE is DTX this time.**

Note: For eCPRI 7-2a, to save CPU resources, SW will firstly average covariance matrices over ports then perform validation.

For covariance matrix validation for SB CoMa correlation metric (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22742\_replaced([11157172](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks6SFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall validate the covariance matrix per port (Cov\_pi(H) and Cov\_pi(V), averaged over polarizations). The validation method is same as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2165\_replaced([11154516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). However, the validation is done for covariance matrix per port separately, not averaged over ports (per SRS resource as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2162\_replaced([11154482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

---

#### 3.18.3.3.0-5 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Combine covariance matrices per UE (ID: 11155973)

**3.18.3.3.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `13377905`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
13377905:
SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-B]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The logic of the requirement has been moved to L1-DU, see [13332437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_DVMIENXOEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-B]

Cov(H,pi) and Cov(V,pi) shall be combined into one covariance matrix by calculating average values of each element among them.

Averaging is performed per SRS resource set.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
Cov(H) = Σ [Cov(H, pi) / NumP]
where the summation is over pi.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10351.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$Cov(V) = \sum\_{pi} \frac{Cov(V, pi)}{NumP}$
The equation shows that the covariance of V is equal to the sum over pi of the covariance of V and pi, divided by NumP.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10351.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Where Cov(H,pi) and Cov(V,pi) are the averaged covariance matrices per port for the SRS resource set, with [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the letters "pi" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are a gradient of colors, with shades of orange, yellow, blue, and purple. The background is white, and the image is framed by a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10351.004.png[/image\_path][/image-2] indicate port index i.

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "NumP" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are a light blue and yellow gradient, with a slight blur effect. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10351.005.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is the [Before CB015122-B] number ports for received [CB015122-B] total number of SRS ports with valid [End CB015122-B] covariance matrices.

Additionally, if the UE has SRS resource shared between resource sets with antenna switching and codebook usage, the SRS covariance matrix calculated from the shared SRS resource shall be adopted in both UL BM and DL BM.

Note that a UE may be configured with multiple SRS resources which are mapped to different slots. In that case, the port averaging shall comprise all ports of the same SRS usage within an SRS period.

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

---

#### 3.18.3.3.0-6 SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) Filter CoMa per UE in time domain (ID: 11156001)

**3.18.3.3.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13377907`)

SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa)
[CB015122-B]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The logic of the requirement has been moved to L1-DU, see [13332439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_J59cotXOEfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-B]

The instantaneous port averaged Cov(H) and Cov(V) shall be [CB015122-B] separately [End CB015122-B] filtered in time domain if they are valid (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6991\_replaced([11155895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2164\_replaced([11154500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The IIR filter is define as below:

**rrmDlAvgCov = (1 - rrmDlCoMaFilterCoefficient) \* rrmDlAvgCov + rrmDlCoMaFilterCoefficient \* rrmDlInstCov**

where

* rrmDlAvgCov is the long-term covariance matrices (obtained after application of the IIR filter);
* rrmDlInstCov represents the instantaneous port averaged covariance matrices Cov(H) and Cov(V) which are calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6989\_replaced([11155973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
* rrmDlCoMaFilterCoefficient is the filter coefficient. It shall be calculated as the value of **(SRS periodicity/rrmDlBeamSelectTimer). The** rrmDlBeamSelectTimer is the timer duration (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7000\_replaced([11156122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in unit of slot, for beam selection. The SRS periodicity is from the periodicityAndOffset in SRS configuration (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6974\_replaced([11155756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvM_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*\*\*

Note: rrmDlCoMaFilterCoefficient is less than or equal to 1.0 and if the number of to-be-averaged CoMa is less than or equal to **rrmNumOfCoMa (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6965\_replaced([11155684](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxII_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2138\_replaced([11154054](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqadvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the rrmDlAvgCov shall be calculated as arithmetic average, if the number of to-be-averaged CoMa is higher than** rrmNumOfCoMa, the rrmAvgCov shall be calculated according to above IIR filter equation.\*\*\*\*

[Before CB015122-B]

High important note: one CoMa here refers to combined covariance matrix (Cov(H) and Cov(V)) which are combined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6989\_replaced([11155973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB015122-B]

High important note: The instantaneous port averaged CoMa refers to Cov(V) or Cov(H), as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6989\_replaced([11155973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), depending on which filtered long-term CoMa (horizontal or vertical) is calculated.

[End CB015122-B]

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

If NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = True, 5G-L2-PS shall calculate values of [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written as $w\_v^H \vec{R}*{i,v} w\_v$. The expression consists of the following components:

- $\vec{R}*{i,v}$: This represents a matrix or tensor denoted by $R$, with subscripts $i$ and $v$, and a vector arrow above it, indicating it might be a vector or a tensor.

#### 3.18.3.4.0-2 Beam Selection for Dl DL beamforming sync up for CA (ID: 11156051)

**3.18.3.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11156063`)

Beam Selection for Dl
To enable DL beamforming sync up between Pcell and Scell(s), for each UE in Pcell, 5G-L2-PS shall maintain a list of Scell(s), rrmEligibleScellsList, which includes Scell(s) that meet all below eligible conditions:

- The SRS beamforming sync up indicator, in Pcell's Scell context (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2683\_replaced([11120559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR03PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), indicates sync up is needed between Pcell and Scell, and

- Scell is in status of activated (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2804\_replaced([11121880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), [CB006449-CC] and

-    If SCell is configured with UL CA, no periodic SRS is configured for the UE on this SCell. [End CB006449-CC]

Pcell and Scell shall exchange the information about their muting status for energy efficiency (CB008133). Pcell shall only send sync up message to Scell(s) when Pcell and Scell are not muted or Pcell and Scell are all muted.

About DL SU-MIMO, for each UE in Pcell which has valid CoMa (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6995\_replaced([11156011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9U_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), Pcell shall send sync up message to Scell in rrmEligibleScellsList if any condition as below is met:

- the DL beam selection procedure on Pcell is executed (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6995\_replaced([11156011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9U_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and below sync up information is changed compared with the previous sync up.

- the timer rdDlSrsPcellAgeTimerDuration of UE on Pcell is expired. The duration of rdDlSrsPcellAgeTimerDuration is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25877\_replaced([11114009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpgYyvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

About DL SU-MIMO, the sync up message from Pcell to Scell includes below information. The timer rdDlSrsPcellAgeTimerDuration of UE on Pcell shall be restarted when Pcell sends sync up message to Scell.

- Selected DFT beams for PDSCH (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6995\_replaced([11156011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9U_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- PDSCH Power offset if DL power balance is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13465\_replaced([11118538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For Scell which needs sync up DL MU-MIMO information from Pcell [CB013098-C] due to below conditions:

-     Sync up indicator is 'Do sync up for DL SU-MIMO and MU-MIMO' or

-     Sync up indicator is 'Do sync up for DL SU-MIMO' and DL MU-MIMO are enabled on Pcell & Scell with same tapering configuration. See 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_10012\_replaced([11302559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqgVc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) about values of sync up indicator.

, [End CB013098-C] the sync up message from Pcell to Scell shall include below information:

- Information for the case of DL SU-MIMO as specified above.

- If Pcell is not muted for energy efficiency, beamforming gain information and tapering compensation factor (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17254\_replaced([11156015](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9VPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be sent to Scell. NOTE: DL pairing is disabled on cells which are muted for energy efficiency, so there is no need to sync up beamforming gain information between Pcell and Scell for muted cells.

When Scell receives sync up message from Pcell, 5G-L2-PS in Scell shall execute below steps:

- If Pcell is muted for energy efficiency but Scell is not or vice versa, discard the sync up message. Otherwise continue below steps.

- Map DFT beams of Pcell to pattern IDs of DFT beams in Scell.

- Store sync up information for DL SU-MIMO and DL MU-MIMO (if needed) in UE context.

- Restart the timer rdDlSrsScellAgeTimerDuration of UE. The duration of rdDlSrsScellAgeTimerDuration shall be the R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17503\_replaced([11114003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpgYyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- Beams of next PDSCH transmission shall be switched to reported beams from Pcell for DL SU-MIMO.

When rdDlSrsScellAgeTimerDuration is expired or Scell is not active, 5G-L2-PS in Scell shall execute below steps:

- Cleanup related sync up information in UE context in Scell.

-     Beams of next PDSCH transmission shall fallback to PMI or refined beams according to CSI report for SU-MIMO.

---

#### 3.18.3.4.0-4 Beam Selection for Dl Beam selection methods for DL (ID: 11156100)

**3.18.3.4.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `13375889`)

Beam Selection for Dl
[CB015122-B]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The logic of the requirement method 2 has been moved to L1-DU, see [13338218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_rwcPs9qAEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

else

[End CB015122-B]

There are several beam selection methods defined for [CB015122-B] usage in [End CB015122-B] DL [Before CB015122-B] beam [End CB015122-B]. The main difference is how to search for the two beams if two beams are required for rank > 2. For rank <= 2, only one beam is used. R&D parameter rdBeamSelectionAlgType(5G\_UP\_ALG\_24915\_replaced([11158162](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktAYsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is used to decide which of the beam selection methods shall be applied:

 0: Sequential searching method. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11618\_replaced([11156117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 1: Joint searching method 1. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11619\_replaced([11156173](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 2: Joint searching method 2. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11620\_replaced([11156247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note: The RedCap UEs support only up to 2 MIMO layers according to 3GPP 38.306 4.2.21.1 which means that only one beam is needed (there is no need to calculate the second best 2D-DFT DL beam).

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

---

#### 3.18.3.4.1 Sequential searching method

##### 3.18.3.4.1.0-1 Sequential searching method Calculate the best Dl beam (ID: 11156122)

**3.18.3.4.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13377456`)

Sequential searching method
[CB015122-B]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The requirement for finding the best DL beam is moved to L1-DU, since L1-DU selects best/second best/etc. beams

The algorithm shall be triggered when the **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer of UE is expired, where the algorithm is handled in L1-DU, see [13338221](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0QEHY9qAEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). The** rrmDlBeamSelectTimer shall be maintained per UE per SRS resource set. Its slot duration shall be defined as R&D parameter **rdDlBeamSelectTimer, [13378891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0hm4w_2-EfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). It shall be not be smaller than SRS periodicity in slot so** rrmDlCoMaFilterCoefficient in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6993\_replaced([11156001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9UfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) will not be larger than 1).  gNB-DU shall double **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer for the UEs described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29538\_replaced([11158109).](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_xqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)*****\****\*

When the **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer of a UE is expired, the below steps shall be executed:**

1. Restart the timer of **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer using rdDlBeamSelectTimer, [13378891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0hm4w_2-EfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).**

2. Request lower layers (L1-DU) to evaluate the best DFT beams according [13338217](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_imXs0NqAEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

else

[End CB015122-B]

This requirement defines the algorithm for finding the best Dl beam from covariance matrices which are averaged via the IIR filter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6993\_replaced([11156001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9UfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The algorithm shall be triggered when the **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer of UE is expired. The** rrmDlBeamSelectTimer shall be maintained per UE per SRS resource set. Its slot duration shall be defined as R&D parameter (**rdDlBeamSelectTimer, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11383\_replaced([11113992](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpgYxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) default value is 200 slot. It shall not be smaller than SRS periodicity in slot so** rrmDlCoMaFilterCoefficient in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6993\_replaced([11156001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9UfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) will not be larger than 1).  gNB-DU shall double [CB015122-B] the value of [End CB015122-B] **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer for the UEs described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29538\_replaced([11158109).](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_xqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)*****\****\*

When the **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer of a UE is expired, the below steps shall be executed:**

1. Restart the timer of **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer with [13378891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0hm4w_2-EfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)**using rdDlBeamSelectTimer, [13378891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0hm4w_2-EfCPDo8cGBoqIw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).\*\*\*\*

2. Find the best horizontal and vertical DFT beams (**hBest and** vBest) according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7003\_replaced([11156138](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2176\_replaced([11154707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kstdwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*

3. The best DL beam is the Kronecker product of DFT beams **vBest and** hBest.\*\*\*\*

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

##### 3.18.3.4.1.0-3 Sequential searching method Calculate the second-best 2D-DFT Dl beam (ID: 11156149)

**3.18.3.4.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13377464`)

Sequential searching method
13377464:
Sequential searching method
[CB015122-B]
if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1
The requirement shall be removed, as sequential searching method is not not supported.
else
[End CB015122-B]
The algorithm for finding **the second-best 2D-DFT Dl beam is the same as** the second-best 2D-DFT UL beam defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2181\_replaced([11154797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kstdx_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) except independent correlation threshold **rdDlSrsCorrelationFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_11381\_replaced([11113986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpgYw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is used for Dl. Additionally power [Before CB015122-B] balancedness [CB015122-B] ratio [End CB015122-B] between best and second best beam shall be checked as below:*****\*
assume [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is written as:
$a1 = w\_{best\_h}^H R\_{SRS\_h} w\_{best\_h}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10373.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] in horizontal,  [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$a2 = W\_{secondbest\_h}^H R\_{SRS\_h} W\_{secondbest\_h}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10373.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]  in horizontal, and [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in white text against a white background. The equation is:
$b1 = w\_{best\_v}^H R\_{SRS\_v} w\_{best\_v}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10373.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]  in vertical, [image-3][image\_desc]b2 = WHsecondbest\_v RSRS\_v Wsecondbest\_v[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10373.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] in vertical:
If (a2*b2)/(a1*b1) < a given threshold* rdPowerRatio (5G\_UP\_ALG\_8629\_replaced([11113979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpgYwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then the second-best beam shall not be used.\*
If the second best beam is not to be used due to [Before CB015122-B] power unbalancedness [ CB015122-B] too low power ratio [End CB015122-B] between best beam, then
 For PDSCH
o If only one best beam is needed, then the best SRS beam shall be adopted.
o else if two beams are needed, if dlMimoMode is "CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" or "OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" the** two beams shall be SSB/refined beams defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2025\_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); If dlMimoMode is "CL 8x4 MIMO" t**he two beams shall be PMI /SSB/Refined beams defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2028\_replaced([11112211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UEs under 8 ports mode and SSB/refined beams defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2025\_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UEs under 4 ports mode. Note that this may lead to PDSCH and PDCCH using different beams.**\*\*
 For UE specific CSI-RS
o The two beams for 4 port CSI-RS shall be SSB/refined beams defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2025\_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
 
Note: For PDCCH only best beam is needed so best SRS beam shall be adopted whether the 2nd best beam is available or not.
[CB015122-B]
end
[End CB015122-B]

#### 3.18.3.4.2 Joint searching method 1

##### 3.18.3.4.2.0-1 Joint searching method 1 Calculate the best DL beam (ID: 11156179)

If rank = 3 or 4, then 2 beams are used. Two beams are jointly determined according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11627\_replaced([11156192](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkbPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

##### 3.18.3.4.2.0-2 Joint searching method 1 Calculate two beams jointly (ID: 11156192)

**3.18.3.4.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13377471`)

Joint searching method 1
13377471:
Joint searching method 1
[CB015122-B]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The logic of the requirement is removed, as Joint searching method 1 is no longer supported.

else

[End CB015122-B]

The two beams are jointly selected by following steps:

Step 1: For all candidate horizontal and vertical DFT beams, the beam power are calculated is:

For horizontal beam j, [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$P\_{h,j} = abs(w'*{h,j} \* R*{SRS,h} \* w\_{h,j})$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

For vertical beam j, [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$P\_{v,j} = abs(w'*{v,j} \* R*{SRS,v} \* w\_{v,j})$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Where

 [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w\_{n,j}" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are a light brown color with a subtle gradient, and they have a dark outline. The background is black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is the horizontal DFT beam weight vector.

 [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w\_{v,j}".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is the vertical DFT beam weight vector.

 [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "RSRS,h" in a stylized font. The "R" is larger and bolder than the other letters, and the "SRS,h" is smaller and appears to be a subscript. The text is in a gradient of blue and orange, with a slight blur effect.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] is the horizontal long-term covariance matrix.

 [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "RSRS,v" in a stylized font. The letters are in a dark color, possibly black or dark blue, and appear to be slightly blurred. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5] is the vertical long-term covariance matrix.

Step 2: Find 10 horizontal beams with maximum power and 6 vertical beams with maximum power. Generate total 60 2D-DFT beams by Kronecker product of horizontal beam and vertical beam. For each 2D-DFT beam, the beam power is the product of horizontal beam power and vertical beam power:

[image-6][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in black text on a white background. The equation is:
$P\_j = P\_{h,j} \* P\_{v,j}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6]

Step 3: Find the beam pair {beam a, beam b} from 60 2D-DFT beams:

For i from index of total 60 2D-DFT beams

For j = 0 to i

Calculate the correlation between beam i and beam j: [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in white text against a black background. The formula is:
`corr(i,j) = abs((Wh,i ⊗ Wv,i)' * (Wh,j ⊗ Wv,j))`
Here's a breakdown of the components:
\* `corr(i,j)`: This likely represents a correlation function or coefficient between two entities indexed by `i` and `j`.
\* `abs(...)`: This denotes the absolute value of the expression within the parentheses.
\* `Wh,i` and `Wv,i`: These likely represent vectors or matrices, possibly related to horizontal (`h`) and vertical (`v`) components, indexed by `i`.
\* `Wh,j` and `Wv,j`: Similar to the above, but indexed by `j`.
\* `⊗`: This symbol typically represents the element-wise product (Hadamard product) of two matrices or vectors.
\* `'`: This symbol usually denotes the transpose of a matrix or vector.
\* `*`: This symbol likely represents matrix multiplication.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7]

If corr(i,j) > rdDlSrsCorrelationFactor then corr(i,j) = 1

Calculate beam pair power: [image-8][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$P\_{i,j} = P\_i \* P\_j \* (1 - \sqrt{corr(i, j)})$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8]

End

End

The beam pair (a,b) is the beam pair which achieves the maximum beam pair power  [image-9][image\_desc]The image contains the text "P a,b" in a blurry, close-up view. The letters are in a dark color, and the background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9]

Step 4: If  [image-10][image\_desc]The image contains the mathematical equation "P\_a = P\_b". The equation is written in black text on a white background. The letters "P" are capitalized, and the subscripts "a" and "b" are lowercase. The equals sign is centered between the two "P" terms.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10], then the switch to the diagonal beam pair (beam c, beam d), where beam c weight is [image-11][image\_desc]The image contains mathematical notation. It shows the expression "Wh,a ⊗ Wv,b". The symbol "⊗" represents the Kronecker product.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.012.png[/image\_path][/image-11] and beam d weight is [image-12][image\_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression $W\_{h,b} \otimes W\_{v,a}$. The expression consists of two variables, $W\_{h,b}$ and $W\_{v,a}$, separated by the symbol $\otimes$, which typically represents the Kronecker product.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10378.013.png[/image\_path][/image-12]. Otherwise beam pair (beam a, beam b) are output.

For rdDlSrsCorrelationFactor see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11381\_replaced([11113986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpgYw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB015122-B]

end

[End CB015122-B]

#### 3.18.3.4.3 Joint searching method 2

#### 3.18.3.4.3-1 Joint searching method 2

**3.18.3.4.3-1.0-4**  (ID: `12770193`)

Joint searching method 2
Due to the pronto 02688605, there is higher residual HARQ BLER issue in TMO field. According to the log analysis, SRS I/Q data in some eAxC received in L1-Hi are lost for some partial antennas in some slots (found in AEHC in TMO network). Before the problem is solved between RU and L1, a workaround solution is requested in L2-PS: if the current PDSCH transmission is HARQ retransmission with the number of retransmission >= a given threshold, then use the legacy beams (PMI beams) instead of SRS beams for the current PDSCH transmission.

If actDlSrsBm = true AND (NRCELL.tmpActFeat1.bit24 = 1 (for 23R1 release) or NRCELL.actSrsBeamFallbackByRetrx = true (after 23R1 release)) **AND the current number of HARQ retransmission >= rdSrsBeamFallbackByReTrxThrd [PR852940] AND the current beam for PDSCH is DFT beam AND the used beam for previous PDSCH (re)transmission on the current HARQ process is DFT beam [End PR852940] (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17126\_replaced([11114114](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kphm6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then**

 If UE is served with 8 port cell specific CSI-RS, then the beam(s) for PDSCH shall be PMI/SSB/Refined beams defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2028\_replaced([11112211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The beam for PDCCH is forced to SSB/Refined beams.

The beam change does not affect on the SRS state defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6963\_replaced([11155665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxIIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The time duration of using legacy beams for PDSCH is dependent on the value of NIDD parameter srsDlBeamFallbackOption:

 If srsDlBeamFallbackOption = "fallback once", then legacy beam is only used for the following HARQ retransmission of this TB. For the next TB transmission, SRS beam is used if it is valid.

 If srsDlBeamFallbackOption = "fallback until next beam calculation", then legacy beam is used until the next beam selection time (rrmDlBeamSelectTimer expired). When rrmDlBeamSelectTimer expired, SRS beam is used according to beam selection method (5G\_UP\_ALG\_11616\_replaced([11156100](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9XPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 If srsDlBeamFallbackOption = "fallback until different beam available", then until the next beam selection time (rrmDlBeamSelectTimer expired) legacy beam is used. When rrmDlBeamSelectTimer expired,  if averaged CoMa updated condition (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29619\_replaced([11155739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvMPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is met, gNB-DU executes the beams selection algorithms defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11616\_replaced([11156100](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9XPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

o If the new best SRS beam is different with the last best SRS beam, then stop fallback and use SRS beam;

o otherwise use the legacy beam until the next beam selection time.

**[CB012971-E]** For the case of eCPRI 7-2a, **[End CB012971-E] the WA also works for UEs with valid SRS based subband beams (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21411\_replaced([11156802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OzvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), all SRS based beam shall not be used.**\*\*\*\*

The adaptation with DL MU-MIMO (CB008305) refer to 5G\_UL\_ALG\_7454.

Note: This workaround solution is only enabled before the SRS lost issue is solved. When the SRS lost issue is solved, this workaround solution shall be disabled or removed.

---

#### 3.18.3.4.3-2 Joint searching method 2

**3.18.3.4.3-2.0-1**  (ID: `11156402`)

Joint searching method 2
The parameter srsDlBeamFallbackOption can be online modified. When the value of srsDlBeamFallbackOption is online modified:

 For UEs who are not triggered to fallback, the new value shall take effect immediately. From the current slot, L2-PS shall use the new value to determine the fallback option.

 For UEs who are already triggered to fallback, the new value shall take effect as below:

o If the old value is “fallback once”, then for UEs who are using legacy beam(PMI/SSB beam) as fallback, L2-PS shall continue to use legacy beam for the current TB. From next TB transmission, L2-PS shall stop fallback and determine if UEs shall be fallback to legacy beams according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17122\_replaced([11156372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0LdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the new value of srsDlBeamFallbackOption.

o If the old value is "fallback until next beam calculation", then for UEs who are using legacy beam(PMI/SSB beam) as fallback, L2-PS shall continue to use legacy beam until next beam selection time (rrmDlBeamSelectTimer expired). From next beam selection time, L2-PS shall stop fallback and determine if UEs shall be fallback to legacy beams according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17122\_replaced([11156372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0LdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the new value of srsDlBeamFallbackOption.

o If the old value is "fallback until different beam available",  then for UEs who are using legacy beam(PMI/SSB beam) as fallback, L2-PS shall continue to use legacy beam until next beam selection time (rrmDlBeamSelectTimer expired). From next beam selection time, no matter if the new selected best SRS beam is same as the old best SRS beam or not, L2-PS shall stop fallback. And from next beam selection time, L2-PS shall determine if UEs shall be fallback to legacy beams according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17122\_replaced([11156372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0LdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the new value of srsDlBeamFallbackOption.

13377613:
Joint searching method 2

[End CB015122-B]
The two beams are jointly selected by following steps:
Step 1: For all candidate horizontal and vertical DFT beams, the beam power are calculated as:
For horizontal beam j, [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$P\_{h,j} = abs(w'*{h,j} \* R*{SRS,h} \* w\_{h,j})$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10384.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
For vertical beam j, [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$P\_{v,j} = abs(w'*{v,j} \* R*{SRS,v} \* w\_{v,j})$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10384.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]
Where
 [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w n,j" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are a light color with a darker outline, and the overall image has a soft focus.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10384.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is the horizontal DFT beam weight vector.
 [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w\_{v,j}".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10384.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is the vertical DFT beam weight vector.
 [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "RSRS,h" in a stylized font. The "R" is larger and bolder than the other letters, and the "SRS,h" is smaller and appears to be a subscript. The text is in a gradient of blue and orange, with a slight blur effect.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10384.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] is the horizontal covariance matrix.
 [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "RSRS,v" in a stylized font. The letters are in a dark color, possibly black or dark blue, and appear to be slightly blurred. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10384.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5] is the vertical covariance matrix.
Step 2: Find 10 horizontal beams with maximum power and 6 vertical beams with maximum power. Generate total 60 2D-DFT beams by Kronecker product of horizontal beam and vertical beam. For each 2D-DFT beam, the beam power is the product of horizontal beam power and vertical beam power:
[image-6][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in black text on a white background. The equation is:
$P\_j = P\_{h,j} \* P\_{v,j}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10384.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6]
Step 3: Find the beam pair {beam a, beam b} from 60 2D-DFT beams:
For i from index of total 60 2D-DFT beams
For j = 0 to i
if ([image-7][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression written in a light-colored font on a white background. The expression is:
`abs(Ph,i - Ph,j) < NRCELL.dttBeamDiffThresholdH`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10384.010.png[/image\_path][/image-7] AND [image-8][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is: abs(P\_{u,i} - P\_{u,j}) < NRCELL.dftBeamDiffThreshold.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10384.011.png[/image\_path][/image-8])
Calculate the metric of beam pair: [image-9][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
`metric(i, j) = Pᵢ * Pⱼ * (1 - corrMetric(i, j))²`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10384.012.png[/image\_path][/image-9], where [image-10][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is for `corrMetric(i, j)` and is defined as the absolute value of the product of two terms, squared, divided by the product of `Pi` and `Pj`. The first term in the numerator is `(w'h,i * RSRS,h * wh,j)` and the second term is `(w'v,i * RSRS,v * wv,j)`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10384.013.png[/image\_path][/image-10]
end
End
End
where:
\* NRCELL/dftBeamDiffThresholdH**- defines the power threshold between two horizontal DFT beams which are candidate for beam selection option 3.**
\* NRCELL/dftBeamDiffThresholdV**-  defines the power threshold between two vertical DFT beams which are candidate for beam selection option 3.**
The beam pair (a,b) is the beam pair which achieve the maximum beam pair metric [image-11][image\_desc]The image contains the text "metric(i,j)". The text is blurry and appears to be in a sans-serif font. The letters are dark on a light background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10384.014.png[/image\_path][/image-11].
Step 4: Output beam pair (beam a, beam b).
[CB015122-B]
end
[End CB015122-B]

#### 3.18.4.1.0-2 Overivew On-line modification of SB BF related NIDD parameters (ID: 11156440)

**3.18.4.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11156445`)

Overivew
**[CB0014094-A] gNB-DU shall support on-line modification of parameters in structure NIDD:NRCELL.srsForSubbandBm. Not every parameter in the structure is on-line modifiable. For all online modifiable parameters in this structure, the modified value is taken into use when the parameter is used by gNB the next time.**

Note: when one parameter is online changed, some first measurement may be not accurate. Some legacy measurement result may be not updated. Detail refers SW design. No need to increase SW complexity for this case since we don't expect customer to change the parameter in this way on purpose frequently and the impact of first several measurement is also limited.**[End CB0014094-A]**

---

#### 3.18.4.1.0-3 Overivew About eCPRI 7-2a and 7-2e (ID: 11156450)

**3.18.4.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11156454`)

Overivew
From DL SB BF related functionalities point of view:

For the case of eCPRI 7-2a, the BTS.actEcpri72e equals to 'disabled'.

For the case of eCPRI 7-2e, the BTS.actEcpri72e equals to 'Ecpri72eULDL'.

---

#### 3.18.4.1.0-4 Overivew SB BF enabled UE (ID: 11156460)

**3.18.4.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11156471`)

Overivew
An UE is considered as subband beamforming UE in a given cell if the following conditions are met:

* This cell is subband beamforming enabled, that is NIDD:actDlSrsSubbandBm for this cell is equal to true.
* UE is indicated by Cplane. [Before CB009527-B] In this chapter WB SRS is used for WB SRS for subband BF even wide band BF can also have WB SRS configured according NIDD:bSRS and cSRS. [End CB009527-B]

---

#### 3.18.4.1.0-5 Overivew Buffer identifier for L1 (ID: 11156476)

**3.18.4.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11156481`)

Overivew
5G-L2-PS shall maintain one identifier for UEs that have subband beamforming enabled to help L1 to maintain its channel matrix storage

---

#### 3.18.4.1.0-6 Overivew Ping-Pong pattern IDs for RU (eCPRI 7-2a only) (ID: 11156487)

**3.18.4.1.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `11156507`)

Overivew
For the case of eCPRI 7-2e:

5G-L2-PS doesn't need to store ping-pong pattern IDs for SB BF because BWVs for SB BF are directly calculated by L1 Radio in slots for scheduling PDSCH. The ping-pong buffer is also managed by L1 Radio which is not visible to upper layers. To tigger SB BF for PDSCH, 5G-L2-PS shall send UE identifier for SB BF in PDSCH sending request to trigger RZF [CB009527-D] or SVD [End CB009527-D] based SB BF for transmitting PDSCH. See the detail in definition of PDSCH sending request message.

For the case of eCPRI 7-2a:

The maximum number of BWVs needed per UE shall be decided by bandwidth of the cell in unit of PRB, bfSubbandSize: beamforming subband size, maxRank: maximum rank of PDSCH of the UE which is hard coded as 4. The maximum number of BWVs needed for the UE is:

rrmMaxBWVs = roundup (bandwidth/bfSubbandSize+1)\*maxRank,

5G-L2-PS shall reserve subband beam start pattern IDs for each UE with subband beamforming enabled. The number of IDs is twice the number of BWVs of this UE.  Rationale: Each UE needs two sets of IDs to distinguish the ones that are under update and the others that can be used by PDSCH. RU stores and uses BWVs for each UE in its memory in ping-pong mechanism. When BWVs in ping is updating, the BWVs stored in pong will be used for PDSCH transmission until the update in ping is ready.

5G-L2-PS shall store the two start beam pattern IDs for Ping and Pong for the UE.

5G-L2-PS shall indicate start pattern ID for Ping and Pong for each UE once and L1 will maintain the Ping-Pong scheme.

---

#### 3.18.4.1.0-7 Overivew Number of requested subband BWVs for L1 (eCPRI 7-2a only) (ID: 11156513)

**3.18.4.1.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `11156527`)

Overivew
[CB009527-A]

This requirement is only for the case of eCPRI 7-2a.

[End CB009527-A]

5G-L2-PS shall indicate to L1 the number of BWVs within single beamforming subband equal to the rank from the latest valid CSI report after rank adaption defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23994\_replaced([11139686](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krpGxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Rank update for VoNR special scheduling shall not impact here if NRBTS/NRCELL.actDlVonrRestrictMaxMcsAndLayer is true (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13140\_replaced([11139539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krn4p_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: all procedures that reset or replace reported Rank saved at gNB side will also be used here.

[End CB009527-A]

5G-L2-PS shall save the broken antenna(TRX) info from high layer as cell level property for subband BF. At cell setup stage the all TRX of the cell shall be seen as valid.

#### 3.18.4.1.0-9 Overivew Indication for MMSE regularization term (eCPRI 7-2a only) (ID: 11156548)

**3.18.4.1.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `11156558`)

Overivew
[CB009527-A]

This requirement is only for the case of eCPRI 7-2a.

[End CB009527-A]

5G-L2-PS shall indicate regularization term but whether L1 use it or not depends L1 configuration as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13937\_replaced([11107475](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kofsKfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If rdMmseRegularizationMode (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22652\_replaced([11158523](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktC0-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 2 (dynamic adjusting based on signal quality) and  rdIncludeSrsVolatilityStatusMetric(5G\_UP\_ALG\_23159\_replaced([11158466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktCN_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is true and  NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsSinrThreshold > rrmMinWbSrsSinr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14919\_replaced([11107414](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kofFF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) :

- If SINRavg (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22633\_replaced([11157155](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks6SEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is invalid then SINRavg shall be considered as rrmMinWbSrsSinr in this requirement.

- If the UE is lowChannelVolatileUe (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22751\_replaced([11157478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

-- If SINRavg < rrmMmseFactorLowVolatileT1

regularization term is 0.01;

-- elseif SINRavg  < rrmMmseFactorLowVolatileT2

regularization term is 0.001;

-- else

regularization term is 0.0001.

- else (the UE is highChannelVolatileUe or earlyWbSrsCorr status in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22751\_replaced([11157478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

-- If SINRavg  < rrmMmseFactorHighVolatileT1

regularization term is 0.01;

-- elseif SINRavg  < rrmMmseFactorHighVolatileT2

regularization term is 0.001;

-- else

regularization term is 0.0001.

elseif rdMmseRegularizationMode is 1 (fix adjusting based on channel volatility) and  rdIncludeSrsVolatilityStatusMetric (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23159\_replaced([11158466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktCN_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is true

- If the UE is lowChannelVolatileUe (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22751\_replaced([11157478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

-- regularization term is rdMmsePowerFactor  ;

- else (the UE is highChannelVolatileUe or earlyWbSrsCorr status)

-- regularization term is rdMmsePowerFactor\*10 ;

else:

- 5G-L2-PS shall indicate regularization term according to rdMmsePowerFactor which is defined in the same way as L1 parameter in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19840\_replaced([11110396](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpDs3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall make sure regularization term is within range [0.1, 0.0001] before sending to L1.

rrmMmseFactorLowVolatileT1 = min {rdMmseFactorLowVolatileStep1 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23138\_replaced([11158629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktDcDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsSinrThreshold, 40dB};

rrmMmseFactorLowVolatileT2 = min {rdMmseFactorLowVolatileStep2 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23140\_replaced([11158639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktEDEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + rrmMmseFactorLowVolatileT1 , 40dB};

rrmMmseFactorHighVolatileT1 = min {rdMmseFactorHighVolatileStep1 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23134\_replaced([11158607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktDcCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsSinrThreshold, 40dB};

rrmMmseFactorHighVolatileT2 = min {rdMmseFactorHighVolatileStep2 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23136\_replaced([11158618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktDcC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + rrmMmseFactorHighVolatileT1 , 40dB};

Note: Assuming all parameters here have unit as dB.

#### 3.18.4.1.0-10 Overivew SINR difference for L1 (ID: 11156565)

**3.18.4.1.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11156570`)

Overivew
[Before CNI-99771] Input:

1. rrmCorrAvgCqi = rrmAvgCqi + rrmDeltaCqi which is correct average WB-CQI (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7557\_replaced([11125689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))); The same default value as scheduler for PDSCH can be adopt when these variables are unavailable.
2. Rank for subband BWVs calculation which is the number of requested subband beam (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13887\_replaced([11156513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks1ZkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));
3. CQI to MCS mapping tables in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3028\_replaced([11126310](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqw9C_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); Always assume PTRS OFF, Number of PRB as 133. Note: There are 8 tables: Rank 1 to Rank 4, with and without 256QAM.
4. Two CQI to SINR formulas in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3009\_replaced([11126006](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqwV8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
5. The mcs-Table used by this UE in LA is 'qam256' or not. Note: 'qam64LowSE' UEs are not supported.

Algorithm:

1. If mcs-Table is 256QAM:SinrQ4 =15.1, SinrQ6 =20.5+ rdPbMaxSinrAdjust64QAM(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14359\_replaced([11114086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kphm4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), SinrQ8 = 26.5 + rdPbMaxSinrAdjust256QAM(5G\_UP\_ALG\_15639\_replaced([11114080](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpg_8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Else if mcs-Table is not 256QAM: SinrQ4 =15.0,  SinrQ6 =21.1+ rdPbMaxSinrAdjust64QAM(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14359\_replaced([11114086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kphm4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

1. Map rrmCorrAvgCqi to SinrLA via formulars in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3009\_replaced([11126006](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqwV8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
2. Decide modulation k based on mapping rrmCorrAvgCqi to MCS via tables in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3028\_replaced([11126310](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqw9C_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the selected rank, with or without 256QAM;
3. If modulation k is lower than rdPbModulationOrder (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15634\_replaced([11114073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpg_6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or selected rank is 1, then SinrDiff = 50dB (invalid);

Else SinrDiff = 2x(SinrQk - SinrLA), where Qk is Q4 / Q6 or Q8 depends on modulation k.

Output:

Send SINR difference (SinrDiff) to L1.

[End CNI-99771]

---

#### 3.18.4.1.0-11 Overivew Mapping relationship between PRB/SRS SB/BF SB (ID: 11156577)

**3.18.4.1.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11156582`)

Overivew
This requirement only applies to eCPRI 7-2e.

In 5G-L2-PS, it shall maintain mapping relationship between index of PRB, BF SB and SRS SB. The mapping relationship is defined as below:

The mapping between index of PRB and BF SB shall be calculated as below:

indexBfSb = rounddown(indexPRB/sizeBfSb)

- indexBfSb is the index of BF SB.

- indexPRB is the index of PRB.

- sizeBfSb is the size of BF SB.

The mapping between index of PRB and SRS SB shall be calculated as below:

IF indexPRB < freqDomainShift

indexSrsSb = 0

NOTE: it’s possible that some PRB(s) at low edge have no SRS signal scheduled because freqDomainShift is higher than zero (for example, some PRBs at low edge are blanked by the blanking feature). These PRB(s) shall be mapped to the first SRS SB for simplification.

ELSE

indexSrsSb = (indexPRB – freqDomainShift)/sizeSrsSb

indexSrsSb = MIN(indexSrsSb, numSrsSb – 1)

NOTE: it’s possible that some PRB(s) at high edge have no SRS signal scheduled. These PRB(s) shall be mapped to the last SRS SB for simplification.

- freqDomainShift is the value of freqDomainShift in SRS resource. See SRS-Resource definition in 3GPP 38.331.

- indexSrsSb is the index of SRS SB. For WB SRS, only index 0 is valid.

- numSrsSb is the number of SRS SB in whole BW.

ENDIF

Below table is an example about mapping between index of PRB, BF SB and SRS SB.

The cell BW is 20MHz (51 PRBs), the BF SB size is 4, first two PRBs are blanked. Two SRS SB are configured, and SRS SB size is 20 PRBs (cSRS = 11, bSRS = 1). In this example, SRS signal cannot be scheduled on PRBs 2~3 and 44~50 because the SRS bandwidth can be configured is up to 40 PRBs according to 3GPP. The SRS frequency domain shift is 4 PRBs.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| nPRB | BF SB index (bfSbIndex) | SRS SB Index (srsSbIndex | Notes |
| 0 | 0 | INVALID | Two PRBs are blanked, no SRS signal on these PRBs |
| 1 |  |  |  |
| 2 | 0\* | PDSCH can be scheduled on these PRBs. No SRS signal on these PRBs due to freqDomainShift alignment with boundary of BF SB by L3. |  |
| 3 |  |  |  |
| 4 | 1 | 0 | These PRBs shall be mapped to the SRS SB index 0 |
| 5 |  |  |  |
| 6 |  |  |  |
| 7 |  |  |  |
| 8 | 2 |  |  |
| 9 |  |  |  |
| 10 |  |  |  |
| 11 |  |  |  |
| 12 | 3 |  |  |
| 13 |  |  |  |
| 14 |  |  |  |
| 15 |  |  |  |
| 16 | 4 |  |  |
| 17 |  |  |  |
| 18 |  |  |  |
| 19 |  |  |  |
| 20 | 5 |  |  |
| 21 |  |  |  |
| 22 |  |  |  |
| 23 |  |  |  |
| 24 | 6 | 1 | These PRBs shall be mapped to the SRS SB index 1 |
| 25 |  |  |  |
| 26 |  |  |  |
| 27 |  |  |  |
| 28 | 7 |  |  |
| 29 |  |  |  |
| 30 |  |  |  |
| 31 |  |  |  |

#### 3.18.4.1.0-12 Overivew Indication for capturing PDSCH BWVs in RU (ID: 11156590)

**3.18.4.1.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11156595`)

Overivew
This requirement only applies to eCPRI 7-2e.

When 5G-L2-PS sends PDSCH sending request to L1 Radio with beams of SB BF, it shall inform L1 Radio with below information about how to capture PDSCH BWVs and related SRS CE in RU for troubleshooting purpose:

- The sampling rate, selBwvSubband, for capturing PDSCH BWVs and related SRS CE data in RU. The sampling rate indicates L1 Radio which BF SB scheduled for PDSCH shall be captured. By default, selBwvSubband = rdSamplingRatePdsch (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27824\_replaced([11158854](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktFROfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If PDSCH is scheduled for HARQ retransmission, selBwvSubband = ROUNDUP(0.5 \* rdSamplingRatePdsch).

- The method about how to store captured data in RU. It is configured via rdSampleStoreMethod (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27818\_replaced([11158833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktFRNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- Please refer to L1 interface about PDSCH sending request for detail.
