### 3.18.4.2 SRS Reception

### 3.18.4.2-1 SRS Reception

**3.18.4.2-1.0-1**  (ID: `11156720`)

SRS Reception
Note: If the cell enters power saving mode,

subband BWVS for PDSCH/CSI-RS will not be used; CoMa is needed; Channel correlation for channel volatility is needed (used in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21817\_replaced([11157124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

subband beam correlation to DFT beams for EIRP is not needed subband BF gain [CB008322-G] and MMSE regularization term [End CB008322-G] is not needed but still 5G-L2-PS may indicate these calculation request to L1 for simplicity. Final decision depends on SW.

---

### 3.18.4.2-2 SRS Reception

#### 3.18.4.2-2.0-1 SRS Reception SB BF UE with measurement gap impact Criteria (ID: 11156732)

**3.18.4.2-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11156742`)

SRS Reception
As defined by 3GPP, each periodical SRS resource within SRS resource set for antenna switching usage will have one occurrence for each SRS periodicity.

[CB009527-E] For the case of eCPRI 7-2e, SRS occurrence of a UE with SB BF is not overlapped with measurement gap.

For the case of eCPRI 7-2a, [End CB009527-E] If NRCELL.srsForSubbandBm/actHoWithSbBf is true and for a UE with SB BF and measurement gap configured:

- Criterion 1: For this UE, 5G-L2-PS shall check whether at least one occurrence of at least one SRS resource within the set are overlapped with measurement gap.

- Criterion 2: For this UE, 5G-L2-PS shall check whether all occurrences of the set have at least one SRS resource overlapping with gap.

---

#### 3.18.4.2.0-1 SRS Reception Indication for SRS decoding (ID: 11156605)

**3.18.4.2.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `12578331`)

SRS Reception
**For the case of eCPRI 7-2e, to ensure L1 Radio correctly handle SRS CE, 5G-L2-PS shall send the SRS CE operation indicator to L1 Radio according to below rules. About mapping between index of PRB and SRS SB, see ([11156577](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks1ZnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

* If index of current SRS SB is 0 (the first SRS SB), 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this to L1 Radio for handling BF SB CE at starting PRB(s). For the case of WB SRS, it shall always be considered as the first SRS SB.
* If index of current SRS SB is (numOfSrsSB – 1) (the last SRS SB), 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this to L1 Radio for handling BF SB CE at ending PRB(s). The numOfSrsSB is the number of SRS SB configured in cell. For the case of WB SRS, it shall always be considered as the last SRS SB.
* If SRS signal is the first time to be received on related SRS SB and SRS port, 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this to L1 Radio that correlation calculation on related SRS SB is not needed.
* 5G-L2-PS shall indicate L1 Radio how to handle SRS CE for case of DTX and high interference. The default behavior is decided by RD parameter, rdSrsCeOperation, defined in ([11158704](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktEDIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB012971-E]

* 5G-L2-PS shall indicate L1 Radio to calculate and send back singular values to DU in SRS receiving response. The singular value is calculated using SVD with the latest SRS CE on the middle PRB of SRS subband (see [12580757: Singular value calculation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_U0YvMDIBEfCfjdcwDn2YOQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). 5G-L2-PS shall implement a round-robin algorithm to make sure each SB BF UE has chance to be updated with the latest singular values. The number SVD operation per TTI shall not exceed limitation of L1 RU (see [12580757: Singular value calculation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_U0YvMDIBEfCfjdcwDn2YOQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). Once 5G-L2-PS receives singular values from L1 Radio, it shall log this information in TTI trace for feature analysis purpose.

[End CB012971-E]

When one SRS resource is to be received, 5G-L2-PS shall indicate L1 the legacy information for SRS decoding defined in ([11155751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: all DRX, measurement gap, UL CA, remote interference mitigation and additional UL mitigation for RIM RS detection and etc. is the same as ([11155751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.18.4.2.0-2 SRS Reception Indication for subband BWVs calculation (eCPRI 7-2a only) (ID: 11156626)

**3.18.4.2.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `12877285`)

SRS Reception
**[CB009527-A]**

**This requirement is only for the case of eCPRI 7-2a.**

**[End CB009527-A]**

If criterion 1 of SB BF UE with measurement gap impact (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27388\_replaced([11156732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is met: 5G-L2-PS shall suspend indicating BWV calculation when gap starts and resume the BWV calculation when gNB receives all SRS resources within the set again. The exact slot for BWV calculation follows later restriction.

If Cplane indicate current cell has minimal SRS periodicity for subband BF, (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_11618\_replaced([11304985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqtJyfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

5G-L2-PS shall enabled additional BWV calculation

else

5G-L2-PS shall disable additional BWV calculation

When additional BWV calculation is disabled, the BWV calculation slot is:

When all ports of SRS resources in the SRS resource set are to be received at L1 and at the BWV calculation slot indicated by CPlane 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_10970\_replaced([11289580](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqB0UfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When additional BWV calculation is enabled, the BWV calculation slot is:

When all ports of SRS resources in the SRS resource set are to be received at L1 and at the BWV calculation slot indicated by CPlane 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_10970\_replaced([11289580](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqB0UfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **the first time for a UE, and additional BWV calculation slot decided by 5G-L2-PS.**

5G-L2-PS shall indicate L1 the following information for subband BWVs calculation:

* The subband beamforming identifier of the UE (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13882\_replaced([11156476](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0yifvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));
* The beamforming subband size (NRCELL/bfSubbandSize).
* Number of requested BWVs per subband (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13887\_replaced([11156513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks1ZkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* The broken antenna info of the conected RU to the cell.

5G-L2-PS shall indicate additional BWV calculation with these restriction: The maximum number of UEs whose BWV are calculated for each slot based on L1 HW capacity is according to 5G\_UP\_8271\_replaced([11398824](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uf9bXvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); time length between twice BWV calculation for a UE can not be smaller than 10 slots for any frame structure; when there is multi-UEs need BWV calculation, the older the previous BWVs of a UE is, the higher priority will this UE be indicated for BWV calculation; each UE of the cell that needs RT BF will have BWV calculated at least once within one SRS periodicity.

Rationale: L1 requires Cplane to spread different UEs BWV calculation to different slot if several UEs' last SRS resources drop to the same slot.

---

#### 3.18.4.2.0-3 SRS Reception Indication for SRS Covariance Matrices(CoMa) calculation (ID: 11156649)

**3.18.4.2.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `12825045`)

SRS Reception
5G-L2-PS shall indicate L1 the starting PRB and subband size (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2153\_replaced([11154391](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksromvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of subband based on which the SRS Covariance Matrices (CoMa, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6982\_replaced([11155852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **are calculated.  
The slot of CoMa request shall be the same as SRS resource for SB BF.**

**For the case of eCPRI 7-2e, 5G-L2-PS shall just select SRS SB for CoMa by sweeping the SB within current SRS subband. The size of SRS SB for CoMa is calculated from bSRS and cSRS for WB BF. [PR856729] If two SRS symbols per slot is enabled and the comb for SB BF is comb4 and the SRS SB size calculated from bSRS and cSRS for WB BF is smaller than 8 PRB, then use 8 PRB.[End PR856729]**

**For the case of eCPRI 7-2a, 5G-L2-PS shall maintain the cell specific SB size in number of PRBs according bSRS and cSRS of the cell and sweep the SB within the SRS bandwidth for CoMa calculation.**

**High important note: L1 requires all UEs within the cell that need CoMa have the same number of PRBs. The subband for CoMa and for CSI-RS beams calculation may have different number of PRBs and start PRB.**

**Note: Specific information elements containing information from C-Plane are defined respectively in  starting PRB and subband are defined  in the  5G\_L2\_IF\_411\_replaced([10975309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (see freqDomainShift) and 5G\_L2\_IF\_115\_replaced([10968891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (dlSrsBmConfig.srsSubbandSize)**

---

#### 3.18.4.2.0-4 SRS Reception Indication for 4-port UE specific CSI-RS beams calculation (ID: 11156669)

**3.18.4.2.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `12788565`)

SRS Reception
5G-L2-PS shall indicate one BF sub-band whose channel estimation is used by L1 for the BWVs calculation of wideband short-term CSI-RS beams. The slot is the same as subband BWVs calculation in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13880\_replaced([11156626](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2Ap_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**For the case of eCPRI 7-2a:**

- 5G-L2-PS shall sweep the BF SB for the BWVs calculation of 4 wideband short-term CSI-RS beams within the SRS bandwidth.

**[CB009527-B] For the case of eCPRI 7-2e:**

- 5G-L2-PS shall randomly select one SRS SB which has valid SRS CE (see status VAL in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26998\_replaced([11156904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks4c5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on all SRS ports.

- If the valid SRS SB cannot be found, 5G-L2-PS shall still use legacy beams for transmitting CSI-RS for CSI.

- If the valid SRS SB can be found, 5G-L2-PS shall inform L1 Radio to calculate BWVs for wideband CSI-RS beams with SRS CE at selected BF SB by providing below information:

1) Position of middle PRB within selected SRS SB.

2) UE buffer identifier.

**[End CB009527-B]**

Note: The SB set shall be the same as BF subband. SW may have some simplification for the last subband.

Note: The wideband short-term CSI-RS beams are always 4 BWVs comprising both polarizations so each port of CSI-RS will be transmitted via both polarizations of RU.

---

#### 3.18.4.2.0-5 SRS Reception Indication for EIRP correlation expansion calculation (ID: 11156683)

**3.18.4.2.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11156698`)

SRS Reception
[CB009527-E]

For the case of eCPRI 7-2e, if EIRP control is active and the DFT beam response has been received from Cplane:

- 5G-L2-PS shall trigger EIRP expansion coefficient calculation one time per EIRP sample period (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22030\_replaced([11118888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1sPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) via PDSCH sending request that uses subband beams.

- [Before CB009527-E-UPD001] 5G-L2-PS shall receive expansion coefficient values from PDSCH sending response. If 5G-L2-PS doesn’t receive PDSCH sending response within the time window of rrmEirpCalculationWindow (5G\_UP\_ALG\_28568\_replaced([11158875](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktFRPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall trigger EIRP expansion coefficient calculation again in the next PDSCH sending request that uses subband beams.

[End CB009527-E-UPD001]

For the case of eCPRI 7-2a, [End CB009527-E] if EIRP control is active and the DFT beam response has been received from Cplane:

- 5G-L2-PS shall indicate one BF sub-band in sweeping way whose BWVs are used by L1 to calculate expansion coefficient. The SB set shall be the same as BF subband.

- The EIRP expansion coefficient calculation if need shall be one time per EIRP sample period (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22030\_replaced([11118888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1sPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- If criterion 1 of SB BF UE with measurement gap impact (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27388\_replaced([11156732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is met: 5G-L2-PS shall suspend indicating EIRP expansion coefficient calculation when gap starts and resume EIRP expansion coefficient calculation when gNB receives all SRS resources within the set again.

---

#### 3.18.4.2.0-6 SRS Reception Indication for capturing SRS CE in RU (ID: 11156705)

**3.18.4.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11156710`)

SRS Reception
This requirement only applies to eCPRI 7-2e.

When 5G-L2-PS sends SRS receiving request to L1 Radio for UE which is configured as SB BF, it shall inform L1 Radio with below information about how to capture SRS CE in RU for troubleshooting purpose:

- The sampling rate, selSrsCESubband, for capturing SRS CE data in RU. The sampling rate indicates L1 Radio which BF SB scheduled for SRS shall be captured. Its value is configured in rdSamplingRateSrsCe (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27822\_replaced([11158844](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktFRN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- The method about how to store captured data in RU. It is configured via rdSampleStoreMethod (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27818\_replaced([11158833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktFRNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- Please refer to L1 interface about SRS receiving request for detail.

### 3.18.4.3 Beam selection for DL

#### 3.18.4.3.0-1 Beam selection for DL Subband BF (ID: 11156752)

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11156757`)

Beam selection for DL
Subband BWVs update (eCPRI 7-2a only)

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11156771`)

Beam selection for DL
[CB009527-A]

This requirement is only for the case of eCPRI 7-2a.

[End CB009527-A]

5G-L2-PS shall set subband BWVs as valid only after 5G-L2-PS receives feedback that BWVs of the required number of layers are calculated successfully from L1 and with some latency added.

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11156776`)

Beam selection for DL
Subband BWVs aging (eCPRI 7-2a only)

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11156791`)

Beam selection for DL
[CB009527-A]

This requirement is only for the case of eCPRI 7-2a.

[End CB009527-A]

5G-L2-PS shall consider subband BWVs including BWVs for UE specific CSI-RS are valid for this UE in 5G-L2-PS if the interval from last valid subband BWVs received from L1 is less than rrmSubbandBeamAging. Otherwise, subband BWVs are invalid for this UE in 5G-L2-PS.

Denote periodicity of BWVs as periodicityBwv within which gNb receives all 4 ports of SRS.

if periodicityBwv  < 160  (slots)

rrmSubbandBeamAging = periodicityBwv \* 2 + rdSubbandBeamAgingConstant (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20833\_replaced([11158189](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktAYt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

else

rrmSubbandBeamAging = periodicityBwv + rdSubbandBeamAgingConstant (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20833\_replaced([11158189](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktAYt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11156797`)

Beam selection for DL
Subband BWVs usage

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11156802`)

Beam selection for DL
Criteria for subband BF usage

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `13434069`)

Beam selection for DL
If the cell is not under power saving mode, for UE which is configured with SB BF, 5G-L2-PS shall try to apply the subband BF for **PDSCH according to below conditions:**

**For the case of eCPRI 7-2a:**

* the subband BWVs are updated successfully at both BU and RU side, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14113\_replaced([11156757](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
* the subband BWVs are not outdated, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14111\_replaced([11156776](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
* small PRB condition is not met, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21412\_replaced([11156825](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks310_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* RU restriction is not met, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22202\_replaced([11156841](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks311vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Rank of PDSCH equals to number of BWVs, refer to rank decision in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21414\_replaced([11156886](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks4c4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

5G-L2-PS shall indicate these BWVs for PDSCH scheduling via indicating the start pattern ID for these BWVs and corresponding rank. Detail refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13891\_replaced([11112241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**For the case of eCPRI 7-2e:**

[CB014315-A]

* If LT CFO is enabled (see [11151369](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksYtq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) AND LT CFO <= rdDlLtCfoThdSuMimo (see [13434062: rdDlLtCfoThdSuMimo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_jl5WVSEwEfGbZ5_vsUrUNw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), and

[End CB014315-A]

[Before CB014315-A]

* If PDSCH is scheduled with RAT0 and the criteria of SRS quality (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26998\_replaced([11156904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks4c5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is met, SB BF shall be applied.

[CB014315-A]

* If the criteria of SRS quality (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26998\_replaced([11156904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks4c5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is met, and

[End CB014315-A]

* If PDSCH is scheduled with RAT1, 5G-L2-PS shall check below steps due to RU restriction defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28998\_replaced([11156877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks312_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

{

If numOfPrb < bfSbSize, SB BF shall NOT be applied.

}

5G-L2-PS shall indicate utilizing SB BF for PDSCH in PDSCH sending request. See detail in L1 interface for PDSCH sending request.

If the cell is not under power saving mode, 5G-L2-PS shall try to apply the subband BWVs for **UE specific 4 port CSI-RS only when all the following conditions are met.**

**For the case of eCPRI 7-2a:**

* the subband BWVs are updated successfully at both BU and RU side, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14113\_replaced([11156757](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
* the subband BWVs are not aging, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14111\_replaced([11156776](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

5G-L2-PS shall indicate these BWVs for UE specific CSI-RS for channel acquisition. Detail refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13891\_replaced([11112241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**For the case of eCPRI 7-2e:**

* it's controlled by RD parameter defined in CP3. If it is enabled, 5G-L2-PS shall inform L1 Radio to calculate RZF or SVD at selected BF SB for transmititng CSI-RS in CSI-RS sending request. See details in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21094\_replaced([11156669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2ns_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and L1 interface for CSI-RS sending request.

If the cell is under power saving mode, subband BWVs shall not be used for any UE and any physical channel.

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11156825`)

Beam selection for DL
Small PRB restriction (eCPRI 7\_2a only)

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11156835`)

Beam selection for DL
[CB009527-A]

This requirement is only for the case of eCPRI 7-2a.

[End CB009527-A]

5G-L2-PS shall maintain mid-PRB index that L1 used for BWVs calculation for each sub-band. Refer to L1 algorithm 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14126\_replaced([11107396](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koeeD_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13924\_replaced([11107540](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kog6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5GMAX Massive MIMO Algorithm specification §5.1.2.2.

If number of PRB to be scheduled for this UE's PDSCH in current slot is less than rdMinNumPrbSbBeam (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21397\_replaced([11158494](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktC08_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall check the distance between startPRB of each PDSCH RBG and mid-PRB of the BF sub-band that include this startPRB for RAT0 and the distance between startPRB and mid-PRB of the BF sub-band that include this startPRB for RAT1. If the distance for one of the PDSCH RBG is larger than rdMaxDistPrbSbBeam (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21399\_replaced([11158506](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktC09fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall not indicate sub-band BWVs for this PDSCH.

Rationale: Currently L1 only calculate sub-band BWVs based on channel estimation of mid-PRB within the BF sub-band, so if the PDSCH only have limited number of PRBs, the BLER would be higher compared to larger number of PRBs.

Note: Later L1 add interference detection functionality and etc. which may change the PRB for BWV calculation but L2 here does not adapt accordingly for simplicity.

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11156841`)

Beam selection for DL
RU restriction (eCPRI 7-2a only)

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `12876687`)

Beam selection for DL
12876687:
Beam selection for DL
**[CB009527-A]**

**This requirement is only for the case of eCPRI 7-2a.**

**[End CB009527-A]**

After FD scheduling (that is start Prb allocation step), if the number of beams to be used in a slot exceeds RU's capacity of max number of beams per slot or max number of beams per symbol, gNB-DU shall not indicate sub-band BWVs for any UE scheduled **for this slot transmission.**

Rationale: 5G-L2-PS cannot indicate changed subband size currently.

**Note: For UE** with valid subband BWVs, gNB-DU shall increment the number of sub band beams as soon as a PRB of RAT1 allocation overlaps a subband beam. For a dynamicswitch RAT0, gNB-DU shall count the number of subband beams like a RAT0 allocation.\*\*\*\*

fig: in this example, for the UE with subband beams, this RAT1allocation uses 6 BF subbands

Each "BF subban" segment is further divided into two parts, with "BF" and "subban" written vertically.

Note: For the cells with small cell bandwidth on RF6.2 32/64TRX mMIMO RUs, the cell will be indicated via NIDD:NRCELL/limitedBeamsPerStreamPerSlot, the actually number of beams per slot for the cell actually is 31 which is smaller than the one RU reported, but based on analysis the actual usage won't exceed 31 if smallest BF subband size is 4PRB. Thus no special handling is added for this fake RU capability.

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11156877`)

Beam selection for DL
RU restriction (eCPRI 7-2e only)

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11156881`)

Beam selection for DL
For the case of eCPRI 7-2e, due to restriction in L1 Radio (B\_MUL), 5G-L2-PS shall not schedule more than one UE using SB BF beams within the same BF SB. For example, if BF SB size is 4-PRB, 4-PRB in each BF SB cannot be allocated to multiple SB BF UEs in frequency domain.

This RU restriction only apply to SB BF UE. It means to FDM schedule WB BF and SB BF UEs in the same BF SB is OK.

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11156886`)

Beam selection for DL
Rank decision

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `12521579`)

Beam selection for DL
**For the case of eCPRI 7-2e:**

PDSCH rank is always decided by 5G-L2-PS.

**For the case of eCPRI 7-2a:**

When the subband BWVs are updated successfully and is not outdated **and small PRB condition is not met, 5G-L2-PS shall decide rank for UE's PDSCH transmission as below:**

Denote number of subband BWVs received from L1 as N.

**For initial transmission of PDSCH:**

[Before CNI-137616-A]

If rdRankForRtBeam (5G\_UP\_ALG\_19887\_replaced([11158576](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktDcA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 1: Always rank decided by 5G-L2-PS will be used.

else if rdRankForRtBeam is 0: [End CNI-137616-A]

{If 5G-L2-PS adjusted the rank as the UE is in transient phase (rank degradation) or rank adaptation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3210\_replaced([11139690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krpGx_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9661\_replaced([11139510](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krn4ovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13140\_replaced([11139539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krn4p_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then 5G-L2-PS shall use this rank for PDSCH transmission.

else 5G-L2-PS shall use rank N for UE PDSCH transmission. }

**For retransmission of PDSCH:  
Rank of retransmission shall always be the same as initial transmission.**

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `11156904`)

Beam selection for DL
SRS quality measurement (eCPRI 7-2e only)

---

**3.18.4.3.0-1.0-3.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11156923`)

Beam selection for DL
This requirement only applies to eCPRI 7-2e.

In 5G-L2-PS, it shall maintain the SRS quality table for each SB BF UE. 5G-L2-PS shall utilize this table to dynamically decide whether SB BF can be applied for PDSCH to SB BF UE.

In the SRS quality table, one column represents one SRS port, one row represents one SRS SB (if SRS is configured as WB, only one row is needed). Each item in the table includes SRS CE status as below:

- INV: SRS is not scheduled yet on related SRS port and SRS SB.

- VAL: SRS CE is done on related SRS port and SRS SB without DTX [CB009527-B] and High interference. [End CB009527-B]

- DTX: SRS power/SINR on related SRS port and SRS SB is less than pre-defined thresholds. Its status is reported by L1 via SRS receiving response.

[CB009527-B]

- HI\_INTF: High interference is detected on related SRS port and SRS SB (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26920\_replaced([11107641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kohhYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

[End CB009527-B]

[CB009527-E]

When a cell enters RI state = 2 (remote Interference is detected, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9324\_replaced([11161371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktT6t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall reset SRS quality table of all SB BF UEs to initial status (INV status), 5G-L2-PS shall also discard SRS report related to SB BF from L1 Radio.

[End CB009527-E]

The table below is an example of SRS quality table. In SRS SB#0, the port2 is detected as DTX. In SRS SB#1, the port1 is detected as high interference. In SRS SB#5, SRS CE is not done yet.

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| indexSrsSb (see definition in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27068\_replaced([11156577](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks1ZnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | port0 | port1 | port2 | port3 |
| 0 | VAL | VAL | DTX | VAL |
| 1 | VAL | HI\_INTF | VAL | VAL |
| 2 | VAL | VAL | VAL | VAL |
| 3 | VAL | DTX | VAL | VAL |
| 4 | VAL | VAL | VAL | VAL |
| 5 | INV | INV | INV | INV |

In the below algorithm, the srsSbSet includes all SRS SBs which can be mapped to PRBs scheduled for PDSCH. About mapping between PRB and SRS SB, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27068\_replaced([11156577](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks1ZnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall execute below steps to decide whether SB BF shall be applied for transmitting PDSCH:

1) For each SRS SB in the set of srsSbSet, if any SRS SB includes INV status, then SB BF cannot be applied.

2) 5G-L2-PS shall calculate srsQualityIndicator using the below formula:

srsQualityIndicator(srsSbSet, rank) = numValidSrsPort(srsSbSet)/(rank \* numOf(srsSbSet))

where

- numValidSrsPort(srsSbSet) is the total number of valid SRS ports (under VAL status) within SRS subbands in set of srsSbSet.

-  numOf(srsSbSet) is the number of SRS subbands in the set of srsSbSet.

3) If srsQualityIndicator > rdSrsQualityIndThreshold,

then SB BF shall be applied. About rdSrsQualityIndThreshold, see definition in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27010\_replaced([11158691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktEDH_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

### 3.18.5 WB/SB BF switching algo (Basic)

#### 3.18.5.1 State machine for SRS configuration

##### 3.18.5.1.0-1 State machine for SRS configuration Overview of the states (ID: 11156941)

**3.18.5.1.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `13429028`)

State machine for SRS configuration
13429028:
State machine for SRS configuration
[CB014315-A]

The state machine defined in this chapter is only valid when NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Basic'. When NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced', the switching algorithm is defined in [13432274: WB/SB BF switching algorithm (Enhanced)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Oc5CoB7HEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

[End CB014315-A]

If NRCELL/actDlSrsSubbandBm is true, 5G-L2-PS shall maintain state machine about SRS configuration for any UE which is eligible for SB BF monitoring on current serving cell (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_11282\_replaced([11305474](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqxbNPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), for the following cases:

·    when P-SRS for long term **DL BF is configured to one UE’s for current serving cell and UE has capacity of 4R TAS SRS resources for the current serving cell.**

·    when P-SRS for subband BF is configured to one UE’s for current serving cell.

Otherwise, no configuration state machine shall be maintained.

The state machine shall be setup when the C-Plane configures or updates the UE and the U-Plane with the relevant P-SRS configuration.

Note 1: with no special proclaim again, all SRS in this chapter means P-SRS(periodic SRS).

For FDD PCell + TDD FR1 SCell CA UE (including UL CA and SRS carrier switching), UE in TDD FR1 SCell does not support SB BF.

For:  
- TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 [CB014067-B], or   
- FR1 TDD + TDD + FDD (with intra-band contiguous TDD CCs with TDD PCell) [End CB014067-B]  
UL CA UE, UE can be under SB\_BF\_CONF state on only one serving cell at the same time.

**Note: For:  
- TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 [CB014067-B], or   
- FR1 TDD + TDD + FDD (with intra-band contiguous TDD CCs with TDD PCell) [End CB014067-B]  
UL CA UE, reconfiguration to P-SRS for SB BF on [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell may cause reconfiguration of codebook P-SRS and TAS P-SRS for WB BF on PCell; reconfiguration to P-SRS for SB BF on PCell may cause reconfiguration of codebook P-SRS and TAS P-SRS for WB BF, even release of TAS P-SRS for WB BF on [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell. (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_15304\_replaced([11307177](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tq6lMPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detail).**

The main states managed are the followings (see the figure hereafter):

·    State of **SRS\_TRANS is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21332\_replaced([11156967](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));**

·    State of **WB\_BF\_CONF is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21334\_replaced([11156985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));**

·    State of **SB\_BF\_CONF is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));**

In the following state machine, the procedure to activate the SRS configuration (setup/modification) is defined in [11153999: Modification of SRS configuration and activation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a state diagram illustrating the transitions between different states related to SRS (Sounding Reference Signal) configuration. The diagram consists of four states: "SRS\_Trans", "SB\_SRS\_Conf", "WB\_SRS\_Conf", and "Stop State".
- **SRS\_Trans**: This is the central state, represented by a double circle, indicating it's a significant or initial state.
- **SB\_SRS\_Conf**: This state, represented by a single circle, is labeled "SB\_SRS\_Conf". It has a self-loop indicating that certain conditions can keep it in this state. The conditions for staying in this state are "rdSrs ToL3Timer Expired", "rd Srs Switch Prohibit Timer expired", and "rdNumber SrsCheck meets".
- **WB\_SRS\_Conf**: This state, also a single circle, is labeled "WB\_SRS\_Conf". It also has a self-loop with the conditions for staying in this state being "rd Srs Switch Prohibit Timer expired" and "rdNumber Srs Check meets".
- **Stop State**: This state is represented by a thick black circle, signifying the end of a process or a terminal state.
There are several transitions between these states, indicated by arrows and labeled with events or conditions:
- From "SRS\_Trans" to "SB\_SRS\_Conf": An arrow points from "SRS\_Trans" to "SB\_SRS\_Conf" labeled "Receive WB SRS configuration" (red arrow) and "SB SRS configuration activation" (green arrow).
- From "SB\_SRS\_Conf" to "SRS\_Trans": An arrow points from "SB\_SRS\_Conf" to "SRS\_Trans" labeled "Receive SB SRS configuration" (green arrow).
- From "SRS\_Trans" to "WB\_SRS\_Conf": An arrow points from "SRS\_Trans" to "WB\_SRS\_Conf" labeled "Receive SB SRS configuration" (red arrow) and "WB SRS configuration activation" (green arrow).
- From "WB\_SRS\_Conf" to "SRS\_Trans": An arrow points from "WB\_SRS\_Conf" to "SRS\_Trans" labeled "Receive WB SRS configuration" (green arrow).
- From "WB\_SRS\_Conf" to "Stop State": An arrow points from "WB\_SRS\_Conf" to "Stop State" labeled "Receive WB SRS release".
The diagram visually represents a system's behavior in response to different SRS configuration and release events.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-09161836.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

File: SRS\_States.vsd

Folder: [3 L2RT Algorithms](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:f:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/5G%20UP%20Algorithms/3%20L2RT%20Algorithms?csf=1&web=1&e=UqUpZa)

##### 3.18.5.1.0-2 State machine for SRS configuration State of SRS_TRANS (ID: 11156967)

**3.18.5.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12789179`)

State machine for SRS configuration
When the U-Plane uses the new setting to manage DCI Format 0\_1 before the reception of the RRC reconfiguration complete [PR850237-26R1], if not already used by the U-Plane [End PR850237-26R1], then the transient phase concerns only the SRS management as detailed hereafter.

When the SRS configuration is modified and until its activation ([11153999: Modification of SRS configuration and activation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), the U-Plane applies the following procedure:

 When enters this state:

 Stop the **rrmWbSrsConfigProhibitTimer** and rrmWbSrsReleaseProhibitTimer if either one of them is running.\*\*\*\*

 5G-L2-PS shall save newly received SRS configuration.

 Under this state:

 5G-L2-PS shall stop monitoring DL Buffer/channel quality periodically which is defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21345\_replaced([11157044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 5G-L2-PS shall stop indicating legacy SRS request to L1.

 [Before PR850237-26R1] ; When UE has RRC Reconfiguration complete received for the relevant WB SRS [PR850237-26R1] When the new SB configuration is activated (see [11153999: Modification of SRS configuration and activation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) [End PR850237-26R1], switch to **SB\_BF\_CONF.**

 [Before PR850237-26R1] ; When UE has RRC Reconfiguration complete received for the relevant SB SRS [PR850237-26R1] When the new configuration with WB BF is activated (see [11153999: Modification of SRS configuration and activation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) [End PR850237-26R1], switch to **WB\_BF\_CONF.**

 If gNB-CU rejects the reconfiguration, gNB-DU shall roll back the previous SRS configuration before RRC Reconfiguration. Note: this roll back indication may be included in User modify messages and the details depends on CP3 design.

**rrmWbSrsConfigProhibitTimer = max {NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/wbSrsConfigProhibitTimer**, (rrmPeriodSrsCheck +1) *NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/numWbSrsConfigSample}.*\*\*\*

**rrmWbSrsReleaseProhibitTimer = max {NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/wbSrsReleaseProhibitTimer, (rrmPeriodSrsCheck +1)\* NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/numWbSrsReleaseSample, (rrmCoMaAgedCycle+1) \* SRS periodicity}, SRS periodicity is the periodicity of WB SRS.**

rrmPeriodSrsCheck (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21345\_replaced([11157044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

##### 3.18.5.1.0-3 State machine for SRS configuration State of WB_BF_CONF (ID: 11156985)

**3.18.5.1.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `13429495`)

State machine for SRS configuration
It's the state for UEs with WB BF configuration take effect as legacy 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6973\_replaced([11155751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2146\_replaced([11154169](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note: SW may take different implementation because the tasks are distributed to different cores, the end-to-end behavior is the same.

When enters this state:

· Start/restart the **rrmWbSrsConfigProhibitTimer**

· SRS configuration related measurement in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21342\_replaced([11157039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be reset.

· 5G-L2-PS shall start indicating WB BF request to L1 and update DFT beams as defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6962\_replaced([11155660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2135\_replaced([11154028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqacvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Under this state:

· When the serving cell enters is not under power saving mode (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2550\_replaced([11118320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqB9PfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **and not Remote Interference Mitigation (RIM) scheme (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9172\_replaced([11163373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** and not additional UL mitigation for RIM RS detection (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13520\_replaced([11162042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-APvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **and (UE has "BWP switch" state machine runs and BWP status as "scheduled in large BWP"):**\*\*\*\*

{

· 5G-L2-PS shall monitor and evaluate whether SB BF is recommended for a UE (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21342\_replaced([11157039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

· When rdSrsToL3Timer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21393\_replaced([11158477](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktC08PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expired and 5G-L2-PS sends the first N UEs in waitingWbSrsUeList to Cplane as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21391\_replaced([11157614](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then for these N UEs, restart the **rrmWbSrsConfigProhibitTimer.**

}

· When 5G-L2-PS has user setup / modification received for the changed periodic SRS and this resource will be used for DL BF, switch to **SRS\_TRANS.**

· When the serving cell enters power saving mode (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2550\_replaced([11118320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqB9PfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **or Remote Interference Mitigation (RIM) scheme (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9172\_replaced([11163373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** or additional UL mitigation for RIM RS detection (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13520\_replaced([11162042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-APvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **or SB BF pool is used for WB BF (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_11655\_replaced([11305823](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tqz3c_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or stop recommending indicated by Cplane, 5G-L2-PS shall stop recommending UEs for SB BF. When the serving cell come out of above status, 5G-L2-PS shall start monitoring and evaluation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21342\_replaced([11157039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rdSrsToL3Timer for all UEs that shall be monitored.**\*\*\*\*

· Beside cell level status change, 5G-L2-PS shall stop the monitor for this UE if the UE capability is not 4R TAS SRS **or UE is not scheduled in large BWP** or with DCI-based switch procedure ongoing (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1868\_replaced([11111144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLBkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). 5G-L2-PS shall start the monitor for this UE if the UE capability is supporting 4R TAS SRS **and UE is scheduled in large BWP without DCI-based switch procedure ongoing (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1868\_replaced([11111144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLBkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). SRS configuration related measurement in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21342\_replaced([11157039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be reset when monitor.**\*\*\*\*

·     If rdDisableSbBfVoNR = True, 5G-L2-PS shall stop the monitor for this UE if the UE is configured with VoNR bearer. About rdDisableSbFbVoNR, see definition in [13431483: rdDisableSbBfVoNR (CNI-165571)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_zsqxYh4WEfG9L99MQBns2Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

· When WB BF is released and no P-SRS resource configured anymore by L3, 5G-L2-PS shall stop the monitor for this UE as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21315\_replaced([11156930](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks4c5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

· Beside above status change:

* For:  
  - TDD FR1 + TDD [CB014067-B], or
* FR1 TDD + TDD + FDD (with intra-band contiguous TDD CCs with TDD PCell) [End CB014067-B]   
  FR1 UL CA UE,
* 5G-L2-PS shall stop the monitor for this UE on PCell if SRS for SB BF is configured on [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell.
* 5G-L2-PS shall stop the monitor for this UE on [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell if SRS for SB BF is configured on PCell or [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell is deactivated or transform precoder is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3270\_replaced([11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on PCell.
* 5G-L2-PS shall start the monitor for this UE on PCell if SRS for SB BF is deconfigured on [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell.
* 5G-L2-PS shall start the monitor for this UE on [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell if SRS for SB BF is deconfigured on PCell and [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell is activated and transform precoder is disabled on PCell.
* SRS configuration related measurement in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21342\_replaced([11157039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be reset when monitor stops.

---

##### 3.18.5.1.0-4 State machine for SRS configuration State of SB_BF_CONF (ID: 11157009)

**3.18.5.1.0-4.0-6**  (ID: `12880651`)

State machine for SRS configuration
It's the state for UEs with SB BF configuration take effect as legacy 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6973\_replaced([11155751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2146\_replaced([11154169](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note: SW may take different implementation because the tasks are distributed to different cores, the end to end behavior is the same.

When enters this state:

· Start/restart the **rrmWbSrsReleaseProhibitTimer.**

· SRS configuration related measurement in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21342\_replaced([11157039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be reset.

· 5G-L2-PS shall start indicating SRS request to L1 and update short term and long term beams as defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13751\_replaced([11156407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0Le_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

· **[Before CB015640-C] For the case of eCPRI 7-2e, set the** rrmNoAddDlDmrsSwitchEnabled to False**.**\*\*\*\*

· **For the case of eCPRI 7-2a, [End CB015640-C] The** rrmNoAddDlDmrsSwitchEnabled is always set to False on SCell.\*\*\*\*

· If NRCELL/actNoAddDlDmrsSwitchSbBf is true and UE has addditional DMRS (dmrsAdditionalPosition is not equal to 'pos0' (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9301\_replaced([11115621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpwQY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) on P(S)Cell **: gNB-DU shall**

- set the **rrmNoAddDlDmrsSwitchEnabled to True on P(S)Cell.**

- shall mark the UE as 'additional DL DMRS enabled SB BF UE' on P(S)Cell.

Under this state:

· 5G-L2-PS shall monitor DL Buffer/channel quality periodically as defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21345\_replaced([11157044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

· 5G-L2-PS shall evaluate whether to request WB BF as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21380\_replaced([11157558](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8HSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS shall inform L3 to change this UE’s SRS resource to WB BF and restart the **rrmWbSrsReleaseProhibitTimer.**

· When 5G-L2-PS has user setup / modification received for the changed periodic SRS and this resource will be used for DL BF, switch to **SRS\_TRANS.**

· When SRS for SB BF is released and no P-SRS resource configured anymore by L3, 5G-L2-PS shall stop the monitor for this UE as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21315\_replaced([11156930](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks4c5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

· If **rrmNoAddDlDmrsSwitchEnabled = True and none of the conditions (cell and UE level) defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27685\_replaced([11157646](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uWvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met:**

-5G-L2-PS shall perform additional DL DMRS switching (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27186\_replaced([11157630](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

-Start/restart the **rrmNoAddDlDmrsConfigProhibitTimer timer.**

· If SB BF is released, 5G-L2-PS shall reset the **rrmNoAddDlDmrsSwitchEnabled and clean up measurement and counters for DMRS switch in [11157630](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)**.\*\*\*\*

· If NRCELL/actNoAddDlDmrsSwitchSbBf is online changed from true to false, if UE is marked as 'additional DL DMRS enabled SB BF UE', set **rrmNoAddDlDmrsSwitchEnabled to false and clean up measurement and counters for DMRS switch in [11157630](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), stop the** rrmNoAddDlDmrsConfigProhibitTimer timer.\*\*\*\*

The **rrmNoAddDlDmrsConfigProhibitTimer timer is initiated with min(**rdNoAddDlDmrsConfigProhibitTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27202\_replaced([11158729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktEqIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), **rrmWbSrsReleaseProhibitTimer initalisation value** (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21332\_replaced([11156967](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))).***\****\*

---

#### 3.18.5.2 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation

##### 3.18.5.2.0-1 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Overview of periodic measurements and evaluation (ID: 11157044)

**3.18.5.2.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `13432327`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
[CB014315-A]

The periodic measurements and evaluation algorithm defined in this chapter is only valid when NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Basic'. When NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced', the switching algorithm is defined in [13432274: WB/SB BF switching algorithm (Enhanced)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Oc5CoB7HEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

[End CB014315-A]

If NRCELL/actDlSrsSubbandBm is true and SRS configuration state machine (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21329\_replaced([11156937](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks4c6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is setup for UE, 5G-L2-PS shall evaluate the SB or WB BF configuration.

For UEs under **WB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21334\_replaced([11156985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) except special cell and UE status as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21334\_replaced([11156985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):**

5G-L2-PS shall make measurements for each interval rrmPeriodSrsCheck:

1. Monitoring Buffer Status (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21353\_replaced([11157336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): High or Low
2. Monitoring radio link quality (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): Good or Bad

Evaluate UE’s status according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21376\_replaced([11157453](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with at least valid NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/numWbSrsConfigSample measurements:

* SB BF is recommended (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21378\_replaced([11157541](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8HRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Maximum number of UEs that can be measured at same time depends on gNB entity level capacity.

For UEs under **SB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

If the periodic SRS for SB BF is configured in handover procedure, 5G-L2-PS shall suspend the monitor until first valid CSI report for channel acquisition is received. Otherwise, **5G-L2-PS shall make measurements for each interval rrmPeriodSrsCheck:**

1. Monitoring Buffer Status (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21353\_replaced([11157336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): High or Low
2. Monitoring radio link quality (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): Good or Bad

Evaluate UE’s status according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21376\_replaced([11157453](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with at least valid NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/numWbSrsReleaseSample measurements:

* WB BF is recommended (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21380\_replaced([11157558](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8HSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

where rrmPeriodSrsCheck is **20 slot.**

##### 3.18.5.2.0-2 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Fallback Function of Subband DL beamforming (informative) (ID: 11157068)

**3.18.5.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11157086`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
11157086:
Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
[CB009527-A]
NOTE: to make requirement to be more generic, this requirement is revised by replacing names of WB SRS and SB SRS to SB BF and WB BF. PLEASE remove this NOTE when a new version is created.
[End CB009527-A]
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating the "8322 Fallback Function". The flowchart uses different shapes to represent states and decisions. Rounded rectangles represent states or actions, while diamond shapes represent conditions or decisions. Arrows indicate the flow between these elements.
Here's a breakdown of the flowchart:
**Legend:**
\* A rounded rectangle with a solid border represents an "Edge".
\* A dashed line represents a "Fall back function".
\* A diamond shape represents a "condition".
\* A rounded rectangle with a dashed border within a larger rounded rectangle represents "RRC configuration & active feature".
**Flowchart Elements:**
1. **Start:** A solid black circle at the top indicates the start of the process.
2. **State (1) WB BF (8247):** The process begins with Wideband Beamforming (WB BF) with identifier 8247.
3. **Condition (2) If eligible for WB SRS:** A decision point checks if the system is eligible for Wideband Sounding Reference Signal (WB SRS).
\* If "yes", the flow proceeds to condition (3).
4. **Condition (3) If RRC re-conf. allowed:** Another decision point checks if RRC reconfiguration is allowed.
\* If "yes", the flow proceeds to state (4).
5. **State (4) SB BF (8322/9527):** The process moves to Shortband Beamforming (SB BF) with identifiers 8322/9527.
6. **Condition (5) If non-eligible for SB BF:** A decision point checks if the system is non-eligible for SB BF.
\* If "yes", the flow proceeds to condition (6).
7. **Condition (6) If RRC re-conf. allowed:** A decision point checks if RRC reconfiguration is allowed.
\* If "yes", the flow proceeds to state (1) WB BF (8247). This indicates a fallback to the initial state.
8. **Condition (7) If SB beam conditions:** A decision point checks the Shortband (SB) beam conditions.
\* If "yes", the flow proceeds to condition (8).
9. **Condition (8) If SRS CoMa valid:** A decision point checks if the SRS Channel Measurement (CoMa) is valid.
\* If "yes", the flow proceeds to state (9) WB BF (8247).
10. **State (9) WB BF (8247):** The process returns to Wideband Beamforming (WB BF) with identifier 8247.
11. **State (10) UE reported DL WB BF (534/2200):** This state represents User Equipment (UE) reported Downlink Wideband Beamforming (DL WB BF) with identifiers 534/2200. This state is reached via a dashed line from condition (8), indicating a fallback function.
12. **Label (11) RRC re-configuration:** This label is associated with a dashed line originating from condition (3) and pointing towards state (4), signifying an RRC reconfiguration event.
13. **Label (12) Fallback by RRC re-configuration:** This label is associated with a dashed line originating from condition (6) and pointing towards state (1), indicating a fallback triggered by RRC reconfiguration.
14. **Label (13) Dynamic fallback w/o RRC re-configuration:** This label is associated with a dashed line originating from condition (8) and pointing towards state (10), indicating a dynamic fallback that does not involve RRC reconfiguration.
The flowchart outlines a complex decision-making process for beamforming fallback mechanisms, considering eligibility for different beamforming types, RRC reconfiguration status, and specific beam conditions.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10510.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
File: FlowCharts-8322Fallback.pptx
Folder:
 
(1) UE is served by SRS based DL beamforming with sub-band SRS resources using wideband beams.
(2) UE is selected on scheduled PRB ratio (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21353\_replaced([11157336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on radio link quality check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), see overview (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21376\_replaced([11157453](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21345\_replaced([11157044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
(3) RRC re-configuration rate is limited to one per 500ms per UE by default.
(4) UE is served by SRS based DL beamforming using sub-band beams. NOTE: for eCPRI 7-2a, SRS is configured as wideband resource (CB008322). For eCPRI 7-2e, SRS can be configured as wideband or sub-band resource based on configuration (CB009527).
(5) UE is de-selected on scheduled PRB ratio (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21353\_replaced([11157336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on radio link quality check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), see overview (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21376\_replaced([11157453](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21345\_replaced([11157044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
(6) See (3)
(7) If sub-band beam condition is met as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21411\_replaced([11156802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OzvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
(8) SRS Covariance Matrix (CoMa) is average over time and can be still valid for some time even if latest channel matrix is not valid anymore.
(9) UE is dynamically served by SRS based DL beamforming using wideband beams.
(12) SRS is RRC re-configured for WB BF for example with larger SRS period. Usually, SRS period for WB BF is longer than SB BF.

##### 3.18.5.2.0-3 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation On-line modification of WB and SB switch related NIDD parameters (ID: 11157091)

**3.18.5.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12479968`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
5G-L2-PS shall support on-line modification of parameters in structure NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch. Not every parameter in the structure is on-line modifiable. For all online modifiable parameters in this structure, the modified value is taken into use when the parameter is used by gNB the next time.

Note: when one parameter is online changed, some first measurement may be not accurate. [CB014094-B] Some legacy measurement result may be not updated. Detail refers SW design. [End CB014094-B] No need to increase SW complexity for this case since we don't expect customer to change the parameter on purpose frequently and the impact of first several measurement is also limited.

---

##### 3.18.5.2.0-4 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Power estimation of SRS for SB BF (ID: 11157103)

**3.18.5.2.0-4.0-5**  (ID: `12880640`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
For UEs under WB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21334\_replaced([11156985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or SB\_BF\_CONF **(5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

**-**For the case of eCPRI 7-2e, the algorithm in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27600\_replaced([11154591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) specifies how to calculate SRS power per port per RE (SRS\_EPRE). If UE is not under **SRS\_DL\_BM\_VALID, then SRS power shall be considered as invalid.**\*\*\*\*

**-**For the case of eCPRI 7-2a, 5G-L2-PS shall calculate SRS power per port per RE (SRS\_EPRE) based on averaged CoMa (rrmAvgCov: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2166\_replaced([11154579](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for codebook SRS and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6993\_replaced([11156001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9UfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for TAS SRS) for DL BM. Only the CoMa that are used for DL BM shall be considered. If the codebook SRS is not used for DL BM, it shall not be used. Power calculation based on CoMa is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2165\_replaced([11154516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If there is no valid averaged CoMa or the UE is not under **SRS\_DL\_BM\_VALID, then consider this power is invalid.**\*\*\*\*

For UEs under WB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21334\_replaced([11156985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

5G-L2-PS shall estimate SB\_BF\_SRS\_EPRE as below:

1. Calculate P\_SRS based on number of PRB (n\_prb\_srs) for periodic sub-band SRS resources that are configured to the UE, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10497\_replaced([11119432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

* P\_SRS = min (P\_Cmax , P0\_SRS + 10Log (2^µ \* n\_prb\_srs) + alpha\_srs\* PL +rrmAdjustedAccumulatedTpcPE)

Where rrmAdjustedAccumulatedTpcPE shall be accumulated δ\_srs (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10497\_replaced([11119432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) after been cut within range -rdMaxAccumulatedTpcPE to + rdMaxAccumulatedTpcPE (5G\_UP\_ALG\_24109\_replaced([11158675](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktEDG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if CLPC for SRS is enabled for this UE.

If (NRBTS/NRCELL/actUlClosedLoopPwrCtrl is puschSrs or pucchPuschSrs) [05602058] AND [actSeparateSrsCLPC (in cell configuration) equals to False], [End 05602058] then CLPC for SRS is enabled for UEs that have SRS for wideband BF.

[CB015640-A] P0\_SRS, calculated based on NIDD:p0NominalSrs, shall be received by gNB-DU(UPlane) from gNB-DU(CPlane). [End CB015640-A]

For TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 UL CA UE, only if transmission buffer in UL is not split between PCell and SCell (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10377\_replaced([11122349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqfQNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PHR report based on a reference format is used to calculate the downlink pathloss PL on SCell (see [11121669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqZwrfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

Note: P\_SRS for powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10497\_replaced([11119432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is not changed.

Note: SW also adds TPC of RAR to accumulated TPC here but it does not matters much so it is left unchanged.

Note: Accumulated δ\_srs shall not be reset on SCell after SCell is deactivated.

Note: POWER\_HEADROOM\_63 can be reported easy for PHR report based on a reference format (see [11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for the reason). Since POWER\_HEADROOM\_63 corresponds to PH>=38 according to chapter 10.1.17 of 38.133, downlink pathloss is not accurate, in case POWER\_HEADROOM\_63 is reported in PHR report based on a reference format.

2. Calculate P\_SRS\_SB\_BF  [CB015640-A] as P\_SRS in step 1 [End CB015640-A] with replacing [CB015640-A] P0\_SRS with P0\_SRS\_SB\_BF, [End CB015640-A] n\_prb\_srs with the number of SRS PRB for SB BF n\_prb\_sb\_bf and rrmAdjustedAccumulatedTpcPE is 0. Because CLPC for SRS for SB BF is disabled always;

[CB015640-A] P0\_SRS\_SB\_BF, calculated based on NIDD:p0NominalSrsSbBf, shall be received by gNB-DU(UPlane) from gNB-DU(CPlane). [End CB015640-A]

NOTE: due to supporting SB SRS for SB BF, the value of n\_prb\_sb\_bf may differ from the respective number of WB SRS.

3. Calculate POWER\_DIFF = P\_SRS\_SB\_BF - P\_SRS;

4. SB\_BF\_SRS\_EPRE = WB\_BF\_SRS\_EPRE + POWER\_DIFF - 10Log (n\_prb\_sb\_bf/n\_prb\_srs) +deltaComb, where WB\_BF\_SRS\_EPRE is SRS\_EPRE. If comb for WB BF is comb2 while comb for SB BF is comb4, deltaComb = +3dB; If comb for WB BF is comb4 while comb for SB BF is comb2, deltaComb = -3dB. The else case deltaComb=0.

For UEs under SB\_BF\_CONF **(5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

The SB\_BF\_SRS\_EPRE shall be SRS\_EPRE from CoMa.

Note: the SRS power estimated is not accurate for the following reasons:

1) UE’s Pmax may change (UE may support Maximum Power Reduction) but gNB is not aware of this.

2) accumulated TPC is not the same between gNB and UE because even some TPC is non-DTX PUSCH TPC but UE may ignore it for some reason. There is also no clear definition whether UE would reset accumulated TPC of PUSCH when SRS is reconfigured, while based on current CLPC solution, the two physical channel adopts the same accumulated TPC.

Note: SRS power estimated via CoMa and real SRS signal may have gap because CoMa include H-V combine and the gain of H-V combine depends on number of TRX columns and rows, UE's SRS channel estimation result.

---

##### 3.18.5.2.0-5 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Correlation averaging of SRS for SB BF (ID: 11157124)

**3.18.5.2.0-5.0-5**  (ID: `13429029`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
If NRBTS/NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch/channelStabilityThreshold >0: 5G-L2-PS shall keep a filter for the instant correlation of channel estimation metric (Cinst\_p , 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21789\_replaced([11107408](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kofFFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), p = 0~3 for the 4 ports of TAS SRS) received from L1 for a UE, the averaged correlation Cavg shall be calculated as below:

Cavg has initial value as 1.

set the UE as earlyWbSrs status.

**For the case of eCPRI 7-2e:**

Cinst is the averaged correlation value among SRS ports which meet below conditions in current L1 Radio report. If no any SRS port can be selected, use the correlation value of SRS port with the highest port power in current L1 Radio report.

- The SRS port is not reported as DTX, and

- The SRS port is not reported as high interference, and

- Correlation value of SRS port is higher than 0.

**For the case of eCPRI 7-2a:**

Cinst is the calculated according to below steps.

**{**

**1) Validity of C**inst\_p **:**\*\*\*\*

* If measurement gap is set up for a UE and some of SRS occurrence is impacted according to criterion 1 of SB BF UE with gap impact (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27388\_replaced([11156732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), correlation for this UE is invalid until gap is released.
* If Cinst\_p is invalid value or part of the twice 4 ports of SRS used for correlation calculation is invalid or all ports has Cinst\_p = 0:

-- 5G-L2-PS shall consider the correlation report of this time is invalid and not update average correlation. Part of the twice 4 ports of SRS used for correlation calculation can be invalid due to new SRS configuration, measurement gap release and etc.

* else

{

-- Decide port power and conditional port SINR shall be used:

If NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsSinrThreshold = rrmMinWbSrsSinr, SINR measurement is disabled, port power shall be used for SRS port validation and downgrading;

else if NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsSinrThreshold > rrmMinWbSrsSinr: SINR measurement is enabled, port SINR and port power shall be used for SRS port validation, SINR shall be used for downgrading. Detail refer to L1: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13935\_replaced([11107463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kofsJfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

-- a) If Cinst\_p is invalid value or reported the first time after SRS of SB BF decoding started to be indicated by 5G-L2-PS for a UE then 5G-L2-PS shall discard this Cinst\_p. **0 is also considered as invalid. N1 ports are left as valid.**

-- b) 5G-L2-PS shall select first N2 = min {N1, number of BWV from L1} Cinst\_p with conditional power or SINR sorted from high to low; Rationale: here only select the port that contribute to BWV. If SINR estimation is enabled, SINR shall be used for sorting and downgrading.

-- c) If a port within N2 has power lower than NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsPowerThreshold or conditional SINR **lower than NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsSinrThreshold is SINR is enabled ,**

5G-L2-PS shall discard this Cinst\_p. N3 ports are left.

-- d) further discard the port Cinst\_p from N3, if Cinst\_p/Cinst\_temp\_avg\_N3 <1/5 where Cinst\_temp\_avg\_N3 is averaged Cinst\_p within N3 ports;

- If there is no valid port left, 5G-L2-PS shall select a Cinst\_p with highest port power or SINR from N1. N3 is 1 in this case.

**}**

**2) Average C**inst\_p **within valid N3 ports to C**inst **;*****\****\*

**}**

After valid Cins is calculated, it shall be filtered according to below algorithm:

* If the number of to-be-averaged correlation (Cinst) is less than or equal to **rdNumWbSrsMeas (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21819\_replaced([11158332](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktBm1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

{

-- Cavg shall be the arithmetic average of all already received Cinst;

}

* Else

{

-- Cavg (t) = (1-rrmDlSrsMeasFilterCoefficient) \* Cavg (t-1) + rrmDlSrsMeasFilterCoefficient \* Cinst;

where rrmDlSrsMeasFilterCoefficient = 1/**rdNumWbSrsMeas**

* remove **earlyWbSrs status;**

}

Timer **rdWbSrsCorrExpiry shall be set up when UE has SB BF release RRC complete received and stop when UE has SB BF configuration RRC complete.**

earlyWbSrs status shall be removed when SB BF is released.

If NRBTS/NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch/enableSbSrsVolatilityCheck **is false:**

{

- If the timer **rdWbSrsCorrExpiry (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21824\_replaced([11158342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktBm1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expired or**

- when SRS configuration state machine is set up.

-- Cavg = 1

}

Note1: Only UEs under **SB\_BF\_CONF, can receive Cinst\_p.**

if NRBTS/NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch/enableSbSrsVolatilityCheck is false: **Cavg is initial value 1 when a UE receives WB BF for the first time. Cavg is not reset when SB BF is release or WB BF is configured later but is kept for rdWbSrsCorrExpiry time length.**

elseif NRBTS/NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch/enableSbSrsVolatilityCheck is true: Cavg is initial value 1 when a UE receives SB BF Configuration. When SB BF is release or WB BF is configured later, the filtered-averaged SB CoMa correlation metric (rrmSbComaCorrMetric\_final, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22747\_replaced([11157270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks6SGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value is kept same as averaged correlation metric value (Cavg, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21817\_replaced([11157124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) until the timer rdWbSrsCorrExpiry is not expired or not enough number of SB CoMa correlation metric calculations are done.

For:

* TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 [CB014067-B], or
* FR1 TDD + TDD + FDD (with intra-band contiguous TDD CCs with TDD PCell) [End CB014067-B]

UL CA UE, after [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell is deactivated, gNB-DU shall not stop the timer rdWbSrsCorrExpiry if the timer rdWbSrsCorrExpiry is running on [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell.

---

##### 3.18.5.2.0-6 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation SINR averaging of SRS for SB BF (ID: 11157155)

**3.18.5.2.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `12819440`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
For UEs under **SB\_BF\_CONF, if SINR measurement is enabled via NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsSinrThreshold > rrmMinWbSrsSinr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14919\_replaced([11107414](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kofFF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall keep a filter for the instant SINR (SINRinst\_p , 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14919\_replaced([11107414](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kofFF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),**

p = 0~3 for the 4 ports of TAS SRS) received from L1 for a UE, the averaged SINR (SINRavg) shall be:

SINRavg has initial value as 40dB.

earlyWbSrsSinr status shall be set when SB BF is configured to UE and SINR measurement is enabled.

**For the case of eCPRI 7-2e:**

SINRinst is the averaged linear SINR value among SRS ports which meet below conditions in current L1 Radio report. If reported SINR value per port is lower than rrmMinWbSrsSinr, use the value of rrmMinWbSrsSinr. If no any SRS port can be selected, use the SINR value of port with the highest port power in current L1 Radio report.

- The SRS port is not reported as DTX, and

- The SRS port is not reported as high interference.

- [PR853440] SRS port has valid SINR value. NOTE: Invalid SINR value per port shall be discarded and not update averaged SINR value. [End PR853440]

**For the case of eCPRI 7-2a:**

SINRinst is calculated according to below steps**:**

**{**

**1) Validity of SINR**inst\_p **:**\*\*\*\*

- Define rrmMinWbSrsSinr as -40 dB.

- If all SRS ports have invalid value or If criterion 1 of SB BF UE with measurement gap impact (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27388\_replaced([11156732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is met:

-- 5G-L2-PS shall consider the SINR report of this time is invalid and not update average SINR.

- else

{

-- a) If SINRinst\_p is invalid value, then 5G-L2-PS shall discard this SINRinst\_p. N1 ports are left as valid.

-- b) If the SINRinst\_p  is lower than rrmMinWbSrsSinr or the port p has power lower than -140dBm,  5G-L2-PS shall set SINRinst\_p to rrmMinWbSrsSinr.

-- c) 5G-L2-PS shall select first N2 = min {N1, number of BWV from L1} SINRinst\_p with SINRinst\_p sorted from high to low; Rationale: here only select the port that contribute to BWV. N2 ports are left as valid.

-- if there is no valid port left, 5G-L2-PS shall select a SINRinst\_p with highest port power from N1.

}

**2) Average SINR**inst\_p **within valid ports to SINR**inst **;*****\****\*

* Convert SINRinst\_p to linear values if they are not.
* Average SINRinst\_p within valid ports to SINRinst.

**}**

After valid SINRinst is calculated, it shall be filtered according to below algorithm:

* If the number of to-be-averaged SINRinst is less than or equal to **rdNumWbSrsMeas (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21819\_replaced([11158332](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktBm1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). (Note: here the same rd parameters for filter of correlation and SINR is adopted and the possibility of different filters can be defined later if needed.)**

{

-- SINRavg shall be the arithmetic average of all already received SINRinst;

}

* Else

{

-- SINRavg (t) = (1-rrmDlSrsMeasFilterCoefficient ) \* SINRavg (t-1) + rrmDlSrsMeasFilterCoefficient \* SINRinst;

where rrmDlSrsMeasFilterCoefficient = 1/**rdNumWbSrsMeas**

-- remove **earlyWbSrsSinr status;**

}

* convert SINRavg to dB for threshold comparation.

earlyWbSrsSinr status shall be removed when SB BF is released.
