##### 3.18.5.2.0-7 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Subband CoMa correlation metric (ID: 11157172)

**3.18.5.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11157178`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
Subband CoMa correlation metric estimation and averaging

---

**3.18.5.2.0-7.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13477908`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
13477908:
Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
If NRBTS/NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch/enableSbSrsVolatilityCheck is true or **rdIncludeSrsVolatilityStatusMetric (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23159\_replaced([11158466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktCN_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** is true:\*\*\*\*

Channel volatility of a UE under WB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21334\_replaced([11156985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is evaluated by using SB CoMa Correlation metric (rrmSbCoMaCorrMetric\_final).

[CB015122-H]

If NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

Channel volatility shall not be evaluated on SCell if it's deactivated.

The calculation of instantaneous SB CoMa correlation metric and its validity check has been moved to L1, [11155895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

For every time duration (WB BF SRS periodicity \* number of SRS subbands) L2-PS shall requests to L1-DU to calculate rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric(p,n) and rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric(p,n) indicating s\_id.

where:

n is the time index corresponding to occurrence of the UEs SRS subband ‘s\_id’ resource. Such that, time duration between n and n-1 time indices is (SRS periodicity \* number of SRS subbands).

s\_id is the index of the selected SRS subband, where one SRS subband is selected for one UE for the SB CoMa correlation metric computation.

The SRS subband s\_id can be selected randomly but need to be same for one UE when the UE is configured with subband SRS. The random selection of SRS subband can be done such that the SB CoMa correlation metric calculation for the subband SRS UEs shall be uniformly distributed over the time duration (WB BF SRS periodicity \* number of SRS subbands), which reduces the impacts on 5G-L2-PS processing capacity.

SRS periodicity and number of SRS subbands shall be determined from PeriodictyandOffset, B\_srs and C\_srs in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2147\_replaced([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

L2-PS receives from L1-DU the values for rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric(p,n) and rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric(p,n).

else

[End CB015122-H]

5G-L2-PS shall use valid SRS covariance matrices (horizontal CoMa (H\_CoMa) and vertical CoMa (V\_CoMa), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6982\_replaced([11155852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to estimate subband channel correlation. Channel volatility shall not be evaluated on SCell if it's deactivated.

The instantaneous SB CoMa correlation metric at n is calculated for SRS port (pi) corresponding to selected SRS subband s\_id for H\_CoMa and V\_CoMa as below:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a stylized font. The formula defines a metric called "rrmSbHComaCorrMetric" which takes three arguments: "pi", "s\_id", and "n".
The formula is:
rrmSbHComaCorrMetric(pi,s\_id,n) = |(Vec\_H\_CoMa(pi,s\_id,n-1) \* (Vec\_H\_CoMa(pi, s\_id,n)^H))| / (||Vec\_H\_CoMa(pi, s\_id,n-1)||₂ \* ||Vec\_H\_CoMa(pi,s\_id,n) ||₂)
Here's a breakdown of the components:
\* `rrmSbHComaCorrMetric(pi,s_id,n)`: This is the name of the metric being defined, with parameters `pi`, `s_id`, and `n`.
\* `=`: The equals sign indicates the definition of the metric.
\* `| ... |`: The vertical bars denote the absolute value or magnitude of the expression within.
\* `Vec_H_CoMa(pi,s_id,n-1)`: This appears to be a vector or a matrix related to the parameters `pi`, `s_id`, and `n-1`.
\* `*`: The asterisk likely represents multiplication.
\* `(Vec_H_CoMa(pi, s_id,n)^H)`: This is the conjugate transpose (Hermitian transpose) of the `Vec_H_CoMa` vector/matrix with parameters `pi`, `s_id`, and `n`.
\* `|| ... ||₂`: The double vertical bars with a subscript '2' denote the L2 norm (Euclidean norm) of the vector/matrix.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10528.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a sans-serif font. The formula defines a metric called "rrmSbVComaCorrMetric" which takes three arguments: "pi", "s\_id", and "n".
The formula is expressed as a fraction:
The numerator is the absolute value of the product of two terms:
1. `Vec_V_CoMa(pi, s_id, n-1)`
2. `Vec_V_CoMa(pi, s_id, n)^H` (where `^H` likely denotes the conjugate transpose or Hermitian transpose)
The denominator is the product of the L2 norms of two terms:
1. `||Vec_V_CoMa(pi, s_id, n-1)||2`
2. `||Vec_V_CoMa(pi, s_id, n)||2`
The formula is presented with an equals sign preceding the fraction, indicating that "rrmSbVComaCorrMetric(pi, s\_id, n)" is defined by this expression.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10528.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

pi represents SRS port allocated to UE for periodic SRS, pi=0,…,Pi-1.

Pi is the number of SRS ports allocated to the UE for periodic srs (Pi = 2 for codebook SRS configuration, Pi = 4 for TAS SRS configuration).

s\_id is the index of the selected SRS subband (only one SRS subband is selected for one UE for the estimation computation).

Vec(A) is the vectorization function whose output is a vector which is computed by vectorizing the element of matrix A.

Vec\_H\_CoMa(pi,s\_id,n) is the Vec(H\_CoMa(pi,s\_id,n)). H\_CoMa(pi,s\_id,n) is horizontal CoMa defined as Cov\_pi(H) in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6991\_replaced([11155895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) at n corresponding to the SRS subband s\_id and averaged over the antenna polarizations for each port 'pi'.

Vec\_V\_CoMa(pi,s\_id,n) is the Vec(V\_CoMa(pi,s\_id,n)). V\_CoMa(pi,s\_id,n) is vertical CoMa defined as Cov\_pi(V) in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6991\_replaced([11155895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) at n corresponding to the SRS subband s\_id and averaged over the antenna polarizations for each port 'pi'.

Here, Vec(A) is the vectorization function whose output is a row vector which is obtained by stacking the columns/rows of the matrix A on top of one another.

|.| - Absolute value; ||.||2  - Euclidean norm.

**Validity of the metric:**

If H\_CoMA and V\_CoMa corresponding to selected SRS subband s\_id for a SRS port (pi) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6991\_replaced([11155895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not valid for SB correlation metric (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2165\_replaced([11154516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kssPr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at n and n-1, then rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric(pi)/ rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric(pi) is discarded.

[CB015122-H]

end

[End CB015122-H]

**Averaging:**

5G-L2-PS shall calculate the averaged SB CoMa correlation metric at n over the valid SRS ports (p) for the selected SRS subband (s\_id):

If P = 0 (No SRS ports with valid H\_CoMa and V\_CoMa for DL):

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "rrrmSbHCoCorrMetric\_avg(n) = 0". The text is in a light color against a white background, with a black border at the bottom.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10528.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2].

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "rrrnSbVCoMaCorrMetric\_avg(n) = 0". The text is in a light color against a white background, with a black border at the bottom. The letters are slightly blurred, but legible.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10528.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3].

else:

[image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric\_avg(n) = \frac{1}{P} \sum\_{p} rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric(p, n)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10528.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]

[image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
`rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric_avg(n) = 1/p * sum(rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric(p, n))`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10528.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]

p represents SRS port allocated to UE for periodic SRS with valid H\_CoMa and V\_CoMa for DL.

P is the number of SRS ports allocated to the UE for periodic SRS with valid H\_CoMa and V\_CoMa for DL.

[CB015122-H]

If NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 0

For UE under WB\_BF\_CONF, 5G-L2-PS need to store both SRS covariance matrices (horizontal CoMa and vertical CoMa, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6982\_replaced([11155852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksyWQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at n and n-1 for each SRS port corresponding to the selected SRS subband s\_id for the subband CoMa correlation metric calculation. Here, n and n-1 are the time indexes (defining the time duration) between the consecutive H\_CoMa and V\_CoMa corresponding to the SRS subband ‘s\_id’, which is (SRS periodicity \* number of SRS subbands). SRS periodicity and number of SRS subbands shall be determined from PeriodictyandOffset, B\_srs and C\_srs in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2147\_replaced([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The SRS subband s\_id can be selected randomly but need to be same for one UE when the UE is configured with subband SRS. The random selection of SRS subband can be done such that the SB CoMa correlation metric calculation for the subband SRS UEs shall be uniformly distributed over the time duration (SRS periodicity \* number of SRS subbands), which reduces the impacts on 5G-L2-PS processing capacity.

end

[End CB015122]

Note: Setting rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric\_avg(n)/ rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric\_avg(n) equal to zero will result in not considering this UE for SB BF if the number of times CoMa corresponding to all the SRS ports are invalid makes the correlation metric below the threshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note:  SB CoMa correlation metric calculation may be restricted for some UEs for some slots if the cell is overload and 5G-L2-PS reaches its processing capacity limit.

---

**3.18.5.2.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11157270`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
Filtering the averaged subband CoMa correlation metric

---

**3.18.5.2.0-7.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13429030`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
13429030:
Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
If NRBTS/NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch/enableSbSrsVolatilityCheck is true or **rdIncludeSrsVolatilityStatusMetric (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23159\_replaced([11158466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktCN_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** is true:\*\*\*\*

5G-L2-PS shall keep separate filters for both rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric\_avg/ rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric\_avg metrics corresponding to the SRS subband s\_id for each UE (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22743\_replaced([11157178](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks6SFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

--If the number of averaged SB CoMa correlation metric (rrmSbVComaCorrMetric\_avg/ rrmSbHComaCorrMetric\_avg) calculated is less than or equal to **rdNumSbSrsCorrCal (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22749\_replaced([11158539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktC0-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric\_filtered shall be the arithmetic average of all already calculated rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric\_avg.

rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric\_filtered shall be the arithmetic average of all already calculated rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric\_avg.

if **rdWbSrsCorrExpiry (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21824\_replaced([11158342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktBm1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is running and not expired:**

rrmSbComaCorrMetric\_final(n) = Cavg (Rational: filtered-averaged SB CoMa correlation metric value is kept same as averaged WB correlation metric value (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21817\_replaced([11157124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) until the timer **rdWbSrsCorrExpiry is not expired and not enough number of SB CoMa correlation metric calculations are done).**

else

The filtered-averaged SB correlation metric, rrmSbComaCorrMetric\_final(n) = 1 (Rational: UE will be considered as low volatile UE in RLQ monitoring (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) until enough number of SB CoMa correlation metric calculations are done)

--else

{

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a sans-serif font. The formula defines a recursive relationship for a variable named `rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric_filtered(n)`.
The formula is as follows:
`rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric_filtered(n) = (1 - rrmSbCorrFilterCoeff) * rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric_filtered(n-1) + rrmSbCorrFilterCoeff * rrmSbHComaCorrMetric_avg(n)`
This formula indicates that the filtered metric at step `n` is a weighted average of the filtered metric at the previous step (`n-1`) and the average metric at the current step (`n`). The weights are determined by `rrmSbCorrFilterCoeff`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10532.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a sans-serif font. The formula defines a recursive relationship for a variable named `rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric_filtered(n)`.
The formula is as follows:
`rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric_filtered(n) = (1 - rrmSbCorrFilterCoeff) * rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric_filtered(n - 1) + rrmSbCorrFilterCoeff * rrmSbVComaCorrMetric_avg(n)`
This formula appears to represent a filtered version of a metric, likely calculated using a weighted average of its previous filtered value and a current average value. The `rrmSbCorrFilterCoeff` likely represents a filter coefficient that controls the smoothing effect.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10532.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a sans-serif font. The equation is:
`rrmSbCorrFilterCoeff = 1 / rdNumSbSrsCorrCal`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10532.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$$ \text{rrmSbCoMaCorrMetric\_final(n)} = \sqrt{\text{rrmSbHCoMaCorrMetric\_filtered(n)} \* \text{rrmSbVCoMaCorrMetric\_filtered(n)}} $$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10532.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

5G-L2-PS shall stop the **rdWbSrsCorrExpiry timer.**

}

For:  
- TDD FR1 + TDD [CB014067-B], or   
- FR1 TDD + TDD + FDD (with intra-band contiguous TDD CCs with TDD PCell) [End CB014067-B]   
FR1 UL CA UE, the number of averaged SB CoMa correlation metric shall be reset to 0 on [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell after SCell is deactivated.

Note: SB Correaltion Metric is calculated for the UE under WB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21334\_replaced([11156985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

##### 3.18.5.2.0-8 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Monitor DL traffic scheduled PRB (ID: 11157336)

**3.18.5.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11157342`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
Monitor scheduled PRB

---

**3.18.5.2.0-8.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `13429031`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
For each rrmPeriodSrsCheck (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21345\_replaced([11157044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

5G-L2-PS shall calculate the averaged scheduled PRB ratio for a UE over all the slots within rrmPeriodSrsCheck that are capable for normal PDSCH scheduling (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2373\_replaced([11115215](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpr--_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Where,

scheduled PRB ratio is the ratio of the number of scheduled PRB for this UE to all available PRBs for normal PDSCH schedule.

Normal PDSCH are PDSCH exclude common channels as SIBx, paging, Msg2, Msg4 **and RBGs with at least one blanked PRB.**

If all slots within the rrmPeriodSrsCheck not available for normal PDSCH scheduling or if some slots within the rrmPeriodSrsCheck are skipped due to measurement gap, then 5G-L2-PS shall consider the check is invalid.

Else

{

* If the number available PRBs for normal PDSCH of one slot is 0 then that slot shall be excluded for averaging.
* 1) For UEs under **WB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21334\_replaced([11156985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): If averaged scheduled PRB ratio in percentage is higher than** rrmWbSrsPrbThreshold: Consider the sample as high PRB ratio sample;\*\*\*\*
* 2) For UEs under **SB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): If averaged scheduled PRB ratio in percentage is lower than** rrmSbSrsPrbThreshold: Consider the sample as low PRB ratio sample;\*\*\*\*

where rrmWbSrsPrbThreshold is NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/prbRatioThreshold, rrmSbSrsPrbThreshold is max {NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/prbRatioThreshold- NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/prbRatioHysteresis, 0}.

}

For:  
- TDD FR1 + TDD [CB014067-B], or

* FR1 TDD + TDD + FDD (with intra-band contiguous TDD CCs with TDD PCell) [End CB014067-B]  
  FR1 UL CA UE, if UE's DL buffer utilization (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4185\_replaced([11174341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) remains 0 on [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell throughout the rrmPeriodSrsCheck, then 5G-L2-PS shall consider that the check is valid and there is one low buffer sample for this rrmPeriodSrsCheck on [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell.

---

**3.18.5.2.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11157369`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
Monitor DL Buffer

---

**3.18.5.2.0-8.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12879951`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
**Conditional buffer criterion is enabled via: [Before CB015640-B] actEcpri72e = True and [End CB015640-B] subband BF is enabled and NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/dlBufferThreshold > 0.**

For each rrmPeriodSrsCheck (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21345\_replaced([11157044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

If buffer criterion is enabled, gNB-DU shall calculate DL buffer size dlBufferSize by calculating averaged overall DL buffer size, via received BSR message from L2-Low (excluding message with BSR = 0), of all DRBs configured to the UE within each rrmPeriodSrsCheck.

If dlBufferSize > dlBufferThreshold, the sample shall be a high buffer sample.

Elseif dlBufferSize =< max { 0.1 \* dlBufferThreshold, dlBufferThreshold - dlBufferHysteresis}, the sample shall be a low buffer sample.

Else: the sample shall not be a high or low buffer sample.

Each buffer check sample shall be valid, for UEs with no DRB configured the sample is treated as low buffer sample.

---

**3.18.5.2.0-8.0-3**  (ID: `11157379`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
DL traffic Decision

---

**3.18.5.2.0-8.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11157383`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
If buffer criterion is enabled:

* For UEs under **WB\_BF\_CONF or** SB\_BF\_CONF:\*\*\*\*

Each traffic check sample shall be valid since each buffer sample is valid.

If a sample is a high buffer **or high PRB ratio sample:**

the sample shall be a high DL traffic sample;

Elseif a sample is a low buffer **and low PRB ratio sample:**

the sample shall be a low DL traffic sample;

Else:

the sample is not high or low traffic sample.

~~This note will be deleted after review: there is no clear mapping relation to make sure the threshold NIDD parameter can avoid a sample meet high traffic and low traffic criteria at the same time, for example, a sample with high buffer but low PRB ratio, so here adopts 'if' and 'else if' to avoid the ambiguity.~~

else:

* Traffic sample validity is the same as high PRB ratio sample
* For UEs under **WB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21334\_replaced([11156985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): a high PRB ratio sample shall be a high DL traffic sample;**
* For UEs under **SB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): a low PRB ratio sample shall be a low DL traffic sample;**

---

##### 3.18.5.2.0-9 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Monitor radio link quality (ID: 11157389)

**3.18.5.2.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `11157399`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
[CB009527-A]

NOTE: to make requirement to be more generic, this requirement is revised by replacing names of WB SRS and SB SRS to SB BF and WB BF. PLEASE remove this NOTE when a new version is created.

[End CB009527-A]

For each rrmPeriodSrsCheck (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21345\_replaced([11157044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

If the LA is in earlyDllaMode mode as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11046\_replaced([11125506](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvH1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or there is no valid UL SRS power as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21401\_replaced([11157103](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or (for UEs under SB\_BF\_CONF, [Before CB011117-A] conditional correlation check is enabled via NRBTS/NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch/channelStabilityThreshold >0 [CB011117-A] conditional correlation check for SB BF UE is enabled [end CB011117-A]: averaged correlation is in earlyWbSrs status (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21817\_replaced([11157124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or [Before CB011117-A] Conditional SINR measurement is enabled via: NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsSinrThreshold > rrmMinWbSrsSinr [CB011117-A] conditional SINR is enabled [end CB011117-A]: averaged SINR is in earlyWbSrsSinr status (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22633\_replaced([11157155](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks6SEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), 5G-L2-PS shall consider this Radio Link Quality (RLQ) check is invalid;

Else,

{

1) For UEs under WB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21334\_replaced([11156985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* If spectral efficiency >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/seThreshold and rank >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/rankThreshold and UL SRS power >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/ wbSrsPowerThreshold

and conditional correlation check is enabled: averaged correlation  >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/channelStabilityThreshold:

Consider this sample as good radio link quality;

2) For UEs under SB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* If spectral efficiency < rrmSbSrsSeTreshold or rank < rrmSbSrsRankTresh or UL SRS power < rrmSbSrsQualTresh or conditional SINR is enabled: averaged SINR < rrmSbSrsSinrTresh  or  [Before CB011117-A] conditional correlation check is enabled [CB011117-A] conditional correlation check for SB BF UE is enabled [end CB011117-A]: averaged correlation < rrmSbSrsCorrTresh

Consider this sample as bad radio link quality;

* If averaged SINR is available, if UL SRS power >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/wbSrsPowerThreshold and averaged SINR < rrmSbSrsSinrTresh

Consider the sample as high interference.

where

* spectral efficiency is estimated as below:

ε = R*Qm*rank

where R and Qm are coding rate and modulation order from rrmProposedMcs (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3045\_replaced([11125301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqt5svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), rank is UE reported ones.

* rank for DL (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3165\_replaced([11139212](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlcZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has values 1,2,3,4;
* rrmSbSrsSeTreshold is max {NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/seThreshold – wbSbSrsSwitch/seHysteresis, 0};
* rrmSbSrsRankTresh is max {NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/rankTreshold - wbSbSrsSwitch/rankHysteresis, 1};
* rrmWbSrsQualTresh is NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch.wbSrsPowerThreshold;
* rrmSbSrsQualTresh is NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch.wbSrsPowerThreshold - NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch.wbSrsPowerHysteresis;
* rrmSbSrsCorrTresh = max {NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/channelStabilityThreshold - NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/channelStabilityHysteresis , 0}.
* conditional SINR is enabled: If NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsSinrThreshold > rrmMinWbSrsSinr  [CB011117-A]  and for UEs that criterion 2 of SB BF UE with measurement gap impact (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27388\_replaced([11156732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not met [End CB011117-A], SINR measurement for SB BF is enabled .
* If SINR estimation is enabled, rrmSbSrsSinrTresh is needed and is decided via NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsSinrThreshold + 2dB
* conditional correlation check is enabled: If NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch.channelStabilityThreshold> 0, correlation is checked for UEs with WB [Before CB011117-A] or SB  [end CB011117-A] BF configured.

[CB011117-A]

* conditional correlation check for SB BF UE is enabled:  If (NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch.channelStabilityThreshold> 0) and (criterion 1 of SB BF UE with measurement gap impact (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27388\_replaced([11156732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not met), correlation is checked for UEs with SB BF configured.

[end CB011117-A]

If NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch.channelStabilityThreshold > 0

{

If NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch/enableSbSrsVolatilityCheck is false:

averaged correlation is equal to averaged SRS correlation metric (Cavg in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21817\_replaced([11157124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

else if NRBTS/NRCELL/wbSbSrsSwitch/enableSbSrsVolatilityCheck is true:

For UEs under WB\_BF\_Conf, averaged correlation is equal to filtered-averaged SB CoMa correlation metric (rrmSbCoMaCorrMetric\_final in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22747\_replaced([11157270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks6SGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  
For UEs under SB\_BF\_Conf, averaged correlation is equal to averaged SRS correlation metric (Cavg in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21817\_replaced([11157124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

}

else

correlation related measurement shall not be checked for SB BF configured or release defined in this requirement.

}

##### 3.18.5.2.0-10 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Monitor HARQ NACK (ID: 11157405)

**3.18.5.2.0-10.0-2**  (ID: `11157415`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
For each rrmPeriodSrsCheck (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21345\_replaced([11157044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

For UEs under [Before CB009527-A] WB\_SRS\_CONF [CB009527-A] SB\_BF\_CONF [End CB009527-A] (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall add the times of PDSCH initial transmission that subband beam is used to rrmRtBeamNewTx and the times this kind of transmission receives HARQ NACK to rrmRtBeamNewTxNack.

##### 3.18.5.2.0-11 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Monitor subband BF performance (ID: 11157421)

**3.18.5.2.0-11.0-3**  (ID: `12876844`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
**[CB009527-A]**

**NOTE: to make requirement to be more generic, this requirement is revised by replacing names of WB SRS and SB SRS to SB BF and WB BF. PLEASE remove this NOTE when a new version is created.**

**[End CB009527-A]**

5G-L2-PS shall evaluate SB BF performance via below ways:

1) **[CB009527-A] For the case of eCPRI 7-2e, checks on BWV failure is not needed and UE is never at BWV failure status.** For the case of eCPRI 7-2a, [End CB009527-A] each UE that received SB BF configuration has initial state as not high percentage of BWV failure for this UE.\*\*\*\*

If NRCELL.srsForSubbandBm/actHoWithSbBf is true (enabled):

For every approximately **10 SRS periodicities that are not in measurement gap, gNB-DU shall count the BWV calculation failure times.**

Else:

5G-L2-PS shall count the BWV calculation failure times for approximately 10 continuous SRS periodicity.

If the failure times >= 4, 5G-L2-PS shall mark the UE as high percentage of BWV failure.

To simplify the solution, the counting is not via sliding window but set/reset the UE BWV failure status every approximately **10 SRS periodicity.**

5G-L2-PS may indicate additional BWV calculation within one SRS periodicity but shall only check the BWV failure or not here once.

Rationale: some threshold is not configured properly or the UE unfortunately is not under channel condition good enough for SB BF.

2) Each UE that received SB BF configuration has initial state as good SB BF performance.

If rdMonitorSe (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22981\_replaced([11158664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktEDGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not 0:

-  For UEs that have WB BF be reconfigured to SB BF, 5G-L2-PS shall monitor the SE before and after SB BF is configured.

SE\_WB\_BF is the latest SE before SB BF is configured. SB BF reconfigured to SB BF does not need this evaluation.

After SB BF is configured, SE\_SB\_BF is calculated based on UE reported rank and rrmProposedMcs (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3045\_replaced([11125301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqt5svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the slot after the second successful SB BF CSI report and near to the next CSI report. Rationale: to make sure the rank, CQI is reported based on UE's evaluation of SB BWVs and enough Olla correction at gNB side.

* For UEs with UE specific CSI-RS, define CSI report for channel acquisition based on CSI-RS that is transmitted via SB BWVs as SB BF CSI report.
* For UEs with cell specific CSI-RS, define CSI report after PDSCH transmitted via SB BWVs at least once as SB BF CSI report.  Note it is known CSI report at slot n is based on measurement before slot n-9 but here does not consider this for simplicity.

- If SE\_WB\_BF - SE\_SB\_BF > rdMonitorSe , 5G-L2-PS shall mark the UE as poor SB BF performance.

Note: If rdMonitorSe is not 0, poor SB BF performance UE will be SB BF constrained for a long time after SRS for SB BF is released as defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21380\_replaced([11157558](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8HSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: The absolute time for the monitor will get extended if there is SRS resource falls in measurement gap.

---

##### 3.18.5.2.0-12 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Monitor switch toggle (ID: 11157436)

**3.18.5.2.0-12.0-2**  (ID: `11157449`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
[CB009527-A]

NOTE: to make requirement to be more generic, this requirement is revised by replacing names of WB SRS and SB SRS to SB BF and WB BF. PLEASE remove this NOTE when a new version is created.

[End CB009527-A]

Each UE that received SB BF configuration has initial state as not SB WB BF Toggle.

5G-L2-PS shall 1) count the sucessfuly SB and WB BF Switch times for each UE within 30s. 2) counter the continuous SB and WB BF switch toggle times for each UE. Toggle is defined as: SRS for SB BF released is triggered at the time when rrmWbSrsReleaseProhibitTimer expires (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21380\_replaced([11157558](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8HSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If the successful switch is more than NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/maxWbSbSwitch times or continuous toggle is more than 3 times,

- 5G-L2-PS shall mark the UE as SB WB BF Toggle .

---

##### 3.18.5.2.0-13 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Evaluate UE’s status (ID: 11157453)

**3.18.5.2.0-13.0-3**  (ID: `11157471`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
1) For UEs under WB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21334\_replaced([11156985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): If number of valid [Before CB012971-A] buffer [CB012971-A] traffic [End CB012971-A] check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21353\_replaced([11157336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/numWbSrsConfigSample and number of valid Radio Link Quality (RLQ) check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/numWbSrsConfigSample,

-  [Before CB012971-A] rrmMetricBufferHi is the percentage of high buffer samples within this number of valid buffer check [CB012971-A] rrmMetricTrafficHi is the percentage of high traffic samples within this number of valid traffic check [End CB012971-A] (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21353\_replaced([11157336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

- rrmMetricRlqGood is the percentage of good RLQ samples within this number of valid RLQ check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

and reset the counters regarding [Before CB012971-A] buffer [CB012971-A] traffic [End CB012971-A]check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21353\_replaced([11157336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and RLQ check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for evaluation the next time.

2) For UEs under SB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): If number of valid buffer check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21353\_replaced([11157336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/numWbSrsReleaseSample and number of valid Radio Link Quality (RLQ) check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/numWbSrsReleaseSample (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21357\_replaced([11158231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktA_wfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

5G-L2-PS shall calculate the following metrics:

-  [Before CB012971-A] rrmMetricBufferLo is the percentage of Low buffer samples within this number of valid buffer check [CB012971-A] rrmMetricTrafficLo is the percentage of Low Traffic samples within this number of valid Traffic check [End CB012971-A] (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21353\_replaced([11157336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

- rrmMetricRlqBad is the percentage of bad RLQ samples within this number of valid RLQ check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

- rrmMetricInterferenceHi is the percentage of high interference samples within this number of valid RLQ check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

- rrmRtBeamNewTxNackRatio is the percentage of rrmRtBeamNewTxNack to rrmRtBeamNewTx (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22918\_replaced([11157405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65LfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB012971-A] - rrmMetricTrafficHi is the percentage of high traffic samples within this number of valid traffic check  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21353\_replaced([11157336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

- rrmMetricRlqGood is the percentage of good RLQ samples within this number of valid RLQ check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))); [End CB012971-A]

and reset the counters regarding [Before CB012971-A] buffer [CB012971-A] traffic [End CB012971-A]check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21353\_replaced([11157336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), RLQ check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and HARQ check for evaluation the next time.

Note: SW feedback for some special cases, when one of buffer and RLQ does not have enough samples while the other can have number of samples reachs the max allowed value of the SW, then SW reset the previous counters for simplicity.

Note: numWbSrsConfigSample or numWbSrsReleaseSample samples may be measured not continuously because of some invalid sample in between.

---

##### 3.18.5.2.0-14 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Evaluate UE channel volatility status (ID: 11157478)

**3.18.5.2.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `11157482`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
UE Channel volatility status overview

---

**3.18.5.2.0-14.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11157495`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
[CB009527-A]

NOTE: to make requirement to be more generic, this requirement is revised by replacing names of WB SRS and SB SRS to SB BF and WB BF. PLEASE remove this NOTE when a new version is created.

[End CB009527-A]

The channel volatility status of an UE is represented by rrmChannelVolatilityUeStatus.

rrmChannelvolatilityUeStatus = {earlySbSrsCorr; earlyWbSrsCorr; lowChannelVolatileUe;  highChannelVolatileUe}

earlySbSrsCorr: The volatility of the UE under WB\_BF\_CONF is not defined as not enough SB correlation measurements are available or rdIncludeSrsVolatilityStatusMetric (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23159\_replaced([11158466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktCN_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is false.

earlyWbSrsCorr: The volatility of the UE under SB\_BF\_CONF is not defined as not enough WB measurements are available or rdIncludeSrsVolatilityStatusMetric (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23159\_replaced([11158466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktCN_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is false.

lowChannelVolatileUe: The UE is considered to have low volatile radio channel.

highChannelVolatileUe: The UE is considered to have high volatile radio channel.

---

**3.18.5.2.0-14.0-2**  (ID: `11157500`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
Based on filtered-averaged subband CoMa correlation metric

---

**3.18.5.2.0-14.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13429033`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
IF **rdIncludeSrsVolatilityStatusMetric (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23159\_replaced([11158466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktCN_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** is true:\*\*\*\*

5G-L2-PS shall classify the UE under **WB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21334\_replaced([11156985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on the UE’s channel volatility. The channel volatility is evaluated based on filtered-averaged SB CoMa correlation metric (rrmSbComaCorrMetric\_final, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22747\_replaced([11157270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks6SGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The higher the SB CoMa correlation metric of the UE is, the lesser channel volatility of the UE is.**

IF the number of averaged SB CoMa correlation metric (rrmSbVComaCorrMetric\_avg/ rrmSbHComaCorrMetric\_avg, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22743\_replaced([11157178](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks6SFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) calculated is less than or equal to **rdNumSbSrsCorrCal (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22749\_replaced([11158539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktC0-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

If **rdWbSrsCorrExpiry (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21824\_replaced([11158342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktBm1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is running and not expired and current UE’s channel volatility status is not earlyWbSrsCorr:**

UE’s channel volatility status remains same (as defined using SRS correlation metric (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22754\_replaced([11157522](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8HQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))).

else

Set UE’s channel volatility status (rrmChannelVolatilityUeStatus, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23658\_replaced([11157482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as earlySbSrsCorr status.

ELSE IF filtered-averaged SB CoMa correlation metric >= **rdSbSrsVolatCorrThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22759\_replaced([11158550](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktC0_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

Set UE’s channel volatility status as lowChannelVolatileUe

ELSE IF filtered-averaged SB CoMa correlation metric < **rdSbSrsVolatCorrThreshold:**

Set UE’s channel volatility status as highChannelVolatileUe

ELSE:

IF UE is configured with WB BF for the first time in case of P(S)Cell or [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell is activated in case of [CB014067-B] TDD [End CB014067-B] SCell or current UE’s channel volatility status is earlyWbSrsCorr:

Set UE’s channel volatility status (rrmChannelVolatilityUeStatus, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23658\_replaced([11157482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as earlySbSrsCorr status.

Note: The channel volatility status of the UE under **WB\_BF\_CONF is set to earlySbSrsCorr when the current UE channel volatility status is earlyWbSrsCorr or when the UE configured with WB BF for the first time** or timer **rdWbSrsCorrExpiry (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21824\_replaced([11158342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktBm1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is expired. Otherwise, it is kept same to one defined using averaged SRS correlation metric for SB BF until enough measurements are available (number of valid SB CoMa correlation metric calculated greater than** rdNumSbSrsCorrCal (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22749\_replaced([11158539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktC0-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))).  
Note: In case of UE is reconfigured from WB BF to WB BF, the channel volatility status of the UE will be set as earlySbSrsCorr.***\****\*

---

**3.18.5.2.0-14.0-3**  (ID: `11157522`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
Based on averaged SRS correlation metric

---

**3.18.5.2.0-14.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `12876836`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
**[CB009527-A]**

**NOTE: to make requirement to be more generic, this requirement is revised by replacing names of WB SRS and SB SRS to SB BF and WB BF. PLEASE remove this NOTE when a new version is created.**

**[End CB009527-A]**

If **rdIncludeSrsVolatilityStatusMetric(5G\_UP\_ALG\_23159\_replaced([11158466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktCN_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** is true:\*\*\*\*

5G-L2-PS shall classify the UE under SB\_BF\_CONF **(5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on the UE’s channel volatility. The channel volatility is evaluated based on averaged SRS correlation metric (C\_avg in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21817\_replaced([11157124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The higher the averaged SRS correlation metric of the UE, the lesser channel volatility of the UE is.**

5G-L2-PS shall initial channel status as earlyWbSrsCorr after the UE has SB BF configured successfully.

If the number of to-be-averaged correlation (Cinst , 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21817\_replaced([11157124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is less than or equal to **rdNumWbSrsMeas (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21819\_replaced([11158332](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktBm1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or criterion 1 of SB BF UE with measurement gap impact (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27388\_replaced([11156732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is met:**

Set UE’s channel volatility status (rrmChannelVolatilityUeStatus, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23658\_replaced([11157482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as earlyWbSrsCorr status.

else if averaged SRS correlation metric >=  **rdWbSrsVolatCorrThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22762\_replaced([11158561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktDcAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

Set UE’s channel volatility status as lowChannelVolatileUe

else if averaged RS correlation metric < **rdWbSrsVolatCorrThreshold:**

Set UE’s channel volatility status as highChannelVolatileUe

else:

Set UE’s channel volatility status (rrmChannelVolatilityUeStatus, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23658\_replaced([11157482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as earlyWbSrsCorr status

Note: Volatility status from WB BF is not inherited to UE that are allocated with SB BF.

Note: When SB BF is released and WB BF is reconfigured, the UE’s channel volatility status remains the same as defined by SRS correlation metric until enough SB CoMa correlation metric calculations are done or **rdWbSrsCorrExpiry (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21824\_replaced([11158342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktBm1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) timer is expired.**

##### 3.18.5.2.0-15 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Check whether SB BF is recommended (ID: 11157541)

**3.18.5.2.0-15.0-2**  (ID: `13431411`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
[CB009527-A]

NOTE: to make requirement to be more generic, this requirement is revised by replacing names of WB SRS and SB SRS to SB BF and WB BF. PLEASE remove this NOTE when a new version is created.

[End CB009527-A]

For UEs under WB\_BF\_CONF,

If (rrmWbSrsConfigProhibitTimer expires) or (related metrics in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21376\_replaced([11157453](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are updated after rrmWbSrsConfigProhibitTimer expired):

If SB BF configuration criteria is met:

{

* If NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/sortingMetric is 0:

-- spectral efficiency (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be used as rrmSrsMetric;

* Else if NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/sortingMetric is 1:

-- WB SRS power (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21401\_replaced([11157103](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be used as rrmSrsMetric;

* Else

None.

* If rdIncludeHighVolatileUe (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23147\_replaced([11158437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktCN8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is true and rdIncludeSrsVolatilityStatusMetric (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23159\_replaced([11158466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktCN_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is true:

-- If the UE is lowChannelVolatileUe or earlySbSrsCorr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22751\_replaced([11157478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

rdLowChannelVolatilityPriorityBonus (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23145\_replaced([11158428](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktCN8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is added to the rrmSrsMetric. Rationale: neither spectral efficiency nor SRS power will have changing range larger than 100 so adding 100 can make sure UEs of lowChannelVolatileUe and earlySbSrsCorr have absolute higher priority than UEs of highChannelVolatileUe status.

* If the UE is not SPID UEs indicated by CPlane,

-- If rdSrsExcludeHighSe (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22623\_replaced([11158449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktCN9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 0:

5G-L2-PS shall remove the UE with spectral efficiency > rrmHighSe from waitingWbSrsUeList. Rationale: MorSe simulation shows that UEs that are already at rank4 and almost max MCS will not enjoy the benefit of subband BF so there are advices to exclude this kind of UE. By default, the functionality is disabled.

-- 5G-L2-PS shall maintain the UE's position in the sorted list waitingWbSrsUeList according to rrmSrsMetric.

* Else (SPID UEs)

--5G-L2-PS shall assign the UE with highest priority. Note more than one SPID UEs shall be supported.

}

Else:

{

* 5G-L2-PS shall remove the UE from waitingWbSrsUeList.

}

where SB BF configuration criteria: rrmMetricBufferHi >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/prbSampleHighLowPercentage and rrmMetricRlqGood >= wbSbSrsSwitch/rlqGoodPercentage and the UE is under SRS\_DL\_BM\_VALID and the UE is not 'WB SRS constraint UE' (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4349\_replaced([11177928](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuzIc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and channel volatile check for this UE succeeds.

If rdIncludeHighVolatileUe is false and UE is highChannelVolatileUe (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22751\_replaced([11157478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* the UE has channel volatile check failed

Else

* the UE has channel volatile check succeeded.

rrmHighSe is spectral efficiency of rank4 and MCS = maxMCS - rdSrsExcludeHighSe in the PDSCH MCS table that are configured to this UE, where maxMCS is the maximum MCS index excluding reserved MCS in the MCS table of this UE.

---

##### 3.18.5.2.0-16 Periodic Measurements and Evaluation Check whether WB BF is recommended (ID: 11157558)

**3.18.5.2.0-16.0-6**  (ID: `12880634`)

Periodic Measurements and Evaluation
For UEs under SB\_BF\_CONF,

* If {(rrmWbSrsReleaseProhibitTimer expires and related metrics in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21376\_replaced([11157453](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) meet the SB BF release criteria) or (related metrics in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21376\_replaced([11157453](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are updated and meet the SB BF release criteria after rrmWbSrsReleaseProhibitTimer expired) or (Unexpected cases in Note1 happens after rrmWbSrsReleaseProhibitTimer expired) or  Unexpected case for Scell happens } and (Additional DMRS configuration procedure is not ongoing):
* If DMRS reconfiguration procedure is complete, 5G-L2-PS shall inform Cplane to configure this UE to WB BF and restart rrmWbSrsReleaseProhibitTimer for this UE.

- If rrmMetricInterferenceHi >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/rlqBadPercentage or (UE has high percentage of BWV failure and latest UL SRS power >= rrmSbSrsQualTresh, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or UE has poor SB BF performance (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23655\_replaced([11157421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or UE is SB BF Toggle UE, 5G-L2-PS shall 1) start or restart rdWbSrsConstraintTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22551\_replaced([11158649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktEDE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for this UE, 2) mark the UE as "SB BF constraint UE". When rdWbSrsConstraintTimer expired, mark the UE as "Not SB BF constraint UE" flag.

- Reset interference counter and all measurement related to SB BF release evaluation

where SB BF release criteria are: If the below evaluation conditions are continuously met for rrmContinuousEvaluation times, the SB BF release criteria shall be considered as met. [Before CB015640-B] For eCPRI 7-2a, rrmContinuousEvaluation = 1. For eCPRI 7-2e, [End CB015640-B] rrmContinuousEvaluation = rdSbBfContinuousEvaluation (see [12539763: rdSbBfContinuousEvaluation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ms0n0yDTEfCNjfqfyUlvmw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

* rrmMetricTrafficLo (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21376\_replaced([11157453](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/prbSampleHighLowPercentage or rrmMetricRlqBad >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/rlqBadPercentage or rrmRtBeamNewTxNackRatio >= rdRtBeamHarqNackPercentage (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22923\_replaced([11158592](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktDcBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

where Unexpected case for Scell is: current serving cell is SCell and (current serving cell is deactivated or transform precoder is enabled according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3270\_replaced([11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) on PCell).

where Additional DMRS configuration procedure is not ongoing: (rrmNoAddDlDmrsReleaseProhibitTimer is not running) and (rrmNoAddDlDmrsConfigProhibitTimer is not running).

Note1: Unexpected cases are rdCqiExpiryTime (5G\_L2\_1026\_replaced([11184999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27u9ifvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expired or the rrmCoMaAgedTimer for DL BM expires (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6965\_replaced([11155684](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxII_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for UEs under SRS\_DL\_BM\_VALID status or UE has high percentage of BWV failure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23655\_replaced([11157421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks7gMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note2: It is known the performance monitor or Toggle or etc. that trigger rdWbSrsConstraintTimer is based on historical events and to reduce the complexity of system no aging scheme is designed for them. In customer network usually traffic does not continue very long. Due to asynchronization of measurement and SB BF release handling, it is possible the measurement/counter is higher than the threshold.

Note3: additional DL DMRS reconfiguration procedure is complete if DL DMRS RRC reconfiguration response is received or (DL DMRS RRC reconfiguration response is not received and the timers (rrmNoAddDlDmrsReleaseProhibitTimer and rrmNoAddDlDmrsConfigProhibitTimer) are not running).

---

#### 3.18.5.3 Inform Cplane for SB BF recommendation

##### 3.18.5.3.0-1 Inform Cplane for SB BF recommendation The list for UEs with SB BF is recommended (ID: 11157593)

**3.18.5.3.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13432362`)

Inform Cplane for SB BF recommendation
[CB014315-A]

The algorithm defined in this requirement is only valid when NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Basic'. When NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced', the switching algorithm is defined in [13432274: WB/SB BF switching algorithm (Enhanced)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Oc5CoB7HEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

[End CB014315-A]

If NRCELL/actDlSrsSubbandBm is true, the cell shall maintain the waitingWbSrsUeList for UEs meeting the criteria for SB BF configuration. The list has fixed length of rrmWaitingWbSrsUeListLengh UEs per cell. rrmWaitingWbSrsUeListLengh = 2\*maxNumUeSrs+5;

The list shall be initialized when cell is set up and shall be deleted when the cell is deleted. UEs that are deleted from the cell shall be removed from the list.

For TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 UL CA UE, UE shall be removed from the list on current serving cell in case SRS for SB BF is configured on the other serving cell or (current serving cell is SCell and (current serving cell is deactivated or transform precoder is enabled according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3270\_replaced([11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) on PCell)).

5G-L2-PS shall save the maximum number of UEs that can be configured for sub-band BF (maxNumUeSrs) that is indicated by Cplane at cell setup stage.

5G-L2-PS shall maintain the number of UEs that already have sub-band BF (rrmNumWbSrsUe) for current cell

Note: UE may also receive SRS that covers the whole BWP for wide band BF so the purpose of SRS should be indicated explicitly by Cplane for each UE.

---

##### 3.18.5.3.0-2 Inform Cplane for SB BF recommendation (ID: 11157614)

**3.18.5.3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13432366`)

Inform Cplane for SB BF recommendation
[CB014315-A]

The algorithm defined in this requirement is only valid when NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Basic'. When NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced', the switching algorithm is defined in [13432274: WB/SB BF switching algorithm (Enhanced)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Oc5CoB7HEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

[End CB014315-A]

5G-L2-PS shall communicate to Cplane periodically for SRS reconfiguration.

When the cell specific timer rdSrsToL3Timer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21393\_replaced([11158477](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktC08PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is expired, 5G-L2-PS shall firstly remove UEs (under state of "scheduled in large BWP" if UE has "BWP switch" state machine runs, defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1868\_replaced([11111144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLBkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from waitingWbSrsUeList. Secondly, select the (maxNumUeSrs- rrmNumWbSrsUe) UEs in waitingWbSrsUeList **as candidate for SB BF and remove these UEs from waitingWbSrsUeList and restart** rrmWbSrsConfigProhibitTimer for these UEs.\*\*\*\*

5G-L2-PS shall count the UE's SB BF recommendation **continuous rejection times. SB BF recommendation rejection is defined as: SB BF is recommended to L3 and does not receive SB BF configuration when** rrmWbSrsConfigProhibitTimer expires. When a UE has been rejected for 3 times **continuously, 5G-L2-PS shall 1) start or restart** rdWbSrsConstraintTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22551\_replaced([11158649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktEDE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for this UE, 2) mark the UE as "SB BF constraint UE", 3) reset rejection counter. When rdWbSrsConstraintTimer expired, mark the UE as "Not SB BF constraint UE".*****\****\*

5G-L2-PS shall reset the rejection counter whenever SB BF configuration is received.

Rationale: For some reasons cplane will always reject some UE's SB BF request and these UE will block other UEs be recommended for SB BF. For example, cplane only have 1T4R resource left in SB BF pool while the UE is 2T4R, so 1T4R UEs will always be rejected but for some time later, resource may be available.

Note: there may be some asynchronism status between 5G-L2-PS and L3, for example one UE is under RT SRS releasing procedure but 5G-L2-PS has not received it.

---

### 3.18.6 WB/SB BF switching algo (Enhanced)

#### 3.18.6.0-1 WB/SB BF switching algo (Enhanced) Overview of algorithm (ID: 13432373)

**3.18.6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13432629`)

WB/SB BF switching algo (Enhanced)
13432629:
WB/SB BF switching algo (Enhanced)
This requirement is valid when when NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo equals to ‘Enhanced’.

The state machine for SRS configuration is defined at [13458746: State machine for SRS configuration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1po1ri6DEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

gNB shall maintain two periodic tasks to switch UEs between SB and WB BF pools. One task is for switching WB BF UEs to SB BF. Another task is for switching SB BF UEs to WB BF. The periodicity of each task is configured via R&D parameter rdSbWbBfEvaluationPeriodicity ([13433542: rdSbWbBfEvaluationPeriodicity](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JFB41SEGEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). These two tasks have the same periodicity but with different slot offsets to avoid executing two tasks at the same time.

These two tasks shall NOT be executed in time critical path to avoid impact DL\UL scheduler.

The WB to SB BF switching task is defined at [13432377: Switch from WB to SB BF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9aqaRB7SEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

The SB to WB BF switching task is defined at [13432379: Switch from SB to WB BF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BEJpcR7TEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

In the below figure, it assumes rdSbWbBfEvaluationPeriodicity is 500 slots, the WB to SB BF switching task (blue) is triggered per 500 slots starting at slot n, the SB to WB SB switching task (green) is triggered per 500 slots starting at slot n + 250 (500/2).

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a timeline with five labeled slots: "Slot n", "Slot n + 250", "Slot n + 500", "Slot n + 750", and "Slot n + 1000". Above the timeline, there are five colored squares, each connected to its corresponding slot label by a dashed line. The squares at "Slot n", "Slot n + 500", and "Slot n + 1000" are blue. The squares at "Slot n + 250" and "Slot n + 750" are green. The timeline itself is a horizontal blue line with an arrow at the right end, indicating a progression in time.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-03131521.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

---

#### 3.18.6.1 State machine for SRS configuration

#### 3.18.6.1-1 State machine for SRS configuration

##### 3.18.6.1-1.0-1 State machine for SRS configuration The FWA UE means a UE which is configured with a DRB which has the tag of 'Static UE'. (ID: 13433948)

#### 3.18.6.1-2 State machine for SRS configuration

**3.18.6.1-2.0-1**  (ID: `13458426`)

State machine for SRS configuration
The maximum number BF switching from WB to SB or from SB to WB is defined in this requirement. This value is calculated based on L3 processing capacity and time window length for evaluating BF switching.

rrmMaxNumBfSwitch = FLOOR(rdMaxNumWbSbBfSwitchPerSecond/(2\*(2000/rdSbWbBfEvaluationPeriodicity))).

* rdMaxNumWbSbBfSwitchPerSecond is defined in [13433574: rdMaxNumWbSbBfSwitchPerSecond](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_WLva8SEHEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
* rdSbWbBfEvaluationPeriodicity is defined in [13433542: rdSbWbBfEvaluationPeriodicity](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JFB41SEGEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

---

#### 3.18.6.1-3 State machine for SRS configuration

**3.18.6.1-3.0-1**  (ID: `13433929`)

State machine for SRS configuration
This requirement is valid when when NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo equals to ‘Enhanced’.

The WB to SB BF switching task shall be executed periodically with the algorithm below:

1. Calculate the maximum number of switching from WB to SB BF using the formula rrmMaxNumWbToSbSwitch = MIN(rrmMaxNumBfSwitch, rrmRoomLeftSbBf).
2. The rrmMaxNumBfSwitch is defined in [13458425: Maximum number of BF switching](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_cWoE0y55EfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
3. rrmRoomLeftSbBf is value of NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/maxNumUeSrsOutput minus number of existing SB BF UEs.
4. If the number switching from WB to SB BF is lower than rrmMaxNumWbToSbSwitch, go to the next step. Otherwise, stop the loop.
5. Find the UE which has the highest averaged DL tput among candidates in WB BF pool which meet below conditions:
6. UE is under WB\_BF\_CONF state and evaluation status under this state is met. See [13458757: State of WB\_BF\_CONF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1po1uC6DEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
7. The average DL tput shall be higher than configured threshold. The average DL tput is calculated as number of payload bits, which is transmitted by PDSCH with HARQ initTx with osDFT (or tapered osDFT) beams in current evaluation window, divided by time duration of rdSbWbEvaluationPeriodicity. Its unit is kbits/s. For FWA UE, it shall be higher than NRCELL/wbSbBfSwitchEnh/dlTputThdForSbBfFwa. For other UE, it shall be higher than NRCELL/wbSbBfSwitchEnh/NIDD:dlTputThdForSbBf. About FWA UE, see definition in [13433927: About FWA UE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_B4s8lCEoEfGbZ5_vsUrUNw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), see definition in [13433927: About FWA UE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_B4s8lCEoEfGbZ5_vsUrUNw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
8. The DL spectral efficiency shall be higher than NRCELL/wbSbBfSwitchEnh/seThresholdForSbBf. The DL spectral efficiency is calculated as spectral efficiency (bits/Hz) times DL rank according to the latest CQI and rank in CSI report. See MCS index tables defined in 3GPP 38.214.
9. If the UE cannot be found, stop the loop.
10. Inform L3 to trigger RRC-reconfiguration message for the selected UE and increase number of switching.
11. Go to step 2.

NOTE: to avoid RRC-reconfiguration congestion, 5G-L2-PS shall try to request L3 to trigger RRC-reconfiguration messages in different DL slots.

Note: consider potential impact to L2 CPU usage, detail implementation and optimization leave to EFS.

---

#### 3.18.6.1-4 State machine for SRS configuration

**3.18.6.1-4.0-1**  (ID: `13433945`)

State machine for SRS configuration
This requirement is valid when when NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo equals to ‘Enhanced’.

The SB to WB BF switching task shall be executed periodically with the algorithm below.

1. Calculate rrmNumHighWaterLevel = FLOOR(rdHighWaterLevelSbBf \* NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/maxNumUeSrsOutput). The rdHighWaterLevelSbBf is defined at [13487747: rdHighWaterLevelSbBf](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_liX5T0LeEfGy8ZlFziQwLA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
2. If number of configured SB BF UEs (numConfiguredSbBFUes) is not higher than rrmNumHighWaterLevel, then skip below steps.
3. Calculate the maximum number of switch from SB to WB BF using the formula rrmMaxNumSbToWbSwitch = MIN(rrmMaxNumBfSwitch, rrmNumNonEligibleSbBf, numConfiguredSbBFUes - rrmNumHighWaterLevel).
4. The rrmMaxNumBfSwitch is defined in [13458425: Maximum number of BF switching](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_cWoE0y55EfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
5. rrmNumNonEligibleSbBf is number of non-eligible SB BF UEs which meet conditions defined at step 5.
6. If the number of switched UEs from SB to WB BF is lower than rrmMaxNumSbToWbSwitch, go to the next step. Otherwise, stop the loop.
7. Find the UE which has the lowest averaged DL tput among candidates in SB BF pool which meet below conditions:
8. UE is under SB\_BF\_CONF state and evaluation conditions under this state are met. See [13458764: State of SB\_BF\_CONF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1po1tC6DEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
9. The average DL tput is NOT higher than configured threshold. The average DL tput is calculated as number of payload bits, which is transmitted by PDSCH with HARQ initTx with RT beams (SVD, RZF or SVD-RZF) in current evaluation window, divided by time duration of rdSbWbEvaluationPeriodicity. Its unit is kbits/s. For FWA UE, it shall be NOT higher than NRCELL/wbSbBfSwitchEnh/dlTputThdForSbBfFwa. For other UE, it shall be NOT higher than NRCELL/wbSbBfSwitchEnh/NIDD:dlTputThdForSbBf.
10. If the UE cannot be found, stop the loop.
11. Inform L3 to trigger BF switch for the selected UE and increase number of switching.
12. Go to step 4.

NOTE: To avoid RRC-reconfiguration congestion, 5G-L2-PS shall try to request L3 to trigger RRC-reconfiguration messages in different DL slots.

Note: consider potential impact to L2 CPU usage, detail implementation and optimization leave to EFS.

---

##### 3.18.6.1.0-1 State machine for SRS configuration Overview of the states (ID: 13458747)

**3.18.6.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13458752`)

State machine for SRS configuration
The state machine defined in this chapter is only valid when NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced'. When NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm/subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Basic', the switching algorithm is defined in [11156930: WB/SB BF switching algorithm (Basic)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks4c5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

The state machine includes below states for managing SRS configuration switching from WB BF to SB BF or vice versa:

·    State of **SRS\_TRANS is defined in [13458753: State of SRS\_TRANS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1po1tS6DEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9);**

·    State of **WB\_BF\_CONF is defined in [13458757: State of WB\_BF\_CONF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1po1uC6DEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9);**

·    State of **SB\_BF\_CONF is defined in [13458764: State of SB\_BF\_CONF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1po1tC6DEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9);**

5G-L2-PS shall maintain this state machine per cell for any UE which meets below conditions:

·    SRS based DL WB BF is configured and UE has capacity of 4R TAS SRS resources for current serving cell, OR

·    SRS based DL SB BF is configured for current serving cell.

---

##### 3.18.6.1.0-2 State machine for SRS configuration State of SRS_TRANS (ID: 13458753)

**3.18.6.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13458756`)

State machine for SRS configuration
It's the state for UE when the SRS configuration is modified and until its activation ([11153999: Modification of SRS configuration and activation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)):

When enters this state:

* Stop the timer NIDD:switchProhibitTimerSbToWb and NIDD:switchProhibitTimerWbToSb.
* 5G-L2-PS shall save newly received SRS configuration.

Under this state:

* When the configuration for DL SB BF is activated (see [11153999: Modification of SRS configuration and activation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), switch to **SB\_BF\_CONF.**
* When the configuration for DL WB BF is activated (see [11153999: Modification of SRS configuration and activation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), switch to **WB\_BF\_CONF.**
* If gNB-CU rejects the reconfiguration, gNB-DU shall roll back the previous SRS configuration before RRC Reconfiguration. Note: this roll back indication may be included in User modify messages and the details depends on CP3 design.

---

##### 3.18.6.1.0-3 State machine for SRS configuration State of WB_BF_CONF (ID: 13458757)

**3.18.6.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13458763`)

State machine for SRS configuration
It's the state for UE which is configured with SRS based DL WB BF on current serving cell.

When enters this state:

* Start/restart the timer of NIDD:switchProhibitTimerWbToSb.

Under this state:

* When 5G-L2-PS receives user setup / modification request to update SRS resource for DL BF, switch to **SRS\_TRANS.**
* When DL WB BF is released and no SRS resource configured anymore by L3 on current, 5G-L2-PS shall stop maintaining the state machine.
* 5G-L2-PS shall evaluate UE for switching from WB to SB BF ([13432377: Switch from WB to SB BF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9aqaRB7SEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) if below evaluation conditions are met:

{

[CB014315-C]

- The serving cell is not under power saving mode ([11118320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqB9PfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and

- The serving cell is not under remote interference mitigation scheme ([11163373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and

- The serving cell is not additional UL mitigation for RIM RS detection ([11162042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-APvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and

- UE has "BWP switch" state machine runs and BWP status as "scheduled in large BWP", and

- UE is scheduled in large BWP without DCI-based switch procedure ongoing ([11111144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLBkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and

[End CB014315-C]

- The timer MAX(rdSbWbBfEvaluationPeriodicity, NIDD:switchProhibitTimerWbToSb) is expired. See [13433542: rdSbWbBfEvaluationPeriodicity](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JFB41SEGEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

-  UE capability supports 1T4R and 2T4R, and

- If rdDisableSbBfVoNR = True, UE is NOT configured with VoNR bearer in current cell.

}

---

##### 3.18.6.1.0-4 State machine for SRS configuration State of SB_BF_CONF (ID: 13458764)

**3.18.6.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13458770`)

State machine for SRS configuration
It's the state for UE which is configured with SRS based DL SB BF on current serving cell.

When enters this state:

* Start/restart the timer of NIDD:switchProhibitTimerSbToWb.

Under this state:

* When 5G-L2-PS receives user setup / modification request to update SRS resource for DL BF, switch to **SRS\_TRANS.**
* When DL SB BF is released and no SRS resource configured anymore by L3, 5G-L2-PS shall stop maintaining the state machine.
* 5G-L2-PS shall evaluate UE for switching from SB to WB BF ([13432379: Switch from SB to WB BF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BEJpcR7TEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) if below evaluation conditions are met:

{

- The timer MAX(rdSbWbBfEvaluationPeriodicity, NIDD:switchProhibitTimerSbToWb) is expired. See [13433542: rdSbWbBfEvaluationPeriodicity](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JFB41SEGEfG-foklaHnAaA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

}

## 3.18.7 Additional DMRS switching algo for SB BF

### 3.18.7.0-1 Additional DMRS switching algo for SB BF Overview and monitoring (ID: 11157635)

**3.18.7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11157640`)

Additional DMRS switching algo for SB BF
If **rrmNoAddDlDmrsSwitchEnabled (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = True:**

-If none of the conditions (cell and UE level) defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27685\_replaced([11157646](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uWvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met:

* gNB-DU shall monitor the channel correlation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21817\_replaced([11157124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for UEs under SB\_BF\_CONF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to remove the additional DMRS of UE with less channel volatility for throughput improvement (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27187\_replaced([11157656](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

-gNB-DU shall evaluate and decide for no additional DL DMRS configuration switch (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27285\_replaced([11157666](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

-If any one of the cell level conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27685\_replaced([11157646](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uWvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met: gNB-DU shall stop monitoring for additional DL DMRS switching (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27187\_replaced([11157656](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for SB BF UEs. When the serving cell come out of above status, gNB-DU shall start monitoring and evaluation for all UEs that shall be monitored.

-If any of the UE level conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27685\_replaced([11157646](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uWvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met: gNB-DU shall stop monitoring for additional DL DMRS switching (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27187\_replaced([11157656](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for this UE. When the UE level status related to the conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27685\_replaced([11157646](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uWvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are changed and none of the UE level conditions are met then gNB-DU shall start monitoring for additional DL DMRS switching (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27187\_replaced([11157656](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for this UE.

-5G-L2-PS shall mark the UE 'additional DL DMRS enabled SB BF UE' if Cplane configure the UE with original DL DMRS configuration **[PR795925] i.e; DL DMRS configured with additional DL DMRS** [End PR795925].\*\*\*\*

~~Note:~~The  SB BF release behaviour overwrites DMRS configuration switch behaviour. If SB BF release is triggered then gNB-DU shall release the UE from SB BF configuration and reset additional DMRS to original configuration.

In case of SB BF release, all timers and counters for monitoring of additional DL DMRS switching shall be stopped/released.

---

### 3.18.7.0-2 Additional DMRS switching algo for SB BF Conditions for stopping the monitoring of additional DL DMRS switching (ID: 11157646)

**3.18.7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11157651`)

Additional DMRS switching algo for SB BF
If rrmNoAddDlDmrsSwitchEnabled (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21336\_replaced([11157009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = True:

-Cell level conditions of the serving cell:

-enters power saving mode (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2550\_replaced([11118320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqB9PfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

-Remote Interference Mitigation (RIM) scheme (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9172\_replaced([11163373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

The rrmNoAddDlDmrsReleaseProhibitTimer timer is initiated with min( rdNoAddDlDmrsReleaseProhibitTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27200\_replaced([11158716](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktEDI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), rrmWbSrsReleaseProhibitTimer initalisation value (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21332\_replaced([11156967](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))).

5G-L2-PS shall wait until the RRC complete of a UE received or rrmNoAddDlDmrsConfigProhibitTimer timer expires to initiate another request for RRC reconfiguration even for SB BF configuration release request.
