### 3.18.7.0-5 Additional DMRS switching algo for SB BF Monitor DL DMRS switch toggle (ID: 11157690)

**3.18.7.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11157695`)

Additional DMRS switching algo for SB BF
Each UE under SB\_BF\_CONF has initial state as 'not DL DMRS Toggle' and ~~the 'DMRS Toggle counter' is initialized to 0~~ the counters ‘DL DMRS switch counter’ and the 'DL DMRS Toggle counter' are initialized to 0.

DL DMRS switch counter: gNB-DU shall count the number of successful configuration of DMRS to 'additional DMRS' from DMRS 'without additional DMRS' switch for each UE within 30s.

DL DMRS Toggle counter: gNB-DU shall also count continuous DL DMRS toggle for each UE. Toggle is defined as: DL DMRS with additional DMRS sucessfully configured from DL DMRS without additional DMRS configuration is triggered at the time when **rrmNoAddDlDmrsReleaseProhibitTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27248\_replaced([11157672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) expires.**

If the successful configuration of DMRS to 'additional DMRS' from DMRS 'without additional DMRS' switch is counted equal to 6 times ~~within 30s~~ or continuous toggle is more than 3 times,

- gNB-BU shall start/restart the **rrmNoAddDlDmrsConstraintTimer timer.**

- gNB-DU shall mark the UE as 'DL DMRS Toggle'.

If the **rrmNoAddDlDmrsConstraintTimer timer expires, gNB-DU shall mark the UE as 'not DL DMRS Toggle'.**

The **rrmNoAddDlDmrsConstraintTimer timer is initiated with** rdNoAddDlDmrsConstraintTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27279\_replaced([11158763](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktEqLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*\*\*

---

## 3.18.8 Adaptive SRS ports for non-coherent MIMO UEs

### 3.18.8.0-3 Adaptive SRS ports for non-coherent MIMO UEs Enabling\Disabling of Adaptive number of SRS ports (ID: 11157717)

**3.18.8.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `12647022`)

Adaptive SRS ports for non-coherent MIMO UEs
If an UE has "adaptive number of SRS ports" enabled, and if the C-Plane triggers a modification of nrofSrsPorts to 1 then gNB shall disable "adaptive number of SRS ports" when the modified SRS configuration is activated (see ([11153999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). After that, if nrofSrsPorts is changed back to 2 again, then gNB shall enable "adaptive number of SRS ports" again once the SRS configuration is activated (see ([11153999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

After the activation of the new setting (MAC or RRC layer monitoring), the U-Plane triggers the UL Adaptive SRS rank evaluation if the UE has at least the capability to handle 2 SRS ports.

The "adaptive number of SRS ports" only applies to the Primary Cell.

For FR1 UL CA with UL Tx switching, the "adaptive number of SRS ports" related algorithm is not applied to PCell and SCell. When UL Tx Switching SCell is added via SCell addition/change/swap, "adaptive number of SRS ports" shall be disabled if it was enabled before in PCell. When UL Tx Switching SCell is released via SCell addition/change/swap, "adaptive number of SRS ports" shall be re-evaluated based on the newest condition in PCell.

If:

- UE is already configured with DL+UL SCell, while step-wise SCell Addition procedure for another DL only SCell is ongoing, [CB010741-C] OR

- UE is already configured with DL-only SCell, while SCell Upgrade procedure of existing SCell to DL&UL SCell is ongoing [End CB010741-C]

then:

if:

- ‘old’ band combination (the one before step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C]) did not support UL Tx switching and ‘adaptive number of SRS ports’ was enabled in the PCell, AND

- ‘new’ band combination (the one after step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C]) supports UL Tx switching

then:

- along with configuring UL Tx switching gNB shall disable ‘adaptive number of SRS ports’ in the PCell

if:

- ‘old’ band combination (the one before step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C]) supported UL Tx switching, AND

- ‘new’ band combination (the one after step-wise SCell Addition [CB010741-C] / Upgrade [End CB010741-C]) does not support UL Tx switching

then:

- along with releasing UL Tx switching gNB shall re-evaluate ‘adaptive number of SRS ports’ based on the newest conditions in the PCell.

In above statement, UL Tx switching means both R16 1T UL Tx switching and R17 2T UL Tx switching.

Interaction between "adaptive number of SRS ports" and "dynamic UL waveform switching" is described by ([11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For users which are configured with any full power mode (see ([11355420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucQnHvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the 'adaptive number of SRS ports' related algorithm shall NOT be applied.

A UE with "adaptive number of SRS ports" has an adaptive number of SRS ports state. For a UE with maxNumOfUlLayers 2 a state machine described in ([11157744](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is activated.

When UL maximum number of layer is 1, UE should always keeps in “single Tx” state and SRS port number is one refer to ([11164357](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25sWPPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Notes:**

 After SCell addition [CB010741-C] / upgrade [End CB010741-C], UE capability of nrofSrsPorts in PCell may downgrade from ports2 to port1 according to different capability in different band combination. After SCell release and SCell change, UE capability of nrofSrsPorts in PCell may upgrade from port1 to ports2 again.

 The start/end notification of SCell release procedure is received from C-Plane, see ([11315870](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tr41kPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more information.

---

### 3.18.8.1 Adaptive number of SRS ports Finite State Machine

#### 3.18.8.1.1 Finite state machine description

##### 3.18.8.1.1.0-1 Finite state machine description Initial state of number of SRS ports (ID: 11157753)

**3.18.8.1.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13326160`)

Finite state machine description
The adaptive number of SRS ports state machine starts as soon as the UE has an "adaptive number of SRS ports" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6925\_replaced([11157717](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

* If rsrp parameter is present (5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC\_3114\_replaced([11342871](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wWeGdPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and if rsrp is greater than or equal to rdRsrpCellCenteredThreshold (see 5G\_L2\_1088\_replaced([11186502](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2758qvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the initial state is "ulRank 2" state otherwise the initial state is "single Tx" is port1. 5G-L2-PS shall indicate number of SRS prots to be configured in User Modify Resp.
* If at User Setup the Call Type in the UE Context (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_1169\_replaced([11251589](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TndBffvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is "SA" and if nrofSrsPorts (see 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC\_5360\_replaced([11364126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZvc6fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is port1 then the initial state is "single Tx".
* If at User Setup  the Call Type in the UE Context (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_1169\_replaced([11251589](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TndBffvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is "SA" and if nrofSrsPorts (see 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC\_5360\_replaced([11364126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZvc6fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is ports2 :
* If rsrp parameter is present (see 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC\_3114\_replaced([11342871](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wWeGdPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and if rsrp is greater than or equal to rdRsrpCellCenteredThreshold (see 5G\_L2\_1088\_replaced([11186502](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2758qvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the initial state is "ulRank 2" state otherwise the initial state is "single Tx" . 5G-L2-PS shall indicate number of SRS prots to be configured in User Setup Resp.
* If actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE AND UE is first configured with a VoNR (5QI-1, 5QI-65, or 5QI-66) DRB , set the initial state as "single Tx".
* Note: This is applicable for 5QI1 HO scenario
* [CB008148-B]If NRCELL.actUlTransPreUsageEnh contains 'DCI01\_TpOnOff\_StartTpOn', set the initial state as "single Tx"
* Note: UE is configured for PUSCH Transform Precoder at UE setup (Initial Access, HO, RRE) regardless of SINR [End CB008148-B]

Notes:

* 5G-L2-PS shall indicate number of SRS ports to be configured in User Setup Resp.
* When 5G-L2-PS need indicate number of SRS prots to be configured in User Setup/Modify Resp, "single Tx" shall map to port1, "ulRank 2" shall map to port2.

---

##### 3.18.8.1.1.0-2 Finite state machine description State: singleTx (ID: 11157769)

**3.18.8.1.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12738782`)

Finite state machine description
Refactored by CNI-107035. No change to function.

**State: singleTx**

·When enters this state:

- 5G-L2-PS shall activate newly received SRS configuration.

·Under this state:

- The Rank selection is started according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3224\_replaced([11139906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* The rrmLtrPollTimer (timer defined in [5G\_UP\_ALG\_8305](https://gates.nsn-net.net/requirement/5G_UP_ALG_8305)) is re-started with a value of zero each time a HARQ initial transmission subsequent to timer expiring has UL Rank 1

- If at User Setup the Call Type in the UE Context (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_1169\_replaced([11251589](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TndBffvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is "SA" and if User Modify Req is received with number of SRS ports equal to 2: 5G-L2-PS shall indicate 1 SRS port in the User Modify Resp (see 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC\_5360\_replaced([11364126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZvc6fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- 5G-L2-PS shall request for reconfiguration to number of SRS ports 2 is based on PUSCH sinr measurements.

- For users which are configured with any full power mode (see 5G\_UP\_3769\_replaced([11355420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucQnHvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),  L2-PS shall request the number of SRS ports reconfiguration to 2.

[Before PR849086]  
[PR838599]

If the rank selection for the next transmission is rank2 and the Configured Grant (CG) for the UE is not in one of the following states, gNB-DU shall decide to change the number of SRS ports to 2.

The change to 2 SRS ports is allowed if the UE with Configured Grant (CG) is:

·  not activated in rank1.

·  not involved in a CG activation procedure in rank1.

·  not involved in a CG modification procedure in rank1.

·  not involved in a CG deactivation procedure for a CG previously activated in rank1.

[End PR838599]  
[End PR849086]

- When new 2 port SRS is received, swith to **Reconfiguration1to2SrsPorts.**

---

##### 3.18.8.1.1.0-3 Finite state machine description State: ulRank2 (ID: 11157779)

**3.18.8.1.1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13407485`)

Finite state machine description
·When enters this state:

- 5G-L2-PS starts the “adaptiveSrsPortsKeepRank2Timer” timer whose duration is rdTPinteractAdaptSrsPortsKeepRank2Timer (5G\_UP\_ALG ([11141214](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpv_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if DFT-S-OFDM is activated (NRCELL\actUlDftsOfdm = **true) otherwise rdAdaptiveSrsPortsKeepRank2Timer (5G\_UP\_ALG ([11141177](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

- 5G-L2-PS shall activate newly received SRS configuration.

·Under this state:

- 5G-L2-PS shall request for reconfiguration to number of SRS ports 1 is based on PUSCH Rank indication.  If the “adaptiveSrsPortsKeepRank2Timer” timer is not running, the 5G-L2-PS checks periodicaly the rank selection computed for the next transmission (see requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG ([11139906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

· If DFT-S-OFDM is activated (NRCELL\actUlDftsOfdm = **true), the check is done every rdTPinteractAdaptSrsPortsRankPollingTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG ([11141230](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpxPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

· If DFT-S-OFDM is not activated (NRCELL\actUlDftsOfdm = **false), the check is done every rdAdaptiveSrsPortsRankPollingTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG ([11141189](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

If the rank selection for the next transmission is rank1 for enough consecutive time (rdTPinteractAdaptSrsPortsNbConsecutiveForReconf (5G\_UP\_ALG ([11141242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if DFT-S-OFDM is activated (NRCELL\actUlDftsOfdm = **true) or otherwise rdAdaptiveSrsPortsNbConsecutiveForReconf (5G\_UP\_ALG ([11141204](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxps_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) and the Configured Grant (CG) for the UE is not in one of the following state, the 5G-L2-PS decides to change the number of SRS ports to 1.**

The change to 1 SRS port is allowed if the UE with Configured Grant (CG) is:

· not activated in rank2.

· not involved in a CG activation procedure in rank2.

· not involved in a CG modification procedure in rank2.

· not involved in a CG deactivation procedure for a CG previously activated in rank2.

- When new 1 port SRS is received, swith to **Reconfiguration2to1SrsPorts.**

If the UE has "adaptive number of SRS ports" , AND (actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE AND UE is added with first 5QI1/65/66 DRB in User Setup/ Modify) ,  then set the value of number of srs ports to configure in the User Setup/Modify Response to gNb-CP-RT (see 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC ([11364126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZvc6fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be  port1 (number of SRS port as 1). Switch to **Reconfiguration2to1SrsPorts**

If  actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE AND UE is configured with 5QI1/65/66 DRB, and if  there is User Modification to change the number of SRS ports to 2 or full power mode to disable, leading to change in the state of "adaptive number of SRS ports" to enable,  then set the value of number of srs ports to configure in the User Modify Response to gNb-CP-RT (see 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC ([11364126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZvc6fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be  port1 (number of SRS port as 1). Switch to **Reconfiguration2to1SrsPorts**

If  there is User Modification, when UL Tx Switching SCell is added via SCell addition/change/swap [CB010741-C] /upgrade [End CB010741-C], leading to change in the state of "adaptive number of SRS ports" to disable,  then the value of number of srs ports to configure in the User Modify Response to gNb-CP-RT (see 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC ([11364126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZvc6fvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be  port2 (number of SRS port as 2). Switch to Reconfiguration1to2SrsPort

---

##### 3.18.8.1.1.0-4 Finite state machine description State: Reconfiguration1to2SrsPorts or Reconfiguration2to1SrsPorts (ID: 11157795)

**3.18.8.1.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11157800`)

Finite state machine description
·When enters this state:

- 5G-L2-PS shall save newly received SRS configuration.

·Under this state:

- 5G-L2-PS shall handle the gNB internal failure in  5G\_UP\_ALG\_11839\_replaced([11157842](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks-jgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- The PUSCH transmission is based on single antenna port and scheduled by DCI 0\_0 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14012\_replaced([11171394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuEIoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). with a restriction regarding the DCI format to be used see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26832\_replaced([11153999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: There is some uncertainty about number of SRS ports currently configured in the UE in this state so that ratio of DTX of PUSCH data may be important in this state.

This is taken into account for UL radio link problem detection, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8227\_replaced([11151822](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksbw__vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- When 5G-L2-PS has received confirmation that UE is expected to use this new setting in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26832\_replaced([11153999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), switch to ulRank2 or singleTx.

---

##### 3.18.8.1.1.0-5 Finite state machine description Before Refactor of CNI-107035 State Machine for Adaptive number of SRS port (ID: 11157805)

**3.18.8.1.1.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11157836`)

Finite state machine description
11157836:
Finite state machine description
For a UE with "adaptive number of SRS ports" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6925\_replaced([11157717](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and with maxNumOfUlLayers 2, the Adaptive number of SRS ports state machine defines the number of SRS ports.

**[CB009915-B-UPD005] Modified above diagram.** [End CB009915-B-UPD005]\*\*\*\*

When the state machine starts and the initial state is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30477\_replaced([11157753](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks98cfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Then Rank selection is started according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3224\_replaced([11139906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). This implicitly means that if the UE  is in the "single Tx state", the timer rdUlPmiRiFallBackTimer defined in 5G\_L2\_1087\_replaced([11186580](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_276juPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is started at first initial transmission.

This also implicitly means that L2-PS decision to request for reconfiguration to number of SRS ports 2 is based on PUSCH sinr measurements because when transmission mode is single Tx there is no SRS measurements and L1 doesn't report rank indication in the *UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs.*

This also implicitly means that L2-PS decision to request for reconfiguration to number of SRS ports 1 is based on PUSCH Rank indication.

L2-PS behaves according to the UE "adaptive number of SRS ports" state regarding UL transmission, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3259\_replaced([11157795](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks98evvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When L2-PS decides to change the number of SRS ports, it launches the "User Reconfiguration Required" procedure.

When the L2-PS changes the UE "adaptive number of SRS ports" state to “ulRank 2” it starts the “adaptiveSrsPortsKeepRank2Timer” timer whose duration is rdTPinteractAdaptSrsPortsKeepRank2Timer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10834\_replaced([11141214](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpv_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if DFT-S-OFDM is activated (NRCELL\actUlDftsOfdm = **true) otherwise rdAdaptiveSrsPortsKeepRank2Timer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10839\_replaced([11141177](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

When the “adaptive number of SRS ports” state is “ulRank 2 ” and the “adaptiveSrsPortsKeepRank2Timer” timer is not running, the 5G-L2-PS checks periodicaly the rank selection computed for the next transmission (see requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3224\_replaced([11139906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

 If DFT-S-OFDM is activated (NRCELL\actUlDftsOfdm = **true), the check is done every rdTPinteractAdaptSrsPortsRankPollingTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10835\_replaced([11141230](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpxPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

 If DFT-S-OFDM is not activated (NRCELL\actUlDftsOfdm = **false), the check is done every rdAdaptiveSrsPortsRankPollingTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10840\_replaced([11141189](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

If the rank selection for the next transmission is rank1 for enough consecutive time (rdTPinteractAdaptSrsPortsNbConsecutiveForReconf (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10836\_replaced([11141242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if DFT-S-OFDM is activated (NRCELL\actUlDftsOfdm = **true) or otherwise rdAdaptiveSrsPortsNbConsecutiveForReconf (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10841\_replaced([11141204](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxps_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) and the Configured Grant (CG) for the UE is not in one of the following state, the 5G-L2-PS decides to change the number of SRS ports to 1.**

The change to 1 SRS port is allowed if the UE with Configured Grant (CG) is:

 not activated in rank2.

 not involved in a CG activation procedure in rank2.

 not involved in a CG modification procedure in rank2.

 not involved in a CG deactivation procedure for a CG previously activated in rank2.

---

#### 3.18.8.1.2 Handling of exceptions at procedure User Reconfiguration Required

##### 3.18.8.1.2.0-1 Handling of exceptions at procedure User Reconfiguration Required (ID: 11157847)

**3.18.8.1.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11157859`)

Handling of exceptions at procedure User Reconfiguration Required
[CNI-107035] Refactored by CNI-107035. [End CNI-107035]

If 5G-L2-PS requires for RRC Reconfiguration with number of SRS Ports to two ports:

* If the reconfiguration enter gNB internal failure, 5G-L2-PS shall :

consider the "adaptive number of SRS ports" state is "single Tx" (see 5G\_L2\_656\_replaced([11164313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25sWIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and restart the Long term UL rank computation as defined in  5G\_UP\_ALG\_3224\_replaced([11139906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (i.e reset the rrmUlRiLongTerm value to 1, reinitialize to zero and restart the timer rdUlPmiRiFallBackTimer).

If 5G-L2-PS requires for RRC Reconfiguration with number of SRS Ports to one port:

* If the reconfiguration enter gNB internal failure, 5G-L2-PS shall :

Start a "fallbackRank2" timer

As long as the timer is running, the UE is configured with number of SRS ports 2 and has transmission mode closed loop spatial MIMO with Rank2 and the UL rank selection algorithm 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3224\_replaced([11139906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) runs.

If the UL rank selection algorithm 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3224\_replaced([11139906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) selects Rank2, stop the "fallbackRank2" timer and the "adaptive number of SRS ports" state is "ulRank 2"

If the "fallbackRank2" timer expires start again the RRC reconfiguration procedure with number of SRS Ports to one port, no matter the number of unsuccessful attempts.

* The "fallbackRank2" timer is defined by:
* If DFT-S-OFDM for PUSCH is active (NRCELL.actUlDftSOfdm = True): rdTPinteractionAdaptSrsPortsFallbackRank2Timer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10837\_replaced([11141254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Else: rdAdaptiveSrsPortsFallbackRank2Timer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10833\_replaced([11141162](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxpo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

## 3.18.9 Periodic codebook SRS for Positioning

### 3.18.9.1 SRS Reception for positioning purpose

#### 3.18.9.1.0-1 SRS Reception for positioning purpose Periodic SRS configuration (ID: 11157876)

**3.18.9.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11157892`)

SRS Reception for positioning purpose
If the NIDD parameter NRCELL.actHPPosMethodOptList is enabled, 5G-L2-PS may receive periodic SRS resource configuration of a user from L3 during the user modification procedures for legacy LA/SU-MIMO or during measurement setup for SRS positioning (PsPos\_MeasSetupReq message) in the serving cell [CB007880-B] or in the non-serving cell in case of shared TRP function ([Before CB007880-B-UPD001] NRBTS/NRCELL/actSharedTRP [CB007880-B-UPD001]NRBTS/NRCELL/nrPosDN is configured [End CB007880-B-UPD001]) is enabled [End CB007880-B] in non-beamforming deployment. This Rel-15 P-SRS shall be used for both legacy LA/SU-MIMO purpose and positioning purpose. The parameters stored in user context shall be the same as those for P-SRS for UL beamforming (Please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2147\_replaced([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). SRS positioning information shall be stored in measurement context(5G\_UP\_ALG\_27813\_replaced([11158061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_KnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))].

L2PS shall scheduler P-SRS for both legacy LA(5G\_UP\_ALG\_19441\_replaced([11130836](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krA0ovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))/SU-MIMO(5G\_UP\_ALG\_3216\_replaced([11139853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) purpose and P-SRS for positioning purpose accordingly. Both legacy UL LA(5G\_UP\_ALG\_19441\_replaced([11130836](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krA0ovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and UL SU-MIMO(5G\_UP\_ALG\_3216\_replaced([11139853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are adjusted to be based on pSRS if UE is configured for precise positioning in non-beamforming deployment. So it shall be still able to dynamically switch the number of pSRS ports between 1 and 2 for the non-coherent UE as the requirement (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6925\_replaced([11157717](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3254\_replaced([11157749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks98cPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Please note: it's possible that some users are configured with aperiodic SRS and others are configured with periodic SRS by L3. The SRS allocation algorithm is specified by L3.

---

#### 3.18.9.1.0-2 SRS Reception for positioning purpose Cyclic shift of SRS ports (ID: 11157899)

**3.18.9.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11157904`)

SRS Reception for positioning purpose
The cyclic shift values of each SRS port shall be calculated according to equations defined in 3GPP 38.211 6.4.1.4.2. For detailed examples please see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2149\_replaced([11154208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrokvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) except the transmissionComb = n4 is supported (Please see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27064\_replaced([11107865](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kojWmvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27066\_replaced([11107872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koj9kfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detailed frequency domain SRS parameters).

---

#### 3.18.9.1.0-3 SRS Reception for positioning purpose SRS measurement cycle (periodic SRS) (ID: 11157910)

**3.18.9.1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11157996`)

SRS Reception for positioning purpose
11157996:
SRS Reception for positioning purpose
5G-L2-PS shall trigger SRS reception for NRCELL [CB010680-G] and its associated NRPOSCELLs [End CB010680-G]  for Measurement Context [CB007880-B] in non-shared TRP case ([Before CB007880-B-UPD001]NRBTS/NRCELL/actSharedTRP is FALSE  [CB007880-B-UPD001]NRBTS/NRCELL/nrPosDN is not configured [End CB007880-B-UPD001]) and in shared TRP case  ([Before CB007880-B-UPD001]  NRBTS/NRCELL/actSharedTRP is TRUE [CB007880-B-UPD001]NRBTS/NRCELL/nrPosDN is configured [End CB007880-B-UPD001]) [End CB007880-B], which are configured with periodic SRS in active BWP and for which the UE dedicated configuration is activated (5G\_UP\_ALG\_18227\_replaced([11153313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kslh9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) via Control Plane(Note that Control Plane requests L2-PS to initiate Positioning Measurements when a UE attaches to the cell and moves to RRC Connected state), in slots satisfying the below condition:

[image-0][image\_desc](N_{slot}^{frame,u} n_f + n_{s,f}^u - T_{of} f_{set}) \mod T\_{ars} = 0[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_10639.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where:

For NRCELL:

* 5G-L2-PS shall NOT trigger SRS based legacy LA/MIMO reception for UEs which are NOT in duration of DRX active status even above slot condition for periodic SRS is satisfied.
* 5G-L2-PS shall NOT trigger SRS based legacy LA/MIMO reception for UEs which are in measurement GAP period even above slot condition for periodic SRS is satisfied.
* [Before CB007880-C-UPD001][CB007880-C]5G-L2-PS shall take Remote Interference specific mitigations due to remote interference mitigation scheme (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9172\_replaced([11163373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktYzNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB007880-C][End CB007880-C-UPD001]
* 5G-L2-PS shall NOT trigger SRS based legacy LA/MIMO reception [Before CB007880-C-UPD001] and periodic SRS based Positioning reception [End CB007880-C-UPD001] for UEs due to additional UL mitigation for RIM RS detection (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13520\_replaced([11162042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-APvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB010680-G]

For NRPOSCELL:

* If C-Plane includes PRB blanking information in the message for Positioning Measurement Setup that is received by 5G-L2-PS(NRPOSCELL), 5G-L2-PS(NRPPOSCELL) will not request L1(NRPOSCELL) to perform SRS based Positioning reception in blanked PRBs.

[End CB010680-G]

[CB010680-H]

* 5G-L2-PS shall support Distributed Antenna besides co-located Antenna for RU-SRS.

[End CB010680-H]

For each Measurement Context for which SRS reception needs to be triggered, 5G-L2-PS shall provide below SRS related information to L1-UL according to SRS configuration (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27467\_replaced([11157876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks-jh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) stored in measurement context:

 Time domain position: startPosition and nrofSymbols (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27062\_replaced([11107844](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kojWl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Frequency domain position: starting PRB and number of PRBs (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27485\_replaced([11158001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_KkvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/2153).

 Transmission comb: combOffset and cyclicShift (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27064\_replaced([11107865](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kojWmvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27066\_replaced([11107872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koj9kfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 sequenceId (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2147\_replaced([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23308\_replaced([11094702](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kme6AfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 For the case that UL SU-MIMO needs to be measured over SRS, additional SU-MIMO related information shall be provided to L1. See the details in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3246\_replaced([11155645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhHPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 3.18.9.1.0-4 SRS Reception for positioning purpose Frequency position of SRS (ID: 11158001)

**3.18.9.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11158007`)

SRS Reception for positioning purpose
The starting PRB of SRS shall be calculated according to equations defined in the chapter of 6.4.1.4.3 in 3GPP TS 38.211. Please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2153\_replaced([11154391](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksromvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.18.9.1.0-5 SRS Reception for positioning purpose ToE(UL RTOA) and UL AoA measurement and UL SRS-RSRP handling for positioning service (ID: 11158012)

**3.18.9.1.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11158021`)

SRS Reception for positioning purpose
**[Before CB007880-A]**

As only intermediate measurement result(TOE) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27294\_replaced([11107769](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koivc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is generated and reported from L1 to L2 and there is no final UL-RTOA measurement generated in this feature. L2PS just ignores the intermediate result in this feature.

**[CB007880-A]**

Depends on the request from gNB-CU-CP ([11635344: (2) Step F1AP: PositioningMeasurementRequest](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y-Jtt_wOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), the gNB-DU receives the UL-RTOA measurements and UL SRS-RSRP from L1 during each NRCELL.srsForPositioning.srsUePeriodicity and just keep the latest UL-RTOA measurement and UL SRS-RSRP during Measurement Periodicity. **[Before CB007880-A-UPD002] If current SINR (measured by L1 and transmitted to L2PS) when doing UL-RTOA measurement is less than a reliability threshold defined by  R&D parameter by SINR under a combination of measurement accuracy and PRB  combination (For details please see EFS) it shall be filtered out and shall not be sent to CPRT.** [End CB007880-A-UPD002]\*\*\*\*

[Before PR825728]UL SRS-RSRP measurement shall be forwarded to CPRT.[End PR825728] L2 reports to L3 for UL-RTOA measurement if not filtered not **[CB007880-A-UPD002] by L1** [End CB007880-A-UPD002] and UL SRS-RSRP measurement [PR825728] if not filtered not [End PR825728] per measurement ID within each measurement period.\*\*\*\*

**[End CB007880-A]**

**[CB007880-C]**

Note that in the case of inactive BWP scanning procedure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_16104\_replaced([11111313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpMPyvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) when gNB considers that the UE has switched to the inactive BWP UL-RTOA measurement might be filtered out due to low SINR if SRS for positioning is not configured in inactive BWP.

**[End CB007880-C]**

For super cell, each subcell works as single TRP (Transmission and Reception), the TOE(UL RTOA) measurement **[CB007880-A] and UL SRS-RSRP measurement** [End CB007880-A] shall be performed in **[Before CB007880-A] all subcells** [CB007880-A] the selected subcells **[End CB007880-A] of the super cell, which means the scheduling of SRS for positioning will be done for** [Before CB007880-A] all subcells **[CB007880-A] the selected subcells** [End CB007880-A] for a UE.***\*******\****\*\*

The detailed interface regarding if sending one message for each subcell or for a list of subcells should be defined by EFS.

---

#### 3.18.9.1.0-6 SRS Reception for positioning purpose Forwarding the Delta SFN Initialization Time between Serving Cell and Current TRP from L3 to L1 (ID: 11158027)

**3.18.9.1.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11158038`)

SRS Reception for positioning purpose
L2 shall forward the Delta SFN Initialization Time between Serving Cell and Current TRP from L3 (please refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_15506\_replaced([11325148](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tsq4svvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to L1 for both NRCELL [CB007880-D] and NRPOSCELL [End CB007880-D].

---

### 3.18.9.2 Positioning Cell Contexts in L2RT

#### 3.18.9.2.0-1 Positioning Cell Contexts in L2RT Positioning Cell Contexts (ID: 11158048)

**3.18.9.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11158053`)

Positioning Cell Contexts in L2RT
As defined in 5G\_UP\_11750\_replaced([11369761](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udsKdfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 5G-L2-PS shall provide Positioning Cell contexts.

When positioning functionality for RU-ACCESS (i.e., NRCELL, Radio Units providing access) is deployed as part of a Cell context, it shall not consume any L2 cell slots of its own and shall utilize the L2 processing resources allocated to the Cell.

When positioning functionality for RU-SRS (NRPOSCELL, Radio Units dedicated for positioning accuracy and not for access) is deployed as a Positioning Cell context that is not part of a Cell context, it shall consume cell slots in the L2 cell slot model.

When pool configuration (L2 pool/subpool configurations and L1 pool/subpool configurations) is performed for L2-RT, CP-RT also performs Address Distribution with L2-LO and L2-PS for L2-LO and L2-PS to configure the pools and exchange addresses with CP-RT.  While L2-LO is not impacted by NRPOSCELL, a lean version of L2-PS exists for NRPOSCELL, with which addresses must be exchanged and pools must be configured.

A common interface message is triggered by CP-RT for RU-ACCESS and as well as for RU-SRS.

---

### 3.18.9.3 Positioning Measurement Context in L2RT

#### 3.18.9.3.0-1 Positioning Measurement Context in L2RT Positioning Measurement Context (ID: 11158061)

**3.18.9.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11158072`)

Positioning Measurement Context in L2RT
As defined in 5G\_UP\_11739\_replaced([11369775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udsKd_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 5G-L2-PS shall provide Positioning Measurment context which which shall implement the positioning measurement for one UE for one TRP.

The Positioning Measurement context shall be totally independent from UE context.

L2PS shall send two independent SRS measurement procedures to L1 (one for SU MUMO SRS from the UE context, the other for positioning SRS from the measurement context).

[CB010332-C]In case of a super cell, the SRS measurement for SU MIMO is performed in serving subcell only.[End CB010332-C]

---

## 3.18.10 Load control and aging for periodic SRS for WB BF

### 3.18.10.0-1 Load control and aging for periodic SRS for WB BF Overview (ID: 11158082)

**3.18.10.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11158093`)

Load control and aging for periodic SRS for WB BF
gNB-DU shall discard SRS response if it is aged (5G\_UP\_ALG\_28317\_replaced([11158098](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_xpvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB013710-A] gNB-DU shall skip some SRS processing at some conditions (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29538\_replaced([11158109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_xqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB013710-A]

---

### 3.18.10.0-2 Load control and aging for periodic SRS for WB BF Fail-safe periodic SRS measurements load control (ID: 11158098)

**3.18.10.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11158102`)

Load control and aging for periodic SRS for WB BF
If NIDD: actDlSrsBm is true or actUlSrsBm is true, gNB shall check the age of periodic SRS response for wideband BF before handling it, which counts from the OTA SRS slot to the current slot. gNB shall discard the SRS response if the age is larger than rdSrsResponseAging (5G\_UP\_ALG\_28319\_replaced([11158864](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktFRO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

### 3.18.10.0-3 Load control and aging for periodic SRS for WB BF Reduced periodic SRS processing for load purpose (ID: 11158109)

**3.18.10.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11158127`)

Load control and aging for periodic SRS for WB BF
11158127:
Load control and aging for periodic SRS for WB BF
If reduced periodic SRS processing functionality is triggered (5G\_UP\_543\_replaced([11351277](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubsma_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall skip **consecutive  periodic SRS processing within rrmBeamSelectTimer for the selected UEs (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29611\_replaced([11158133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_xq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and then not skip** consecutive periodic SRS processing within rrmBeamSelectTimer in turns. rrmBeamSelectTimer is **rrmDlBeamSelectTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7000\_replaced([11156122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for load purpose. The skiping or not in this requirement shall work together with legacy functionalities in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2151\_replaced([11154219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrolPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**\*\*\*\*

Note 1: it is known that **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer can be configured to different values via tuning rad parameters, but this functionality always adopts the timer of DL since by default rad setting the two are equal and customers cannot tune them.**

Note 2: if both codebook and TAS p-SRS resource sets are configured to a UE, resources in both sets shall be considered.

Figure: example illustration. SRS periodicity is 40 slots in this example, blue arrow: SRS occurrence. Crossed blue arrow: skipped SRS occurrence. Green arrow: beam update.

The second annotation, spanning from above the 520 marker to the 600 marker, reads "560 timer restart beam update. Note need to consider delay and varity of the SRS EO exesion".

**[CB014465-B] If a UE is not a SB BF UE and has SRS for WB BF periodicity doubled compared to NRCELL.srsForBeamMgmt.srsUePeriodicity, gNB-DU shall double** rrmDlBeamSelectTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7000\_replaced([11156122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and **rrmUlBeamSelectTimer  for the UE. Note the logic is defined in CPlane EFS and indicated to L2 at UE level**[End CB014465-B]***\****\*

### 3.18.10.0-4 Load control and aging for periodic SRS for WB BF Selected UEs for reduced SRS processing (ID: 11158133)

**3.18.10.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11158136`)

Load control and aging for periodic SRS for WB BF
The selected UEs are UEs with

1) p-SRS based wideband BF configured for DL (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6962\_replaced([11155660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or UL (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2135\_replaced([11154028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqacvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , and

2) not belonging to excluded category, and

3) have no traffic or UEs that are static (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29613\_replaced([11158141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks_xrfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Excluded category: UEs with the following configuration shall be excluded from the load-based reduction.

1) With subband BF configured, or

2) With DRX configured or measurement gap configured and skipped ratio by RRC configuration is larger than or equal to 0.5.

where skipped ratio by RRC configuration is the ratio of SRS occurrences that are skipped due to DRX or measurement Gap to all SRS occurrences. The skipped SRS occurrences are ones (not in DRX on duration) or (in gap), which are calculated based on the periodicity and offset of p-SRS, DRX on duration, measurement gap.

---

### 3.18.10.0-5 Load control and aging for periodic SRS for WB BF No traffic or static UEs for reduced SRS processing (ID: 11158141)

**3.18.10.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11158152`)

Load control and aging for periodic SRS for WB BF
No traffic UE: For DL: the UE that has zero data buffered on all DRB bearers for DL for continuous 2 seconds or longer. For UL: the UE that has zero data buffered on all DRB bearers for UL for continuous 2 seconds or longer. If NRCELL/actDlSrsBm is set as enabled, then DL traffic shall be checked. If NRCELL/actUlSrsBm is set as enabled, then UL traffic shall be checked. Note if both NRCELL/actDlSrsBm and NRCELL/actUlSrsBm are enabled, gNB does not distinguish whether a p-SRS resource will be used for UL or DL for simplicity, because in customer network the same codebook p-SRS resource for both UL and DL is recommended as golden parameter.

If CA is configured, the traffic is for the carrier that is configured the p-SRS. Note: Even when Scell needs sync up SRS beamforming information from Pcell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2683\_replaced([11120559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqR03PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU still only consider traffic of Pcell for which p-SRS is configured for simplicity, instead of considering both Pcell and Scell.

Static UE: configuration is defined in 5G\_UP\_14076\_replaced([11352153](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub0iO_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB014465-B] and does not have SRS periodicity doubled compared to NRCELL.srsForBeamMgmt.srsUePeriodicity [End CB014465-B].

---

### 3.18.11.0-4 Rad parameters SRS rdSrsSwitchProhibitTimer (ID: 11158203)

**3.18.11.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11158208`)

Rad parameters SRS
[Before CB008322-G]Short description: This parameter defines the timer for 5G-L2-PS to prohibit UE’s Ping-Pong RRC reconfiguration for different SRS type.

Value range: 100...10000

Default value: 1000

Step size: 1

Unit: slot

Online modifiable: no

Performance impact: minor.

Used in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21332\_replaced([11156967](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5D8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Trigger for deletion: When the R&D parameter has been replaced by a NIDD parameter.

Owner: Xukai Gao

rrmSrsSwitchProhibitTimer = max {rdSrsSwitchProhibitTimer, (rdPeriodSrsCheck +1)\* rdNumSrsCheck }

Note:Change to NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/wbSrsConfigProhibitTimer and default value of NIDD is different from here.

Rationale: 1) New SRS status check must make sure there is at least one time’s monitor result. 5G-L2-PS may put the UE at different slot within rdPeriodSrsCheck to balance the monitor load, but 5G-L2-PS shall not delay more than rdPeriodSrsCheck for the monitor.

2) WB SRS release must make sure at least there is enough valid CoMa to make sure it will not release due to initial DL BM status.  [End CB008322-G]

rdPeriodSrsCheck [5G\_UP\_ALG\_21349\_replaced([11158211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktAYvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

### 3.18.11.0-7 Rad parameters SRS rdWbSrsPrbTresh (ID: 11158242)

**3.18.11.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11158246`)

Rad parameters SRS
[Before CB008322-G]

Short description: This parameter defines the percentage of scheduled PRB versus number of valid PRB for that slot and is used for evaluation of wide band SRS configuration. Note due multi BWP, RAT0/RAT1 co-exist and etc. scenario, the PRB ratio of all UEs in the same slot cannot reach 100%.

Value range: 1...100

Default value: 20

Note for setting: In the stable traffic test mode, if there are maxNumUeSrs UEs scheduled with balanced PRB usage ratio and if all maxNumUeSrs plan to be added with WB SRS then this parameter better be lower than 1/ maxNumUeSrs.

Step size: 1

Unit: NA

Online modifiable: yes

Performance impact: minor.

Used in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21353\_replaced([11157336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

### 3.18.11.0-13 Rad parameters SRS rdWbSrsQualTresh (ID: 11158309)

**3.18.11.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `11158314`)

Rad parameters SRS
[Before CB008322-G]

Short description: This parameter defines the threshold for SRS quality and is used for evaluation of wide band SRS configuration.

[PR721939]The value actually used has relation to  DL oDFT beam, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End PR721939]

If NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsQualityThreshold < rrmMinWbSrsSinr, the value is recommended to be higher than NRCELL/srsForSubbandBm.srsQualityThreshold+ Power step + rdWbSrsQualProh  to make UE have WB SRS released instead of suffering dynamic ping-pong fallback.

with Power step as Coma power can be higher than srs power per port per TRX.

the theoritical value as : 10*LOG10(number of TRX row* sum(abs(wh)^2+ number of TRX column\* sum(abs(wv)^2))/(number of TRX row+number of TRX column))

wh and wv is horizontal combine weight vectors and vertical combine weight vectors defined in 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4843.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Theoretical max | compromised max |
| 4 row 8 column | 13.72 | 7.58 |
| 2 row 8 column | 11.04 | 7.02 |
| 4 row 4 column | 10.02 | 5.31 |

Value range: -150...0

Default value: -120

Step size: 0.1

Unit: NA

Online modifiable: yes

Performance impact: minor.

Used in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21355\_replaced([11157389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks65KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Trigger for deletion: When the R&D parameter has been replaced by a NIDD parameter.

Owner: Xukai Gao

Note:

Change to NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/wbSrsPowerThreshold

[End CB008322-G]

---

### 3.18.11.0-19 Rad parameters SRS rdSrsBufPercent (ID: 11158384)

**3.18.11.0-19.0-1**  (ID: `11158387`)

Rad parameters SRS
[Before CB008322-G] Short description: This parameter defines the percentage of buffer samples that meet the high or low buffer threshold after rdNumSrsCheck .

Value range: 0...100

values between 40-60 better be avoid because both WB SRS configuration and release adopt the same high/low PRB percentage threshold, in this case values around 50 may trigger Ping-Pong switch if the high/low PRB usage prohibit (rdWbSrsPrbProh) is configured with small enough value.

Default value: 20

Step size: 1

Unit: slot

Online modifiable: yes

Performance impact: minor.

Used in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21378\_replaced([11157541](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8HRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21380\_replaced([11157558](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8HSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Owner: Xukai Gao

### 3.18.11.0-24 Rad parameters SRS rdIncludeHighVolatileUe (ID: 11158437)

**3.18.11.0-24.0-1**  (ID: `11158443`)

Rad parameters SRS
This parameter controls whether UEs with high channel volatility status can be included in subband BF.

High volatility UEs can be included in subband BF if the rdIncludeHighVolatileUe is true and rdSbSrsVolatCorrThreshold >= NIDD:wbSbSrsSwitch/channelStabilityThreshold.

Value range:

* false: no include,
* true: include,

Default value: false

Step size: NA

### 3.18.11.0-30 Rad parameters SRS rdMmseRegularizationMode (ID: 11158523)

### 3.18.11.0-34 Rad parameters SRS rdRankForRtBeam (ID: 11158576)

**3.18.11.0-34.0-3**  (ID: `12521585`)

Rad parameters SRS
[Before CNI-137616-A]

This parameter defines whether L2 would overwrite rank at L2 based on number of RT beams from L1.

For the case of eCPRI 7-2e, this parameter is not used.

Value range:

0: L2 would overwrite rank at L2 based on number of RT beams from L1.

1: L2 would prefer to adopt rank at L2;

Default value: 0

Step size: 1

### 3.18.11.0-42 Rad parameters SRS rdMaxAccumulatedTpc  rdMaxAccumulatedTpcPE (ID: 11158675)

**3.18.11.0-42.0-2**  (ID: `11158687`)

Rad parameters SRS
Short description: This parameter defines the maximum absolute value for accumulated TPC at gNB side for estimation of [Before CB009527-A] WB SRS power [CB009527-A] SRS power for SB BF [End CB009527-A].

Rationale: As defined by 3GPP, accumulated TPC shall be used for UE to decide SRS transmission power but due to some misalignment between gNB and UE, the absolute value of accumulated TPC can be very large so this parameter is added to verify the impact.

Value range: 0...50

Default value: 6

Step size: 1

Unit: dB

Online modifiable: yes

Performance impact: minor.

### 3.18.11.0-44 Rad parameters SRS rdSrsCeOperation (ID: 11158704)

**3.18.11.0-44.0-1**  (ID: `11158709`)

Rad parameters SRS
This parameter indicates how to handle SRS CE in L1 Radio when DTX  low SRS power or high inteference is detected. This parameter is applied on eCPRI 7-2e.

Value 0 means L1 Radio shall NOT use the latest SRS CE per port per SRS subband which is detected as DTX  low SRS power or high intererence for calculating BWVs. Value 1 means L1 Radio shall always use the latest SRS CE per port per SRS subband even DTX or high interference is detected.

Value range: 0, 1

Default value: [Before PR806068] 0 [PR806068] 1 [End PR806068]

Step size: 1

Online modifiable: Yes

Specified in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13879\_replaced([11156605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2Ao_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Trigger for deletion: Never

Rationle: -

Owner: Fan , Paul (NSB - CN/Hangzhou)

Short description: This parameter defines default sampling rate for capturing BWVs and related SRS CE in RU on PRBs scheduled for PDSCH for SB BF UE. It's in unit of BF subband. Value 0 means the capturing shall be disabled.

Value range: 0...64

Default value: 16

Step size: 1

Unit: N/A

Online modifiable: no

Performance impact: minor.

Used in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27826\_replaced([11156590](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2AoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Trigger for deletion: When the R&D parameter has been replaced by a NIDD parameter.

Owner: Paul Fan

### 3.18.11.0-60 Rad parameters SRS rrmEirpCalculationWindow (ID: 11158875)

**3.18.11.0-60.0-1**  (ID: `11158879`)

Rad parameters SRS
Short description: This parameter defines the largest time window for receiving EIRP calculation result from L1 Radio via PDSCH sending response. Its default value (12 slots) is calculated as T1a\_max\_cp\_dl (PDSCH sending request, default value is 1345us) plus T4a\_max\_cp (PDSCH sending response, default value is 9 slots).

Value range: 3...20

Default value: 12

Step size: 1

Unit: slot

Online modifiable: No.

Performance impact: No.

Used in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22212\_replaced([11156683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2ntvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Trigger for deletion: When the R&D parameter has been replaced by a NIDD parameter.

Owner: Paul Fan

**3.18.11.0-67.0-1**  (ID: `11158951`)

default value: 8

### 3.18.11.0-68 Rad parameters SRS rdSbBfContinuousEvaluation (ID: 12539763)

**3.18.11.0-68.0-2**  (ID: `12539764`)

Rad parameters SRS
This parameter is used to define number of continuous evaluations, with result of bad, that has to be reached before switching a UE from SB BF to WB BF. [Before PR881825] This parameter only applies to eCPRI 7-2e. [End PR881825]

default value: 3

Unit: degrees

Online modifiable: No

step size: 1

**3.18.11.0-72.0-1**  (ID: `13434063`)

Rad parameters SRS
Short description: This value is the long-term CFO threshold for DL SU-MIMO in unit of Hz. This value is derived from PUSCH. The DL subband BF can be applied to DL SU-MIMO when LT CFO is lower than this threshold.

Step size: 1

Default value: 80

Unit: HZ
